Alain: Speak to me, please.

Josef: I never imagined he possessed such frightful mastery over the bodies of others.

Ilenia: Alain. I can't say how much time has passed since that day, but you've grown so much.

Ilenia: If only I could have been there to witness it.

Ilenia: It seems I owe Josef a great deal for raising you in my absence.

Alain: Josef, see my mother somewhere safe.

Josef: And you, Your Highness?

Alain: We end this long-drawn war now.

Nina: Yes, Your Highness. The sigil shall shatter beneath our combined strength.

Baltro: What evil should I reanimate next? A monster capable of crushing you beneath its heel, perhaps.

Alain: Spirits of Zenoira, hear my call.

Alain: Your emperor is no more, and in his place stands a tyrannical fiend who craves nothing but absolute control.

Alain: Tell me, is this what you truly desire? To sacrifice your very essence in service of this daemon?

Alain: Souls of the departed, if you have any humanity left within you, lend me your aid.

Alain: These souls are not a power one can wield, Baltro. They are human lives, human will in its purest form.

Alain: Let us lift the curse of the unicorn and bring the salvation of heaven to these lost souls.

#### Nina and Alain - Ending

Nina: Hm... What do I do?

Mille: You tell our parents, obviously. I can't believe you would get engaged without even mentioning it to them.

Nina: As if I knew such a thing would happen. It caught me off guard as well, you know.

Nina: Though I suppose they should be aware I'm to marry the king.

Sven: Real bold of ya, sayin' yes to a man and not even tellin' the folks.

Kurt: Not like they'd say no to you marryin' into royalty, though.

Bryce: But they'll be happy, as long as you are. I promise you.

Nina: Oh, how surprised they'll be to learn the truth.

Nina: Oh, Alain! I'm certain you've heard, but I have yet to inform my parents about our engagement.

Nina: In any case, nothing they can say can convince me to abandon our marriage.

Bryce: But I'm not stopping any time soon. You break your promise, and you know what happens.

Bryce: No telling what dark corner a rat might be hiding in, after all.

Sven: Looks like Nina's gonna be living in that castle now.

Kurt: Who woulda thought she'd wind up marrying a king, right?

Bryce: Best keep the opinions to yourself, boys. Don't want to make any problems for the happy couple.

Mille: Our family is forever in your debt, my king.

Mille: Allow me to thank you again for taking her under your wing, and aiding me when I needed it most.

### Ochlys

#### Ochlys Joins the Liberation Army

**Alain:** Hm? An angel, here in Cornia? I daresay that is a rare sight.

**Josef:** The orthodoxy reveres them as an extension of the heavenly Father Himself, my prince. Do try to keep your composure.

**Ochlys:** What manner of men stand before me?

**Josef:** I am the knight Josef, faithful retainer to the royal house of Cornia. Beside me is the very commander of the Liberation Army, none but the great Prince Alain.

**Ochlys:** I am well aware of you, Ser Josef. Word of your exploits has long since reached my homeland. My name is Ochlys, Heavenswing Knight of the Palevian Orthodoxy.

**Ochlys:** Swords of the Liberation, I would request kindness from you, if you can spare the time. The church at Rondmort has been seized by a pack of brigands called the Black Talons.

**Ochlys:** I turn my gaze for one ungodly moment, and look what happens. Apologies. Such a profane outburst ill befits one of my angelic stature.

**Ochlys:** Regrettably, my host alone is far lacking the numbers I would need to mount an adequate rescue.

**Alain:** It seems this cleric is damned without our aid. We should help however we are able.

**Ochlys:** My countless thanks, Prince Alain. It is as though the Father Himself delivered you to me.

#### Ochlys and Alain - Leaving Albion

**Alain:** Angels such as you are almost never seen outside Albion, if I understand correctly.

**Ochlys:** You do.

**Alain:** Then what was your reason for leaving, if you do not mind me asking?

**Ochlys:** Ever since I was a young girl, I could not wait to be rid of my home. Thus, when the opportunity arose to work for the Orthodoxy, I took it and traveled the world's churches under orders from our pontifex.

**Ochlys:** Despite my relative inexperience, everyone met my arrival with such incredible warmth. None more so than Sharon, with whom I quickly became remarkably close.

**Ochlys:** What I failed to understand was: were they not the very same race as the pontifex revered?

**Alain:** Then the basis for which you fled your home was...

**Ochlys:** A mistaken one. At which point I returned to Rondmort to live in the manner I believed in.

**Alain:** Even if you felt it to be a warranted one.

**Ochlys:** It was. Of course it was. Which is why I must always stay at her side, to excise the buds of her doubts before they ever blossom into full-grown roses.

**Alain:** I am more than certain you will do just that, Ochlys.

#### Ochlys and Alain - At Your Side

**Ochlys:** I demand to be part of your unit in the next battle, Alain.

**Alain:** Is there a particular reason you are asking?

**Ochlys:** When any wrong move could be the last you make, there can be no greater blessing than a trusted ally.

**Alain:** You mean to imply you trust me, then? I am glad to hear it.

**Ochlys:** That was purely a hypothetical, I will have you know. All I am saying is that your skill is adequate.

**Alain:** Which is a compliment in itself, coming from you. Thank you, Ochlys.

**Ochlys:** You have got some nerve. Hmph. Take it however you want.

**Alain:** Each of us bears strong proficiency with a shield, allowing us to press the attack while keeping our defenses raised. And given the swiftness of your blade and the precision of its thrusts, I know I never need worry when I have you at my side.

**Ochlys:** Ah...

**Alain:** Ochlys?

**Ochlys:** If that is truly how you feel, then you had better just keep me there. At your side, I mean. And you had best not think of doing otherwise. Understand?

**Alain:** I had not realized she cared so much.

#### Ochlys and Alain - Worry

**Alain:** It feels as though I have been seeing much of you lately, even outside of battle.

**Ochlys:** The search will go twice as fast if we work together.

**Alain:** Very well, if that is what you wish. Why do you insist on following me, Ochlys? It is clear now that you think me too helpless to even leave camp alone.

**Alain:** I only said what I did in order to gauge your reaction. In any case, I think I am finally starting to understand you a little better. Thank you, for always worrying about me.

**Alain:** Now I beg of you, lay down your blade.

#### Ring of the Maiden

**Ochlys:** I have come as you asked, Alain. What seems to be the matter?

**Alain:** Ochlys, I'd like you to have the Ring of the Maiden.

**Ochlys:** Explain yourself.

**Alain:** In all this time, I have yet to find another whom I would trust more intensely with my own safety. As for my part, I have worked tirelessly to become a man deserving of one as strong and stunning as you.

**Ochlys:** To be frank, such cloying words set my teeth to grind. But, well, this is hardly the first time I have found myself bemused by your candor. I suppose somewhere along the way, I have actually grown fond of it.

**Ochlys:** Do you understand?

**Alain:** I would rather hear the sentiment in plain words, if you will. How is it that you think of me, Ochlys?

**Ochlys:** You would make me spell it out for you? I will only say this once, so listen well.

**Ochlys:** While I admit you do have a naive air about you, I have never once doubted the keenness of your blade, nor the kindness of your heart. I care for you deeply, Alain.

**Alain:** Would you mind repeating that, just one more time?

**Ochlys:** I certainly would. I already told you, once is all you get.

**Alain:** It is all I could ever dream of. Ochlys, thank you for being there when it felt like nobody else was. I could imagine no greater life than the one spent at your side.

**Ochlys:** Hmph. You have a way with words, I will give you that.

#### Final Battle

**Ochlys:** What is the matter, Alain?

**Galerius:** The ring is mine to command. Now, bow to your emperor!

**Ochlys:** He is still in there. I am certain of it. Take this strength and bring Galerius to his knees!

**Ochlys:** How dare you make me worry.

**Alain:** Galerius, you saw in Fevrith's innocent people mere vessels to house your own fallen empire. But as long as I live and breathe, you will never inflict such callous devastation on our world.

**Alain:** Mother!

**Alain:** We end this long-drawn war now.

**Ochlys:** Indeed. Today shall see centuries of unholy evil finally put to rest.

**Ochlys:** Enough of your prattle, wretched thing.

**Alain:** Spirits of Zenoira, hear my call. Let us lift the curse of the unicorn and bring the salvation of heaven to these lost souls.

#### Ending

**Ochlys:** I suppose this means you have no more need of me. What? I am not upset, if that is what you are implying. merely say the word and I will be at your side. I will be more than glad to drag you back to the real world.

**Sharon:** Poor Alain. I would be more than glad to cure your royal fatigue, should you ever need it.

### Primm

#### Primm and Alain - Hilda

Alain: Do you and Hilda tend to get along, Primm? For sisters, I can't imagine two more different people.

Primm: Well... hm.

Primm: She excelled at anything she laid her hands on, while I was a bit more clumsy and reserved.

Primm: And once she met her wyvern, that distance only grew all the greater.

Alain: I can understand why.

Primm: Though I'd often watch from afar whenever she went into the mountains to greet her newfound friend.

Primm: But I feared, portly girl that I was, the wyverns were more likely to eat me than welcome my presence.

Alain: I hadn't realized they feed on humans.

Primm: Oh, I was just young and afraid, more than anything.

Primm: Until one day, a band of wyvern poachers found me and took me captive.

Alain: How did you end up getting away?

Primm: Hilda and her wyvern saved me.

Primm: And from that day forth, the three of us spent time together just about every day.

Alain: Meaning you finally had the bond of sisterhood you desired.

Primm: Exactly.

Primm: Or at least, I did. The plague struck our home not long after, and I left the region in search of anything that might lead to a cure.

Primm: But that just makes me even happier that I finally got the chance to see her again.

Primm: Thank you for that, Alain.

#### Primm and Alain - Rescue

Primm: Ah! That soldier needs my help.

Alain: You mustn't, Primm. It's too dangerous.

Primm: Even so, I won't abandon him to his fate.

Alain: Wait!

Primm: I'm sorry, Alain. I couldn't just stand and watch while that poor man lost his life.

Primm: I've actually found myself in a similar situation once before, thrust into battle without even a moment's notice.

Primm: And things seemed to work themselves out then as well.

Alain: Perhaps so. Yet you can't always rely on sheer luck to see you through such fits of danger.

Alain: Assuming such fortuity is what emboldens you now, then you had best forget it ever happened.

Primm: Would you? It was the day we first met, Alain.

Alain: Was it, now?

Primm: In your heart too, I think.

Primm: So don't even consider telling me to forget it.

Alain: Primm...

Primm: Even if the world itself was conspiring against me, I still wouldn't have left that soldier to die.

Alain: And I understand how you feel as well. I often find instinct takes over in such life-or-death circumstances.

Alain: Yet if you're ever going to charge off like that, I merely ask that you bring me with you.

Alain: I just couldn't bear to see you alone again.

Primm: The next time this happens, I'll make sure you're right there with me every step of the way.

Primm: I promise you that.

#### Primm and Alain - Ring of the Maiden

Primm: Is there a reason you've asked me here? I thought you needed healing.

Alain: Well, no. Not exactly.

Alain: I'd like you to have the Ring of the Maiden.

Primm: What a lovely little ring! And in such a beautiful place.

Primm: Heheh. It almost sounded like the prince was proposing for a second there.

Alain: That was my intention, yes.

Primm: Oh, how wonderful. I wish all the best to you and, um... me?

Primm: Wait, me?

Alain: There could be none other.

Alain: Ever since you joined our cause, your skill as a cleric has saved countless lives.

Alain: And by swearing an oath upon these rings, we can draw out-

Primm: Sorry, Alain, but do you mind if I gather my thoughts for a second?

Primm: Phew. Now, what were you saying again? I'm ready to hear it this time.

Alain: Well, I was bade to give this ring to the person I care for most.

Alain: And you were the first and only who crossed my mind.

Alain: With every spark of healing magick I witness, it's as though a part of my own heart is restored as well.

Alain: In time, I've come to realize just how much you mean to me. How I couldn't live without you at my side.

Alain: Marry me, Primm, and together we'll build a life more grand than we ever could have dreamed.

Primm: I'm flattered that you think that highly of me. And so immensely happy.

Primm: I would love nothing more than to be your bride, Alain. I accept, a hundred times over.

Alain: Primm, I'll never forget this day: the day we embarked on a beautiful new journey together.

Primm: Heheh. I just worry what my sister will say when she learns I got engaged before her.

#### Primm and Alain - Final Battle

Galerius: End this, now.

Galerius: Hmph.

Galerius: Gah.

Alain: Mother!

Galerius: How does it feel, hm? Your dear mother, slain by your own hand?

Alain: What is happening to me?

Primm: Alain!

Galerius: What a poor fool he was, doomed to the same fate as the pitiful queen before him.

Galerius: You'd simply be volunteering your own as my next vessel.

Galerius: The ring is mine to command, and a futile demise is all that awaits you now.

Galerius: None can ever hope to halt my designs. Bow to your emperor.

Galerius: This day is won by my hand.

Galerius: You will make a fine Zenoiran vessel once it is over.

Galerius: The ring...

Galerius: But why does it hold such vast energy?

Primm: You're still in there, struggling your way back into our world.

Primm: But I won't let you struggle alone.

Galerius: It will take more than this to defeat me.

Primm: Alain!

Alain: Galerius. You saw in Fevrith's innocent people mere vessels to house your own fallen empire.

Alain: But as long as I live and breathe, you'll never inflict such callous devastation on our world.

Galerius: You will not!

Galerius: Their emperor shall never know defeat.

Baltro: Your Majesty.

Galerius: How goes the rite?

Galerius: Then these insects shall be more than enough. Grant me your strength, and we'll stamp them out together.

Galerius: What do you think you're doing?

Baltro: If it wasn't clear, Your Majesty, the sigil seeks none other.

Galerius: Traitorous fool. Finally gone senile, hm?

Alain: Mother!

Ilenia: Ngh.

Primm: Her breathing is steady.

Alain: Speak to me, please.

Ilenia: Alain. I can't say how much time has passed since that day, but you've grown so much.

Ilenia: If only I could have been there to witness it.

Ilenia: It seems I owe Josef a great deal for raising you in my absence.

Alain: Josef, see my mother somewhere safe.

Josef: And you, Your Highness?

Alain: We end this long-drawn war now.

Primm: I'm with you until the final blow is struck, Alain. Let's shatter this cursed sigil together.

Josef: Come home, both of you.

Alain: Spirits of Zenoira, hear my call.

Alain: Your emperor is no more, and in his place stands a tyrannical fiend who craves nothing but absolute control.

Alain: Tell me, is this what you truly desire? To sacrifice your very essence in service of this daemon?

Alain: Souls of the departed, if you have any humanity left within you, lend me your aid.

Alain: These souls are not a power one can wield, Baltro. They are human lives, human will in its purest form.

Alain: Let us lift the curse of the unicorn and bring the salvation of heaven to these lost souls.

#### Primm and Alain - Ending

Primm: That was quite the crowd we had today, wasn't it?

Primm: I could even hear some other women discussing their "admiration" for you.

Primm: Part of me wanted to tell them to keep their eyes off my husband.

Primm: And with you as king, I'm sure there's nowhere else they would rather be.

Hilda: But if you try to solve all of our problems at once, you'll lose your momentum before you ever even get started.

Hilda: Best of luck, Alain. I'm sure you won't need it.

Primm: I worry I might accidentally say the wrong thing, or that others will criticize my lack of manners.

Primm: The good news is, I tend to forget those fears entirely once you're actually in front of me.

### Raenys

#### Raenys Joins the Liberation Army

**Raenys:** Entirely healed, thanks to your aid.

**Alain:** It seems they have dispatched a squadron to the abbey's location.

**Raenys:** Indeed, and this time my arrows shall support your march. Let us be off. Our abbey lies to the southwest of this point. I shall make for its walls at once and inform my allies of what is to come.

**Scarlett:** Come on, Alain. We cannot let her go alone.

**Scarlett:** That is the abbey up ahead, yes?

**Raenys:** It is. They have offered far beyond their means in treatment and lodging for our wounded soldiers.

**Alain:** And now it is only a matter of time before Zenoira's squadron arrives.

**Scarlett:** Then we will just have to prepare the warmest of welcomes for them.

**Albion Soldier:** Our blessings, Lady Raenys. You delivered us from great danger this day.

**Raenys:** And of course, I shall join the battle myself in defense of my people. Thank you again for agreeing to this. I am prepared to join you whenever you choose to depart.

**Raenys:** My people are safe once more, almost wholly to the benevolence of the Liberation Army. The proper thanks eludes me.

**Raenys:** Lady Scarlett, in what felt like a mere moment, you have become a fine young woman.

**Scarlett:** Do you remember? You cried with me that day.

**Raenys:** I have spent many an idle evening since lamenting my decision to remain behind, with only my thoughts to keep me company. I could but imagine how frightened you must have been, how alone.

**Raenys:** The woman before me now is nothing like the sobbing girl I remember.

**Scarlett:** You missed some of my finest hours, I will have you know.

**Raenys:** Yes, I am painfully aware. But I refuse to miss another. My place is at your side, and nowhere else. I only hope Prince Alain sees it the same way.

**Scarlett:** Do they not need you here?

**Raenys:** Perhaps. But we are all of the same mind: we do whatever is necessary to aid the Liberation.

**Scarlett:** Then come. I am sure Alain will be thrilled to hear the news.

**Scarlett:** I promise, Alain. You will not find anyone in Fevrith as loyal as Raenys.

**Alain:** I am more than glad to welcome her to our ranks.

**Raenys:** I shall do whatever I must to not betray that trust.

#### Raenys and Alain - Wings

**Alain:** I should think it rather lucky that Zenoiran arrow hit your back, yes? Better that than risk your wings being injured, I expect.

**Raenys:** Thus, I should have used them to deflect the blow instead of allowing it to strike me unimpeded.

**Alain:** Not to mention, you can fly with them. I must admit, I am somewhat jealous.

**Raenys:** You are?

**Alain:** Ah, my apologies. I suppose that is an impolite thing to say to an angel.

**Raenys:** I once even sought to sever my own wings in an attempt to become one of you.

**Alain:** What could have driven you to do such a thing?

**Raenys:** Angels such as I find it difficult to truly sympathize with the sorrows of humanity. That distance is surely the reason Lady Scarlett left me here the day she departed for Palevian shores.

**Alain:** Only that you are the same woman she remembers from all those years ago.

**Raenys:** Yet the question still plagues my heart. Is it truly appropriate for me to stand beside her?

**Alain:** It is clear in the kindness she has always borne for you, as well as the sheer delight which crossed her face upon your reunion.

**Raenys:** Yes. You are absolutely right, my prince.

#### Raenys and Alain - Kindness to Herself

**Alain:** I came right away when I heard what happened.

**Raenys:** Speaking of whom, we are due to deploy again any minute now, yes? I must return to her at once.

**Alain:** You mustn't forget to turn that kindness inward at times, else you lose sight of what matters most. Stay now, and see to your recovery however necessary.

**Raenys:** You would truly do such a thing?

**Alain:** I would. And I must ask as well: have you hidden any other injuries from me?

**Raenys:** I have.

**Raenys:** Tell me, how do I become as kindhearted as you, my prince? Whenever I speak with you or with Lady Scarlett, I sense an inexpressible warmth lurking somewhere beneath the surface. It seems all I do is cause you pain and distress.

**Alain:** Though it is difficult for us when you fail to look after your own well-being. In my opinion, if you truly wish to show us kindness, you must first learn how to do the same for yourself.

**Raenys:** But how?

**Alain:** All you need do is treat your own health and your own happiness just as you would hers.

**Raenys:** Forgive me for making you explain in such detail.

**Alain:** It is a virtue in which you far exceed anyone else I have ever met.

**Raenys:** I am glad you believe so, my prince.

#### Ring of the Maiden

**Raenys:** My pleasure to see you, my prince. I was told you have need of me?

**Alain:** Raenys, I'd like you to have the Ring of the Maiden.

**Raenys:** Me, ser? But why?

**Alain:** I have seen firsthand the kindness and strength with which you rise in defense of those you love, even when gravely injured yourself. I could hope for no greater qualities from the one who will bear this ring, and soon serve as my queen.

**Raenys:** Such tender words. When I first arrived at this altar, I thought it some manner of mistake, that I could never fulfill a role so grand. Yet hearing the contents of your heart spoken plain has swept my doubts far off into the aether.

**Raenys:** You and I shall change this world, my prince, into a place where none need ever suffer again.

**Alain:** We shall not know rest until it is so. To be with you is everything I could have ever dreamed of. Thank you, Raenys.

**Raenys:** I shall grasp this ring and remember the heavenly moment we shared here, and of course the striking proposal you have graced me with. I love you, Alain.

#### Final Battle

**Raenys:** Alain!

**Galerius:** The ring is mine to command. Now, bow to your emperor!

**Raenys:** A presence this regal could be none other. It is him. Can you hear me, Alain? You must resist. If you fall, even the greatest peace would be forever blemished by utter despair.

**Raenys:** So many need you, believe in you, and love you.

**Alain:** Raenys!

**Alain:** Galerius, you saw in Fevrith's innocent people mere vessels to house your own fallen empire. But as long as I live and breathe, you will never inflict such callous devastation on our world.

**Alain:** Mother!

**Alain:** We end this long-drawn war now.

**Raenys:** I shall stand beside you until the final arrow strikes its mark.

**Raenys:** They shall never do your bidding.

**Alain:** Spirits of Zenoira, hear my call. Let us lift the curse of the unicorn and bring the salvation of heaven to these lost souls.

#### Ending

**Raenys:** Everywhere I looked amidst the coronation, I saw nothing but the unbridled joy of your citizens. 'Tis proof that this world has been born anew, reshaped by your gentle kindness. Wherever my duty may take me, I shall always pray that memory of your deeds continues to echo through these lands, now and for the rest of time.

**Raenys:** Shall we find a seat somewhere, Lady Scarlett? I am certain you must be tired after so much standing.

**Scarlett:** Thank you, Raenys, but I am all right.

**Raenys:** Perhaps a warm cup of tea, to ease the soreness?

**Scarlett:** It has been a long day for all of us, but I am sure I will sleep well tonight.

**Raenys:** Yes. I feel much the same.

**Scarlett:** Not that I am not confident. You will make a great ruler, I know that for a fact.

### Railanor

#### Railanor and Alain - Rosalinde's Happiness

**Railanor:** What is your involvement with Ter Rosalinde? I demand an answer, now.

**Alain:** I am not certain what you mean.

**Railanor:** I mean to determine what it is you think of her.

**Alain:** Hm. If pressed for an answer, I would say she is a fine ally indeed in the fight against Zenoira.

**Railanor:** And? What else?

**Alain:** You want more? Unless, perhaps, there is a deeper reason than that.

**Railanor:** How very interesting. If this is the man that Ter Rosalinde has chosen, then so be it. I approve.

**Alain:** Approve of what, exactly?

**Railanor:** Nothing you need worry yourself over. I thank you for the assistance, Alain.

**Alain:** I am not certain I understand what just happened.

#### Railanor and Alain - A Failed Scheme

**Railanor:** Ter Rosalinde awaits you beneath the light of the moon, my prince. Go to her.

**Alain:** I am sorry?

**Railanor:** I hope this tryst is as enjoyable for you as it surely will be for her.

**Alain:** Slow down a moment, please. What is it you expect from me?

**Railanor:** As I said before, I wish for you to appease Ter Rosalinde. Now get over there this instant.

**Alain:** And have you told her I would be coming?

**Railanor:** Ngh!

**Alain:** Are you hurt?

**Railanor:** I am fine. Only a mere twist of the ankle.

**Alain:** Here, allow me to carry you to the healer.

**Railanor:** Leave me be. I beg you, you mustn't miss your rendezvous with Ter Rosalinde.

**Alain:** This is not the time for your schemes, Railanor. I will only speak with her after I am certain you are better.

**Railanor:** Ah!

**Alain:** I suggest you seek out Rosalinde after this as well. She seemed rather worried about you when I told her what happened.

**Railanor:** All of my failed schemes, as you so eloquently put it...

**Alain:** So please, take this opportunity to revel in a bout of much-deserved rest.

**Railanor:** Alain...

**Alain:** What is it?

**Railanor:** I do not know what I have done to earn such sympathy from you.

**Alain:** In any event, I should be going now. The others have need of me back in camp.

**Rosalinde:** There you are, Railanor. I was so worried about you I could barely sleep.

**Railanor:** Forgive me, Terras.

**Rosalinde:** The only thing I want is for you to take better care of yourself.

**Railanor:** Then that is precisely what I will do.

#### Ring of the Maiden

**Railanor:** You summoned me, Alain?

**Alain:** I'd like you to have the Ring of the Maiden.

**Railanor:** Surely you have not thought the matter through if you are asking this of me.

**Alain:** I have. I could imagine none other serving the role, Railanor. I hope I have not offended you.

**Railanor:** Not in the slightest. You are an exceptional man, possessed of a strong heart and mind, and above all, a kindness few can match.

**Railanor:** In truth, my feelings for you have grown unabated since the day you so warmly tended to my leg. To hear those words cross my ears has brought me a greater joy than I ever thought possible.

**Alain:** Our time together has been brief, perhaps. Yet I have observed the grace with which you conduct yourself, the selflessness. Such qualities have seen you occupy a genuinely cherished place in my heart.

**Railanor:** Alain...

**Alain:** Would you do me this honor?

**Railanor:** Yes. A hundred times, yes. I will treasure this ring for as long as I live.

**Alain:** And I, the happiest man.

#### Final Battle

**Railanor:** Alain?

**Galerius:** The ring is mine to command. Now, bow to your emperor!

**Railanor:** Looks like I am not the only one fighting back. Come then, Alain. Let us show him what we are capable of.

**Alain:** Railanor!

**Alain:** Galerius, you saw in Fevrith's innocent people mere vessels to house your own fallen empire. But as long as I live and breathe, you will never inflict such callous devastation on our world.

**Railanor:** How does he still stand? Though, his desperation is written on his face.

**Alain:** Mother!

**Railanor:** Be calm, Alain. Her breathing is firm and steady.

**Alain:** We end this long-drawn war now.

**Railanor:** Defeat is only possible once Baltro lies slain by our hand.

**Railanor:** You will come to regret those words.

**Alain:** Spirits of Zenoira, hear my call. Let us lift the curse of the unicorn and bring the salvation of heaven to these lost souls.

#### Ending

**Railanor:** Though my body remains in service of Elheim, know that my heart will forever be yours, Alain.

**Railanor:** Pardon the query, Terras, but were you able to eat enough at the banquet?

**Rosalinde:** I could eat Cornian food every week of the year and never tire of it.

**Railanor:** It might prove a challenge procuring ingredients from Cornia at such frequency, but...

**Rosalinde:** Please, Railanor. Do not trouble yourself. It was just a figure of speech.

**Railanor:** Ah. And yet I still wish to see your every wish fulfilled.

**Rosalinde:** But that is when you arrived. I am not sure you realize just how much it meant in that moment, but thank you, Alain. Truly.

**Rosalinde:** I must have let my guard down now that the war is over.

### Ramona

#### Ramona and Alain - Birds and Mushrooms

**Ramona:** What marvelous architecture. Though in truth, nothing could be more wonderful than the unspoiled nature of these lands.

**Alain:** Indeed. Not even Cornia can boast such verdant forests.

**Ramona:** Yet I will not deny your nation bears far more greenery than ours, at least. Hm?

**Alain:** What is it, Ramona?

**Ramona:** Look above us there, in the sky. Have you ever seen such magnificent birds before?

**Alain:** Only in Elheim, I suppose. They have quite the striking features now that I observe them more closely.

**Ramona:** Likely as a means of adapting to their environment. All life in Fevrith has developed in such a manner. Speaking of birds, there exists a breed in Bastorias which can swim through the ocean with all the elegance of a noble carp.

**Alain:** It must feel wonderful, to possess the freedom to roam either sky or sea whenever the fancy strikes.

**Ramona:** Alas, that particular variety of bird is incapable of conventional flight entirely. But...

**Ramona:** Ah, what a lustrous glow these mushrooms boast. I wonder what they taste like. Best to ask in town if they are poisonous first. If only there were a library I could consult on the matter.

**Alain:** You truly are similar, you know.

**Ramona:** I am sorry?

**Alain:** I speak of you and Yunifi, of course. Your mannerisms are nigh identical.

**Ramona:** You mean to imply I am as excitable as a teenage girl?

**Ramona:** still, I cannot exactly help myself. There is so much of the world I have never seen, having lived in Bastorias my entire life.

**Alain:** I understand how you feel. After all, you never know what wonders may await behind a neighboring tree or a distant mountain.

**Ramona:** It appears the two of us have more in common than I realized.

**Alain:** 'Tis a welcome surprise, yes. I must admit, I am impressed you noticed these birds at all, given how far away from them we stood.

**Ramona:** Do not be. The eyes of an owl are inherently a great deal keener than those of a human.

**Alain:** A natural disadvantage, is it?

**Ramona:** Unfortunately, yes. But feel free to let me know if you ever discover something I have not.

**Alain:** So I shall.

#### Ramona and Alain - Fish Stew

**Alain:** What is it you are doing out here?

**Ramona:** I thought to welcome back the evening's patrol with a hearty meal fit for even the most weary of bestrals.

**Alain:** You must care deeply for your brethren if you are willing to put in such effort for them.

**Ramona:** I hope you enjoy. It is my own personal recipe, honed and heightened through years of steady refinement.

**Alain:** It looks wonderful, Ramona. And what is it, exactly?

**Ramona:** Just about every family does it their own special way, and this particular technique is mine alone.

**Alain:** What a delicious stew it is. Rich in flavor, yet gentle on the palate as well.

**Ramona:** As I am sure you know, Alain, Bastorias has historically had limited relations with the other lands of Fevrith. For better or worse, the majority of bestrals are wholly indifferent to the outside world. We would much rather focus on our own affairs than concern ourselves in those of others.

**Ramona:** Just as the manifold bestral bloodlines strive to help one another, so too should the disparate nations of Fevrith.

**Alain:** I very much agree.

**Ramona:** As for this future you struggle so valiantly to achieve, do you picture bestrals to be a part of it?

**Alain:** I do. I am confident that conversations such as these will engender a world where all races can live in harmony.

**Ramona:** What a pure, noble soul you are. I pray for your success in making the future you believe in an eventual reality.

**Alain:** Together, I have no doubt we shall do so, Ramona.

**Ramona:** Heheh. Now come, eat your stew before the frigid air steals all its warmth.

#### Ring of the Maiden

**Ramona:** Hello there, Alain. What is it you wish to discuss with me?

**Alain:** Ramona, I'd like you to have the Ring of the Maiden.

**Ramona:** I anticipated this from the moment I was summoned forth to this altar, though I cannot say I have found the decision easy.

**Alain:** You should. Do you remember what you said to me? How you dreamt of a future where humans and bestrals can live in harmony, free from the bounds of race or nationality?

**Alain:** In that moment, I knew with you at my side, nothing is impossible, not even the salvation of Fevrith. So please, accept this ring, and together we shall make both of our dreams into the brightest reality.

**Ramona:** My word. Even after all my years on this earth, there is truly no telling what surprises life may have in store.

**Ramona:** If I recall correctly, you spoke much the same regarding the future of our two peoples, how you believed they could overcome their differences and march as one to the same beat.

**Ramona:** You should know that I share your hunger for peace, not merely for Bastorias, but for the world over. I could never spurn the chance to bring such a transformation to pass. I accept, with great pride.

**Alain:** I had faith you would. Thank you, Ramona.

**Ramona:** Let this rite serve as the first step toward a new dawn, for bestral, man, elf, and all life on Fevrith and beyond.

**Alain:** We will make it so, you and I together.

**Ramona:** And once we do, we can mark the occasion with a hearty bowl of fresh fish stew.

**Alain:** My mouth is watering already.

#### Final Battle

**Ramona:** Are you all right, Alain?

**Galerius:** The ring is mine to command. Now, bow to your emperor!

**Ramona:** 'Tis a horror inconceivable.

**Ramona:** Hmph. I knew you would not abandon us so easily. Come, let us deliver our world from this boundless nightmare.

**Alain:** Ramona!

**Alain:** Galerius, you saw in Fevrith's innocent people mere vessels to house your own fallen empire. But as long as I live and breathe, you will never inflict such callous devastation on our world.

**Alain:** Mother!

**Ramona:** You need not worry, Alain. The breath of life still flows through her, and strongly at that.

**Alain:** We end this long-drawn war now.

**Ramona:** Indeed we shall, for every living thing that has suffered under Zenoira's tyranny.

**Alain:** Spirits of Zenoira, hear my call. Let us lift the curse of the unicorn and bring the salvation of heaven to these lost souls.

#### Ending

**Ramona:** Today's ceremony will surely go down in the annals of history, Alain. 'Tis the birth of a new king, and a day when human and bestral at last join arm in arm, just as you promised.

**Ramona:** We can make a feast of it, punctuated by my finest fish stew.

**Ramona:** I must say, I cannot help but admire the sight of it.

**Yunifi:** Everyone saw you studying the brickwork up on the parapets earlier.

**Ramona:** Did you, now? I was not aware my inclinations were that transparent. Though I find it rather embarrassing to have been caught in the act.

### Renault

#### Renault Recruited

Laurent: No matter. The knight-errant Laurent shall see you exterminated down to the very last.

Alain: That's not a name I'm familiar with. Who is he?

Laurent: Now prepare to be run through by the knight-errant Laurent.

Clive: Come. Dispense of that helm and lend your lance to the Liberation.

Laurent: I know not of who you speak.

Laurent: And even if I did, that man perished ten years ago.

Laurent: Now meet your end at the hands of the errant-knight Laurent.

Travis: It's like he's straight out of a faerie tale.

Lex: Yeah? I'm not too big on books, sorry.

Renault: Prince Alain, and Hodrick too.

Hodrick: Have you found peace?

Renault: Unable to bear the weight of my sins, I've traveled these lands in search of some end.

Renault: But it was all an egoistic crusade in the end.

Renault: There is no unmaking the suffering these people have endured under Zenoiran rule.

Renault: They, and the very land itself, grow weary from a decade of war. Famine, plague.

Renault: And I, inadequate as I am alone, could never hope to end their gruesome reign.

Renault: Before such cruel reality, I am utterly powerless.

Clive: If I may, Ser Renault.

Clive: No action can hope to quell the flames of regret. They burn on, ever darkening our minds and consuming our pasts.

Clive: Yet their blaze is not the end of all things. You would see that, should you only turn your gaze forward.

Clive: Forward, to hope. And to the future of all those we hold dear. For there can be no greater treasure than that.

Clive: You said such words yourself, ser. That conviction was ever the paradigm I aspired to achieve.

Renault: You've grown stronger than you realize, Clive.

Renault: It is just as you say.

Renault: No action I take can undo the sins I've wrought upon this continent.

Renault: I shall serve as your spear until the day comes that we've shattered Zenoira's foul tyranny over this land.

Renault: As long as I live and breathe, I am yours to command.

#### Renault and Alain - A Knight of the People

Renault: I fear you may mistakenly be struck by a stone originally intended for me.

Renault: Many in these lands surely harbor great resentment for the deeds I've committed.

Renault: Save your sympathy for one who's worthy of it, rather than waste its blessings on a man such as I.

Alain: Perhaps not consciously.

Renault: But I can never forgive myself for the sins committed in my name.

Renault: Why are you doing this for me, Your Highness?

Renault: In your presence, I shall once more serve as a knight of my people, just as I did so many years ago.

#### Renault and Alain - Ring of the Maiden

Renault: Your Highness, I beg you. Exclude me from your thoughts and offer the rite to one more deserving of its grace.

Alain: I'd like you to have the Ring of the Maiden.

Renault: Please, my prince. I could never be worthy of such an immense honor.

Alain: That's where you're wrong. You need only lift your gaze to see it.

Alain: Listen well, Renault.

Alain: I could never hope to defeat Zenoira without the flame of virtue which glows deep within you.

Renault: Your Highness, I've never met as generous a soul in all my days.

Renault: Even should my body crumble and my flame be reduced to mere ash, I shall never rest until we see Galerius slain.

Alain: Hold, Renault. I would ask you an indulgence first.

Renault: You need only name the thing, and it is yours.

Alain: Zenoira's demise would mean naught if we lose that wellspring of devotion in the process.

Alain: So I ask that you live on in service of our fair nation long after this battle is won.

Alain: And to be frank, I could not bear to lose you.

Renault: Such kindness moves me beyond the limit of words, Your Highness.

Renault: I swear to you, we shall greet tomorrow together and march onward with renewed health and vigor.

Alain: Our covenant is sealed. You have my thanks, Renault.

Renault: And you mine. This humble knight shall never know defeat.

Renault: That, and I promise to prove myself worthy of the honor.

#### Renault and Alain - Final Battle

Galerius: End this, now.

Galerius: Hmph.

Galerius: Gah.

Alain: Mother!

Galerius: How does it feel, hm? Your dear mother, slain by your own hand?

Alain: What is happening to me?

Renault: Hold your composure, Your Highness.

Galerius: What a poor fool he was, doomed to the same fate as the pitiful queen before him.

Galerius: His strength surpasses even Ilenia's. The might of the unicorn runs deep in his veins.

Galerius: strike at this new body of mine, if you dare.

Galerius: You'd simply be volunteering your own as my next vessel.

Galerius: The ring is mine to command, and a futile demise is all that awaits you now.

Galerius: None can ever hope to halt my designs. Bow to your emperor.

Renault: No...

Galerius: This day is won.

Galerius: You will make a fine Zenoiran vessel once it is over.

Galerius: Enough. Can't you see it's over?

Galerius: The ring...

Galerius: But why does it hold such vast energy?

Renault: I knew you weren't lost to us, my prince.

Renault: Now, the future we seek is close at hand. Wrest yourself free from this scourge's grasp, and sound the knell of Zenoira's demise.

Galerius: It will take more than this to defeat me.

Renault: Your Highness!

Alain: Galerius. You saw in Fevrith's innocent people mere vessels to house your own fallen empire.

Alain: But as long as I live and breathe, you'll never inflict such callous devastation on our world.

Galerius: How do you know of that?

Galerius: You will not!

Galerius: Their emperor shall never know defeat.

Baltro: Your Majesty.

Galerius: How goes the rite?

Galerius: Then these insects shall be more than enough. Grant me your strength, and we'll stamp them out together.

Galerius: What do you think you're doing?

Baltro: If it wasn't clear, Your Majesty, the sigil seeks none other.

Galerius: Traitorous fool. Finally gone senile, hm?

Alain: Mother!

Ilenia: Ngh.

Renault: 'Tis a miracle made manifest. Her Majesty is unharmed.

Alain: Speak to me, please.

Alain: Josef, see my mother somewhere safe.

Josef: And you, Your Highness?

Alain: We end this long-drawn war now.

Renault: Baltro and his dark rite shall torment these lands no longer.

Josef: Come home, both of you.

Baltro: What evil should I reanimate next? A monster capable of crushing you beneath its heel, perhaps.

Renault: They are not your marionettes.

Alain: Spirits of Zenoira, hear my call.

Alain: Your emperor is no more, and in his place stands a tyrannical fiend who craves nothing but absolute control.

Alain: Tell me, is this what you truly desire? To sacrifice your very essence in service of this daemon?

Alain: Souls of the departed, if you have any humanity left within you, lend me your aid.

Alain: These souls are not a power one can wield, Baltro. They are human lives, human will in its purest form.

Alain: Let us lift the curse of the unicorn and bring the salvation of heaven to these lost souls.

#### Renault and Alain - Ending

Renault: I've only the utmost gratitude for all these kindnesses and more, my king.

Renault: Hence, I hereby enter a life of servitude in your royal name. I only pray it is enough.

Renault: I'm grateful, old friend.

Hodrick: Yet words shall only carry us so far. Come. Let us dedicate our strength to Cornia reborn.

Hodrick: I pray you share with us the burdens of the crown, rather than attempt to shoulder them entirely yourself.

Hodrick: Though no matter the circumstance, you will have my undying support as captain of the royal guard.

Hodrick: Shall we, Renault? Our work here is far from finished.

Renault: But of course. Let us be off at once.

Josef: Much has transpired on our path toward this moment, Your Majesty.

Josef: Though in truth, bearing witness to your ascension, assisting it in some meager way, will always be my greatest treasure.

Josef: I can still remember when you were but a child. Ah, how you've grown since our days on Palevia, my king.

### Ridiel

#### Ridiel and Alain - Her Mother's Painting

Alain: Are you ready to go now, Ridiel?

Ridiel: I am. Sorry for making you come all the way to my house with me.

Ridiel: Look, I grabbed a little something to remember my mom by.

Alain: It is a marvelous painting, Ridiel. You could hardly tell from looking at it, especially in the manner her sword gleams in the sunlight.

Ridiel: Looking back on it now, I think I realized just how impossible a reality this old thing depicted.

Alain: I am sorry, Ridiel.

Ridiel: After that, it was painful even looking at it, so I shoved it in a closet and tried to forget instead.

Alain: I can only imagine how proud it would make her to know you have inherited her bitter struggle against Zenoira.

Alain: I must know, Ridiel. What were you like as a child?

Ridiel: Where is this coming from?

Alain: I could not say. I am just curious, I suppose.

Ridiel: Sure, if that is what you want.

Ridiel: I had plenty of friends I used to play with, none of whom cared who I was or where I was from.

Ridiel: But the older we got, the less they treated me like one of their own.

Ridiel: It hurt almost as much as losing every friend you have ever known.

Alain: I hope to create a kingdom where none will have to suffer as you have, ever again.

Ridiel: Knowing you, I have a feeling you might just do it.

Alain: Let us pray you are right.

#### Ridiel and Alain - A Place in Cornia

Alain: How would you feel about settling in Cornia, Ridiel? After the end of this war, I mean.

Ridiel: Again, you find a way to catch me off guard.

Alain: That was not my intent. Our prior conversation gave me a fair amount to consider.

Alain: With the start of each day, we put our differences behind us and labor to reach a common goal.

Alain: I want you to be a part of that, Ridiel.

Ridiel: I am not sure Josef would agree with you there.

Alain: The only words he speaks of you now are praise for the excellent work you do in our name.

Ridiel: You are too kind, Prince. I know you are only doing this to make me feel better.

Ridiel: In the past, I would have hated you for taking pity on me.

Ridiel: Turns out all this time I have spent with you and your little army has changed who I am.

Alain: For the better, in my view.

Alain: It pleases me to know the Liberation is able to provide the same comfort for you.

Ridiel: I would not want that kindness of yours to go unanswered, now would I?

#### Ridiel and Alain - Ring of the Maiden

Ridiel: I hear you have something for me, Prince?

Alain: I would like you to have the Ring of the Maiden.

Ridiel: This is not something to joke about. And at a time like this, no less.

Alain: It is no joke. I wish for you to accept this ring from the deepest depths of my heart.

Ridiel: But that means you... We...

Alain: Is it truly such a startling suggestion? I believe I have made my feelings quite clear.

Ridiel: I guess I have picked up on it, but still. Who goes thrusting a ring out of nowhere? The shock killed me.

Alain: You are right. I should never have surprised you like this.

Ridiel: It is funny. All my life, I cursed my mother for settling down with a human.

Ridiel: I swore I would never follow the same path, not in a thousand years.

Ridiel: But you have changed my mind. I will wear that ring with pride.

Alain: I could not ask for anything more. Thank you, Ridiel.

Ridiel: Guess that makes it official, then. Hope you are ready to spoil me.

#### Ridiel and Alain - Final Battle

Galerius: End this, now.

Galerius: Hmph.

Galerius: Gah.

Alain: Mother!

Galerius: How does it feel, hm? Your dear mother, slain by your own hand.

Alain: What is happening to me?

Ridiel: Alain!

Galerius: What a poor fool he was, doomed to the same fate as the pitiful queen before him.

Galerius: His strength surpasses even Ilenia's. The might of the unicorn runs deep in his veins.

Galerius: You would simply be volunteering your own as my next vessel.

Galerius: The ring is mine to command, and a futile demise is all that awaits you now.

Galerius: None can ever hope to halt my designs. Bow to your emperor.

Galerius: You will make a fine Zenoiran vessel once it is over.

Galerius: The ring... why does it hold such vast energy?

Ridiel: It is you. I know it is.

Galerius: It will take more than this to defeat me.

Ridiel: You are back, just like you should be.

Alain: Galerius. You saw in Fevrith's innocent people mere vessels to house your own fallen empire.

Alain: But as long as I live and breathe, you will never inflict such callous devastation on our world.

Galerius: How do you know of that?

Galerius: You will not!

Galerius: Their emperor shall never know defeat.

Baltro: Your Majesty.

Galerius: How goes the rite?

Galerius: Then these insects shall be more than enough. Grant me your strength, and we will stamp them out together.

Baltro: If it was not clear, Your Majesty, the sigil seeks none other.

Galerius: Traitorous fool. Finally gone senile, hm?

Alain: Mother!

Ilenia: Ngh.

Ridiel: I can feel her heart beating from here. She is all right, Alain.

Alain: Speak to me, please.

Josef: I never imagined he possessed such frightful mastery over the bodies of others.

Ilenia: Alain. I cannot say how much time has passed since that day, but you have grown so much.

Ilenia: If only I could have been there to witness it.

Ilenia: It seems I owe Josef a great deal for raising you in my absence.

Alain: Josef, see my mother somewhere safe.

Josef: And you, Your Highness?

Alain: We end this long-drawn war now.

Josef: Come home, both of you.

Baltro: What evil should I reanimate next? A monster capable of crushing you beneath its heel, perhaps.

Ridiel: Say whatever you want, Baltro.
