### Rolf

#### Rolf and Alain - First Meeting

Alain: I take it you are the one they call Rolf.

Clive: We stand with the Liberation.

Alain: That is precisely why we have come. We confront them together.

Alain: You have some skill, Rolf, to be able to hit your mark from such a great distance.

Rolf: As I would hope for a lifelong hunter, yes.

Rolf: By the way, my prince, would you rather have fowl or boar for dinner?

Rolf: Lex asked me to gather provisions, but I find myself struck with an annoying case of decision paralysis. Just pick one, please.

Rolf: An excellent choice. Thank you, my prince.

Lex: You got that meat I asked for?

Rolf: Indeed. A wild turkey from the local forest.

Lex: Not sure I have ever cooked one of those. Think I am better off roasting it, tossing it in a stew, or...

Rolf: Do you mind if I take until morning to think it over?

Lex: Morning? I am supposed to be making dinner tonight.

#### Rolf and Alain - Dreams of Peace

Alain: You used to be a hunter, yes, Rolf? How did you forego that in favor of organizing a local militia?

Rolf: I wanted to protect the peace of our towns and villages. That simply was not going to happen otherwise.

Rolf: It helps that we have a reliable commander leading the charge.

Alain: I appreciate that.

Alain: Yet I must return the compliment. Not every man is capable of mustering an armed force for the sake of others.

Rolf: Peace for the towns and villages of this land is reward enough for me.

Alain: There can be no greater reward.

Rolf: So please, grant me the honor of remaining ever close to you.

Rolf: Together, we can finally bring our dreams of peace to fruition.

Alain: I could want nothing more, Rolf.

#### Rolf and Alain - Ring of the Maiden

Rolf: You called for me, Your Highness?

Alain: I would like you to have the Ring of the Maiden.

Rolf: Me, ser?

Alain: You possess an undying sense of justice, one which leaves you unwilling to overlook even the most banal of evils.

Alain: Not to mention the kindness that compels you to aid any who need it, and ultimately win back an entire continent.

Alain: I would like to chase that dream at your side, Rolf, and this ring serves as a symbol of that desire.

Rolf: Such a thing is far too precious for a man like me.

Rolf: And yet, I know well your aim in this grand conquest. You fight not for riches, nor the sweet taste of glory.

Alain: There is but one prize I hope to claim.

Alain: Just so. I take it you will accept, then?

Rolf: Gladly. I share the same desire, Alain, and together we will make it manifest.

Alain: So we shall.

Rolf: Try as they may to tear us apart, my prince, I will never leave your side. I swear my very life upon it.

#### Rolf and Alain - Final Battle

Galerius: Hmph.

Galerius: Gah.

Alain: Mother!

Galerius: How does it feel, hm? Your dear mother, slain by your own hand.

Alain: What is happening to me?

Rolf: Your Highness!

Galerius: What a poor fool he was, doomed to the same fate as the pitiful queen before him.

Galerius: His strength surpasses even Ilenia's. The might of the unicorn runs deep in his veins.

Galerius: You would simply be volunteering your own as my next vessel.

Galerius: The ring is mine to command, and a futile demise is all that awaits you now.

Galerius: None can ever hope to halt my designs. Bow to your emperor.

Rolf: Galerius!

Galerius: The ring... why does it hold such vast energy?

Rolf: It is you, Alain. I am sure. You have to fight him. Do you hear me?

Galerius: It will take more than this to defeat me.

Rolf: Alain!

Alain: Galerius. You saw in Fevrith's innocent people mere vessels to house your own fallen empire.

Alain: But as long as I live and breathe, you will never inflict such callous devastation on our world.

Galerius: You will not!

Galerius: Their emperor shall never know defeat.

Baltro: Your Majesty.

Galerius: How goes the rite?

Galerius: Then these insects shall be more than enough. Grant me your strength, and we will stamp them out together.

Galerius: What do you think you are doing?

Baltro: If it was not clear, Your Majesty, the sigil seeks none other.

Galerius: Traitorous fool. Finally gone senile, hm?

Alain: Mother!

Ilenia: Ngh.

Rolf: She is all right, merely unconscious.

Alain: Speak to me, please.

Alain: We end this long-drawn war now.

Rolf: Baltro will rue the day he ever set foot in our lands.

Josef: Come home, both of you.

Baltro: What evil should I reanimate next? A monster capable of crushing you beneath its heel, perhaps.

Rolf: Cease your foul words, wretch. We send you to the dark void beyond.

Alain: Spirits of Zenoira, hear my call.

Alain: Your emperor is no more, and in his place stands a tyrannical fiend who craves nothing but absolute control.

Alain: Tell me, is this what you truly desire? To sacrifice your very essence in service of this daemon?

Alain: Souls of the departed, if you have any humanity left within you, lend me your aid.

Alain: These souls are not a power one can wield, Baltro. They are human lives, human will in its purest form.

Alain: Let us lift the curse of the unicorn and bring the salvation of heaven to these lost souls.

#### Rolf and Alain - Ending

Rolf: What a vast burden.

Rolf: But I can think of no burden more agreeable, and none I would rather face it with.

Rolf: I only hope I can serve you as well in peace as I have in war.

Rolf: My bow is ever in your service, Your Majesty. Simply give the order and I will be there.

#### Rolf and Alain - Dinner Provisions

Alain: You truly are an exceptional archer, Rolf.

Rolf: It is only natural for a hunter. Though I suppose this skill serves us well in the army, too.

Alain: Lex mentioned he asked you to gather provisions for tonight.

Rolf: He did. That is the problem. I cannot decide whether fowl or boar would be best for dinner.

Alain: Then why not start with the turkey you just shot?

Rolf: A sensible suggestion. I will bring it back to camp.

Lex: So, Rolf. How are we cooking this turkey?

Rolf: I should like until morning to consider it.

Lex: Morning? We need dinner tonight!

#### Rolf and Alain - Reason to Fight

Alain: Rolf, you were a hunter before all this. What made you organize the local militia?

Rolf: I wanted to protect the peace of my town. Of every town and village like it.

Alain: Then you made the right choice. I appreciate your conviction, and I will see it rewarded.

Rolf: No reward is necessary. Peace for the towns and villages is reward enough.

Alain: You know exactly why you fight.

Rolf: And I know who I wish to fight beside. Together, I believe we can bring that dream of peace to fruition.

### Rosalinde

#### Rosalinde and Alain - Reading

**Rosalinde:** Boo.

**Alain:** Ah! Please do not scare me like that when I am reading, Rosalinde.

**Rosalinde:** Sorry, I could not help myself, seeing you standing there all defenseless.

**Alain:** It is odd, though. You seemed nothing like this when first we met.

**Rosalinde:** Like what?

**Alain:** Friendly, I suppose. You struck me more as a formal princess than one who would play tricks on her commander.

**Rosalinde:** So I thought I would show you a little bit of who I really am, too.

**Alain:** Well, I cannot fault your logic.

**Rosalinde:** Unless you are saying you liked me better before?

**Alain:** You are standing rather close to me, Rosalinde.

**Rosalinde:** Is there something wrong with that?

**Alain:** Not as such, no. It is only that it is impossible to read with my book covered in your shadow.

**Rosalinde:** Ah, yes. Your reading. Perhaps I would not mind joining you in that venture myself. Do not worry, I will make certain I do not obstruct your view.

**Alain:** So much for my quiet afternoon.

#### Rosalinde and Alain - The Burden

**Rosalinde:** Hm? Oh. I must have fallen asleep for a moment.

**Alain:** And deeply at that. Have you been getting enough rest of late?

**Rosalinde:** No, actually. Why did you not wake me up? I am certain my head was rather heavy on your shoulder.

**Alain:** I admit, I did consider it. Yet you seemed peaceful, Rosalinde, without a single trouble in all the world.

**Rosalinde:** Heheh. It feels like it was only yesterday you would lose your composure the minute I drew near to you. Not that I am complaining, of course, but it is barely even half as enjoyable teasing you anymore.

**Alain:** Then all the better, in my view. By the way, Rosalinde, you were speaking in your sleep just now.

**Rosalinde:** Something about wanting to spend more time with you, I assume?

**Alain:** "Why was she chosen instead of me?" I surmise you were speaking of Eltolinde becoming the next Turenos.

**Rosalinde:** Zenoira took my sister from me. Used her body for their vile schemes. The thought alone sets my blood to boil. If only I had been chosen in her place, she never would have gotten her mind taken over by that damned witch.

**Alain:** You wish such harm could have befallen you instead?

**Rosalinde:** Either way, the only thing I can do now is make sure nobody else gets hurt ever again. Thank you for the shoulder, Alain. That was a better sleep than I have had in months.

**Alain:** I merely pray it was to your benefit.

#### Rosalinde and Alain - Sharing Pain

**Alain:** Regarding our recent conversation, Rosalinde...

**Rosalinde:** Do you mean the one we had during our last battle? Or the time I kept you from reading your book?

**Alain:** Neither, in fact. I speak of the day you fell asleep on my shoulder.

**Rosalinde:** What about it?

**Alain:** You would gladly bear such pain alone before you ever considered sharing it with another.

**Rosalinde:** I cannot disagree with that. So trust me, it is better that way.

**Alain:** You are wrong. Compared to you, I am akin to a newborn child, ignorant to the ways of the outside world. All the same, I cannot abide the thought of you weathering these wounds alone for even a day, let alone the rest of your life.

**Rosalinde:** Well, isn't this a surprise. I have never met a human with this much insight into the sorrows my kind can face.

**Alain:** I dare say I would not have realized without it.

**Rosalinde:** All that from a few mumbled words? Very well, Alain. I will do as you ask. But might I make a request of you as well?

**Alain:** What is it?

**Rosalinde:** Stay with me. That way I will know for sure I am not trying to shoulder everything alone.

**Alain:** It would be my greatest honor.

#### The Covenant

**Rosalinde:** Looks like I was right.

**Alain:** What do I do next?

**Rosalinde:** Come back here with the person chosen for the rite. Offer them the Ring of the Maiden, and you are done, that is, if they accept. Doing so should unleash the power stored deep within your own ring.

**Alain:** Is there more?

**Rosalinde:** The covenant between unicorn and maiden requires both sides to be of one mind and one heart. If either betrayed the pact they swore at this altar, they would face terrible consequences. At least, according to the text.

**Alain:** I will have to keep that in mind.

**Rosalinde:** You are a little close, Alain. Is there someone you are thinking of asking? Considering the risk, I would suggest you give the ring to the person you trust most. Or the elf.

**Alain:** Could you perhaps stand back a bit?

**Rosalinde:** I see someone's made up his mind.

#### Ring of the Maiden

**Alain:** Rosalinde, I'd like you to have the Ring of the Maiden.

**Rosalinde:** You realize accepting would make me the queen of Cornia, yes?

**Alain:** Rosalinde, from the very bottom of my heart, I love you. I want nothing more than to spend the rest of my days at your side.

**Rosalinde:** Well, that is more like it. I am ready. This is the happiest day of my life. I might not have been chosen as Turenos, but to be chosen by you is all the greater.

**Rosalinde:** Just know I will be awfully furious if you go dying before me.

**Alain:** I am not sure that is a demand I can meet. Elves live for far longer than mere humans, after all.

**Rosalinde:** Well, if it means ruling beside you, I could try holding on just a bit longer.

#### Final Battle

**Rosalinde:** Alain! Are you...

**Galerius:** The ring is mine to command. Now, bow to your emperor!

**Rosalinde:** Alain's spirit is calling out to me.

**Alain:** Rosalinde...

**Rosalinde:** Alain! I thought I had lost you.

**Alain:** Galerius, you saw in Fevrith's innocent people mere vessels to house your own fallen empire. But as long as I live and breathe, you will never inflict such callous devastation on our world.

**Alain:** Mother!

**Rosalinde:** Do not worry. She is stable.

**Alain:** We end this long-drawn war now.

**Rosalinde:** I will be with you arm in arm through every breath of it.

**Eltolinde:** Today, this horror shall reach its conclusion.

**Rosalinde:** This time, uin nisa, no harm will come to you.

**Rosalinde:** If it is a monster you are after...

**Alain:** Spirits of Zenoira, hear my call. Let us lift the curse of the unicorn and bring the salvation of heaven to these lost souls.

#### Ending

**Rosalinde:** still, I could never be happier than when I am with you, my darling.

**Rosalinde:** Oh? Is that blushing I see? It makes me proud to be your queen, Alain.

**Rosalinde:** Hold on, Alain. I thought maybe you would want to stay with me until it died down. You know, so nobody else would see you like this.

**Rosalinde:** And I think that just made it worse. Seems you are stuck with me, then.

**Railanor:** Congratulations again, Your Majesty.

**Railanor:** Pardon the query, Terras, but you seemed rather busy at the banquet. Were you able to eat enough?

**Rosalinde:** I could eat Cornian food every meal of the day and never tire of it.

**Railanor:** Then I have no choice but to study their cuisine, that I may cook it for you on any trips away from Gran Corrine.

**Rosalinde:** I appreciate the offer, Railanor, but it was just a figure of speech. No studies required.

### Sanatio

#### Sanatio and Alain - Watchful Duty

**Alain:** I know you are watching me, Sanatio, as you have been for at least the past few days now.

**Sanatio:** I had not expected you would notice.

**Alain:** 'Twas difficult not to, considering you have even observed me partaking in the occasional hot springs. Is there something you need from me?

**Sanatio:** It is necessary that I keep a careful eye on you when Lady Scarlett is unable to do so herself. If I were to fail, I would betray the faith Nigel placed in me when he elected to remain here in Albion.

**Alain:** Under different circumstances, it seems likely the two of you could have been fine friends indeed.

**Sanatio:** 'Tis the least I can do in return for the boundless compassion Lady Scarlett has graced me with. Assurance of your safety is but one further step on the path to atonement.

**Alain:** All the same, it is somewhat unsettling to know that assurance extends into the serenity of the hot springs as well. But perhaps you would be willing to join me instead.

**Sanatio:** I should hardly think it appropriate.

**Alain:** I do not mind. We could even invite Lex, if you wish for further company.

**Sanatio:** This is divine duty, my savior, not some jaunt undertaken for my own amusement.

**Alain:** I am certain you can still fulfill that duty, even if you have a bit of fun in the meantime.

**Sanatio:** Very well. I will not dispute your appeals any longer.

#### Ring of the Maiden

**Sanatio:** This timeworn altar of Palevian provenance is inherently linked to the Orthodoxy's doctrine. I must admit, I cannot help but feel its presence. Am I truly the one you wished to summon here?

**Alain:** Sanatio, I'd like you to have the Ring of the Maiden.

**Sanatio:** Then my being here is no happenstance. Yet I am little more than a wicked sinner, forever tarnished by my transgressions against the Church. Reluctant though I am to refuse our savior's request, the most sacred of rites warrants a finer partner than I.

**Alain:** You have clearly thought much on your misdeeds and labored tirelessly to unmake their harms, all while dutifully serving as my trusted guardian. But despite those endeavors, it appears you are unwilling to actually forgive yourself.

**Sanatio:** 'Tis as you say. What is more, should a man of my character be chosen over others more worthy, our army's morale will surely suffer.

**Alain:** Allow me a proposal, then. Join me, and help deliver this world the salvation it seeks. I can think of no greater way to atone for your sins. And should we emerge victorious, you may return to Albion not as a father scorned, but one absolved.

**Sanatio:** What have I done to deserve such kindness? You seek to redeem not only Fevrith, but me as well.

**Alain:** What kind of savior would I be otherwise?

**Sanatio:** I have finally come to understand the unshakable trust Lady Scarlett sees in you, the reason she and so many others would stand beside you through even the harshest of storms.

**Sanatio:** I wish to honor your divine request, my savior. Pray, rest the ring upon my palm.

**Alain:** Thank you for this, Sanatio.

**Sanatio:** No matter what evils the future may hold, I shall ever rise to oppose their reign. Once they do, I promise to live anew, an existence reborn, rejoicing in the heavenly warmth of those we have saved.

#### Final Battle

**Sanatio:** Alain!

**Galerius:** The ring is mine to command. Now, bow to your emperor!

**Sanatio:** I bid you rise, you who redeemed the hearts of so many, including my own. Prove to me that such benevolent deeds were no illusion.

**Alain:** Sanatio!

**Alain:** Galerius, you saw in Fevrith's innocent people mere vessels to house your own fallen empire. But as long as I live and breathe, you will never inflict such callous devastation on our world.

**Alain:** Mother!

**Sanatio:** 'Tis a miracle in truth. She yet lives, Alain.

**Alain:** We end this long-drawn war now.

**Sanatio:** With our savior guiding the assault, this fiend shall finally meet his downfall.

**Sanatio:** The only fate which lies before you is defeat.

**Alain:** Spirits of Zenoira, hear my call. Let us lift the curse of the unicorn and bring the salvation of heaven to these lost souls.

#### Ending

**Sanatio:** And thus, our savior is granted the station he rightly deserves. Considering the salvation you brought our lands, your presence would only serve to restore that trust further. I can think of no judge of character more fitting than you, my savior.

**Sanatio:** Are you certain it was wise to leave our basilica unattended, Ser Nigel?

**Nigel:** What sort of leader would decline an invitation penned by a king?

**Sanatio:** I suppose you have a point, yes.

**Nigel:** 'Tis better you have a companion at your side to shoulder them with you instead.

**Sanatio:** Ser Nigel, thank you. Rest assured, all my worries shall find your ear from this moment forth.

**Nigel:** Good. The great lengths you went to in bringing this bitter war to a close seem to have filled him with an unwavering sense of purpose, both in his search for atonement and in the future of Albion itself. May the Father's blessings ever grace your esteemed kingdom.

**Nigel:** Shall we be off, Sanatio?

**Sanatio:** Indeed. I believe I have said all I must to those I hold closest.

**Nigel:** And what of Alain? Or do you not wish to recount the praises you sung in his honor our entire journey here?

**Sanatio:** Our savior is a king now, Ser Nigel, and not open to such sizable demands upon his time.

**Nigel:** Any attempt you make to curry favor with Cornia's king can only serve to benefit our home. At least, that is how we shall excuse it to anyone who dares complain.

**Sanatio:** Is that truly necessary? I fear this subterfuge is merely a means to justify my own selfish desires.

**Nigel:** Perhaps so. Yet remain discreet, and your peers shall be none the wiser.

**Sanatio:** 'Tis not their opinion of me which troubles me, but that of the Father above.

### Scarlett

#### Scarlett - Prayer at the Cathedral

Scarlett: O Heavenly Father, ruler of land and sky above, we pray this day for deliverance from evil.

Scarlett: Grant us the meager sustenance to nourish our fragile bodies in the times to come.

Scarlett: Guide our lost souls on the path to salvation.

Scarlett: Shine down Your radiant light upon us, for darkness looms thick through all corners of Fevrith.

Scarlett: Such is my request as Your humble servant.

Scarlett: In the name of the guardian Unicorn, and that of the Holy Mother.

Scarlett: Is that you, Alain? How many times must I ask you not to stomp around in the cathedral?

Zenoiran Soldier: Well, look what we have here. Seems we are the first to show.

Zenoiran Soldier: Then you had best get to praying.

Zenoiran Soldier: What the...

Alain: Scarlett! Are you hurt?

Scarlett: What is happening to us, Alain?

Alain: A ship has come ashore on Palevia, one hoisting the banner of the Cornian Army.

Scarlett: Are they aware that you are the prince?

Alain: I cannot say for certain, but they must be Zenoiran.

Scarlett: My cathedral will see no more bloodshed this day. Come, let us move outside.

#### Scarlett Abducted

Josef: Your Highness, it is a relief to see you unharmed.

Chloe: Hold on. Where is Lex?

Josef: First, my prince, this belongs to you.

Alain: A ring?

Josef: The Ring of the Unicorn. Queen Ilenia wished for you to have it.

Josef: I had intended to wait until signs of age played more deeply across your face, but we no longer have such luxury.

Josef: I have the utmost faith you will see it secured.

Alain: A keepsake from my mother. Thank you for this, Josef. Truly.

Josef: Make no further mention of it. Now, let us be off.

Scarlett: A word, Alain?

Scarlett: No, it is nothing. It really is not important.

Scarlett: Our lives have changed so drastically from the peace we had only yesterday. It barely seems real.

Scarlett: Is that why you and Lex spent all your days banging swords down at the shore?

Alain: Which is precisely why your help matters, Scarlett.

Scarlett: Of course. I will do everything I can, as is my role as priestess of the Palevian Church.

Lex: Do not forget about me.

Chloe: Lex!

Lex: What?

Chloe: I am sorry, my prince. Decorum does not come naturally to this fool.

Chloe: There are protocols to observe, rules we must follow as vassals in service of the crown.

Scarlett: Alain? Why have you stopped?

Alain: We are surrounded.

Lex: Not the welcome party I was hoping for.

Scarlett: Get your vile claws off of me!

Chloe: Let her go!

Alain: Chloe!

Hodrick: I should have known you would be party to treachery, Renault. What is the meaning of this?

Renault: Apologies for the icy reception, but we have business with the girl.

Alain: What business could you have with Scarlett? Unhand her this instant.

Renault: As for what he plans to do with her, that is not for one of my station to know. Yet I shall see it done all the same.

Alain: Scarlett! No!

Renault: My work here is concluded. Leave the rest to you and your capable band.

Aubin: Do not worry, boss. I will earn my keep and plenty more.

Lex: straight into the hornet's nest, huh? You have got to do something, Alain.

Alain: Hear me, soldiers of Cornia. I ask that you stand aside for your returned prince.

Aubin: It is nothing personal. Just following orders from the man paying the coin.

Alain: Damn. We have no hope of overcoming such numbers.

Hodrick: Come, my prince.

Clive: I am ashamed to hear you met such misfortune before I arrived.

Josef: Your Highness, this man is Clive, the knight we spoke of earlier.

Alain: A pleasure.

Josef: still, it rankles the mind. I never would have dreamt that Galerius was after Scarlett and not you, my prince.

Alain: Who was that knight who took her?

Josef: His name is Renault, formerly a proud servant of Queen Ilenia, not unlike myself.

Josef: Just as I fell victim to Galerius and his foul magick, it would seem he has met with a similar fate.

Alain: Why Scarlett?

Clive: Perhaps her role as a priestess means something. Lately I have heard tell of Zenoira's desire to spread its roots into the orthodoxy.

Clive: Making one with direct ties a prime target.

Alain: Sitting idly by will only stoke my worry further. Let us be off at once.

Travis: Would not do that if I were you. No chance of helping the girl if you do not even know where you are going.

Alain: And you are?

Clive: Do not worry, he is a friend. A collaborator of mine by the name of Travis.

Travis: Fancy way to refer to a spy. You need intel, dirt, or just the latest weather, I am your man.

Clive: And what of Renault?

Josef: We all share your sense of urgency, but we have no hope of aiding Scarlett without first routing the enemy before us.

Alain: Right. We depart as soon as we are able.

Alain: I hope Scarlett is all right.

#### Renault Reports to Galerius

Renault: I have brought the girl, my liege.

Galerius: Then the hour is upon us.

Scarlett: Whatever you are planning...

Renault: Mind your tongue, child. You stand before the glorious emperor of all Fevrith.

Galerius: Enough.

Renault: Then allow me the honor of introducing them when that time comes.

Zenoiran Soldier: Lord Renault, urgent word. The rebels gather at our gates this very instant.

Renault: Seems our sellswords were not quite as indomitable as they claimed.

Renault: You are dismissed.

Renault: Yes, my liege. Not a single rebel shall be spared my spear.

Scarlett: Please be safe, Alain.

#### Scarlett Recovered

Alain: Scarlett!

Alain: Thank the Father. She still breathes. And she is unhurt, at that. But how?

Scarlett: Alain.

Alain: Is it wise for you to be out of bed?

Scarlett: Thank you, Alain. For everything.

Alain: It was nothing. All I ask in return is that you rest if you need it. The last few days have felt like countless moons.

Scarlett: I already told you. I am okay.

Scarlett: I heard everything back at the sanctuary. Faintly, and through a fog of pain, but still clear enough.

Scarlett: Galerius spoke true. Pontifex Arant is my father.

Scarlett: I am sorry for keeping it hidden. If anyone deserves to know, it is you.

Scarlett: I only hope you can forgive me.

Alain: There is naught to forgive.

Alain: I am certain your father delivered you from Albion praying for your wellbeing above all else, just as my own mother did with me.

Scarlett: I appreciate that.

Alain: From the day we first met, you were always...

Scarlett: Always what?

Alain: Complaining. About how untidy the lodgings were, or how ill-equipped the cathedral was.

Scarlett: My home in Albion was a grand estate with dozens of servants, and our cathedral the greatest architectural marvel.

Scarlett: Besides, I was but a child, secreted away to Palevia.

Alain: I am only teasing. It is good to see you have recovered enough to put up a fair fight.

Scarlett: I would hardly call it fair.

Alain: In all seriousness, I do not wish to put you in harm's way any more than I already have.

Scarlett: I doubt he and his cohorts will spare another thought on me.

Scarlett: What I mean to say is, you need not worry for my safety. I am staying with you, and I will more than earn my keep.

Lex: And here I thought you were a second away from ordering a meal at Death's tavern.

Lex: With that kind of fire, you will be the one doing the cooking.

Scarlett: I would rather you did not tease me, thank you.

#### Scarlett and Alain - Palevia Woods

Scarlett: Do you remember this place, Alain?

Alain: Lex and I used to waste hours in these woods, fashioning fallen branches into makeshift swords.

Scarlett: And eating nuts from the trees until your stomachs hurt. Do not forget.

Alain: Yes, it is a rather embarrassing memory.

Lex: Oh, hey. What are you two doing out here?

Scarlett: I could ask you the same, Lex.

Lex: I figured I would see how the island has been doing since we left.

Lex: You used to get so mad at us for playing back there, Scarlett.

Alain: That was actually more of a you problem, Lex, and only because you kept trying to climb on the statue.

Lex: Guess my stomach has been killing me for some reason.

Scarlett: Please tell me you have not been eating any nuts, at least.

Alain: Of course not.

Alain: How have you been feeling, Scarlett? Do not be afraid to ask if there is anything you need from me.

Scarlett: I am fine, thank you. But I have to say, you have turned into a real worrier ever since I was abducted.

Alain: That should be expected, given the circumstances.

Scarlett: You must have been in some state while I was gone.

Alain: Of course I was. I could barely even eat, out of fear that I might have lost you forever.

Scarlett: Really?

Alain: It was only once you had been taken that I realized just how much you meant to me.

Alain: Just how much I rely on you, every single day of my life.

Alain: I would have felt no joy at the accomplishment without my dearest friend standing beside me.

Scarlett: Is that what I am to you?

Scarlett: I feel the same way, Alain.

Scarlett: I do not want to lose any of my friends to this war. Not you, Lex, Chloe, or Ser Josef.

Scarlett: Things will work out. They have to.

Alain: Indeed they will.

Alain: And by the way, Scarlett. Please do not leave me, ever again.

Scarlett: I would not dream of it.

#### Scarlett and Alain - Not Possession

Alain: Is everything okay, Scarlett? You seem rather irritated.

Scarlett: I was just thinking of all the attractive women you have been taking into the Liberation lately.

Alain: And men, do not forget. We need as many fighters as are willing to join, regardless of gender.

Scarlett: Fighters who you clearly feel deserve your attention far more than I do.

Scarlett: With how long we have known each other, it almost does not seem fair that you keep leaving me out.

Alain: If you ever wish to talk, you are free to insert yourself into any conversation I am having. Everyone would be pleased to see you, I am sure.

Scarlett: That is not what I... Why are you standing so close to me?

Alain: Do you remember the little forest on Palevia, much like this one? We often used to gaze upon its many inhabitants, always careful to keep our distance.

Alain: Josef warned us not to wander the area without an adult, yet we did it anyway.

Scarlett: Listen to me, Alain.

Alain: Your face has gone completely red, Scarlett. Are you feeling all right?

Scarlett: I am fine. What I am trying to say is, I do not want someone else stealing you away from me.

Scarlett: Oops.

Alain: So that is how you feel.

Scarlett: I was only hoping we could talk more.

Alain: I am not some mere possession to be snatched away the moment you avert your eyes.

Scarlett: I know that.

Alain: I suppose this means you truly are jealous.

Scarlett: I am not.

Alain: I will be sure to speak with you more often from now on.

Scarlett: You do not have to do that for me.

Alain: It is not only for you, Scarlett. I have realized today how deeply I miss our conversations as well.

Scarlett: You really mean that?

Scarlett: Hmph. I do not know what took you so long.

Alain: Nor do I.

#### Albion and the Pontificate

Alain: Yet Galerius claimed the man was dead.

Hodrick: The pontificate is a hereditary station, meaning the next in line takes the mitre when their forebear passes.

Hodrick: Thus, we can almost assuredly assume an heir has ascended to the role.

Alain: I do not believe that is likely.

Lex: Not to butt in, but is Scarlett not supposed to be the new pontifex?

Alain: Why would you think so?

Lex: The two of you have been acting real weird ever since we got to Albion. I was going to ask why when I overheard you talking about it. Sorry. I was not trying to pry.

Scarlett: Pontifex Arant only has one heir.

Lex: How long have you known, Alain?

Alain: Since the sanctuary in Cornia. In the eyes of the orthodoxy, Scarlett would rightfully take over in the case of Arant's passing.

Alain: It is possible, yes. But our only hope of learning the truth lies in infiltrating the pontifical chambers.

Scarlett: Then let me do it. I am his daughter.

Alain: It is true that we would be spared a sacrilegious war if you were able to convince him to stand down.

Alain: Yet we must first determine whether he even lives. I know how you feel, Scarlett, but such responsibility cannot rest on your shoulders.

Alain: If Arant truly has passed on, yours would surely be the next life they hope to claim.

Josef: Even a proper scouting mission failed to uncover the truth.

Alain: Indeed. The Basilica's security is far too tight to breach, and he has made no public appearances of late, citing grave illness as the reason.

Hodrick: Whether or not he truly lives, there will be no avoiding conflict with the arm of the orthodoxy loyal to Zenoira.

Josef: If we manage to bring the orthodoxy toward our cause, many of its branches will surely follow.

Lex: So, Scarlett?

Scarlett: I have made my peace with what we have to do. That goes for you too, Alain.

Alain: That is easy enough to say, but this fight will surely see you cross swords with people you know, maybe even people you love. The battle will be painful indeed.

Scarlett: For the people of Albion, I will do whatever it takes.

Alain: Very well. Our destination is set. We march for Albion's capital and Bisfaine Basilica.

Josef: In that case, we must first secure a bridgehead across the River Warnby region.

Alain: Prepare to depart at once.

Josef: Of course, Your Highness.

Alain: One moment, Scarlett. Are you sure you want to go through with this?

Scarlett: To be honest, I am a bit scared.

Alain: I can only imagine.

Scarlett: But praying over the matter will solve nothing. I have to act if I want to see it done, and I plan to do just that.

#### Nigel and Bisfaine Basilica

Nigel: So, you are the one commanding these rebels.

Nigel: Come forth and claim my head. It will not be an easy task, I assure you.

Nigel: What did you call her?

Nigel: Then it is truly you. But what are you doing consorting with insurgents?

Nigel: I relayed the message myself regarding your sacred mission. You were to serve as guide and guardian for the savior who would one day greet Palevia's shores.

Nigel: Wait. You mean to say the man before me...

Nigel: Then you would see our savior turn his blade on the very orthodoxy you claim to represent?

Nigel: Indeed, as ordained by the divine word of His Holiness Pontifex Arant.

Nigel: Blasphemy. I will not suffer this impious slander.

Nigel: They are what?

Scarlett: I do not know what awaits us at Bisfaine Basilica, but I am ready to find out. Let us go, Alain.

Scarlett: The Basilica is not much further now, Alain.

Alain: We should stop for a moment and make certain we are prepared before we head onward.

Alain: Our scouts have confirmed my trepidation. Reclaiming the Basilica will be a challenge unlike any we have faced yet.

Josef: Truly a natural fortress in every sense of the phrase.

Chloe: Your Majesty!

Alain: What is it, Chloe?

Alain: I had a feeling it would be you, Nigel.

Nigel: The state of our orthodoxy was just as I said. Zenoira has fashioned us into mere pawns in their fiendish chess game.

Alain: And Pontifex Arant?

Nigel: His Holiness has long since passed, yet he stands animated in death by the most abhorrent of necromancers.

Scarlett: No.

Alain: I am so sorry, Scarlett.

Josef: Then Baltro has sunk his talons into the sacred flesh of the church itself.

Alain: What do you intend to do now?

Nigel: Make Zenoira suffer for their foul defilement of our most holy patriarch.

Alain: Could you not have made public the truth first? The clergy would surely take notice of such godlessness.

Alain: Yet here you stand, a solitary knight.

Nigel: It would seem Father Sanatio and the hierarchy beneath him all sing Zenoira's hymnal.

Clive: Ser Nigel, does your presence here mean you seek to join our cause?

Nigel: Do not mistake my aims. His Holiness has ventured forth into the great beyond, and Lady Scarlett is the rightful successor to his radiant office.

Nigel: My only wish is to see her granted that role in earnest, and the orthodoxy restored to its proper standing.

Alain: Then we are in alignment. We would welcome your presence among our ranks, even if only until we reach the Basilica.

Nigel: In the name of Lady Scarlett and the lost sanctity of our holy Orthodoxy.

Scarlett: This is it, then. Albion's future rests with us.

#### Sanatio's Confession

Sanatio: I have failed, and so too has my divine calling.

Sanatio: The truth of His Holiness's demise will come to light, and all of his teachings shall be lost like so many feathers on a foul wind.

Nigel: You dare speak his name after the desecration you have engaged in?

Sanatio: Absent a pontifex at its helm, the orthodoxy would fail to adequately direct the faith of its believers.

Sanatio: Trust in our creed would wither and fade. So I resorted to desperate measures, at least until we could find Lady Scarlett.

Nigel: Why did you hide it from me?

Sanatio: It is as I have mentioned before. His Holiness forbade us from even speaking her name.

Sanatio: Lady Scarlett? But how have you come to arrive here? And among the ranks of rebels, no less.

Nigel: You would know all that and more had you only spoken to me, Sanatio.

Nigel: It was I who ushered her out of this land at His Holiness's behest.

Sanatio: Then perhaps my greatest sin was confiding in that Zenoiran sorcerer over my own countryman.

Sanatio: Even so, I am glad to have reached this conclusion.

Sanatio: I would like to believe it amounts to divine providence, ushered forth by the Heavenly Father Himself.

Sanatio: And that the congregation His Holiness loved so dearly can live on in peace.

Sanatio: I leave that charge in your capable hands, Ser Nigel.

Sanatio: Once I face my inquisition, our most sacred of nations can finally step forward anew.

Sanatio: And you, Lady Scarlett, please guide our flock to salvation as their new and worthy pontifex.

Scarlett: That I cannot do.

Scarlett: I had not realized what my father left me with. They needed his blood to break the seals on Fevrith's sanctuaries.

Scarlett: The ones who stole His Holiness away from us. What cruel irony.

Scarlett: Tell me, why have I not faced sentence for my sins?

Alain: Rather than languish in their wake, what would you say to joining our ranks?

Nigel: And that the pontificate will remain vacant until your prophesied charge is complete.

Scarlett: Thank you, Nigel. You will make a fine leader, I am sure of it.

Nigel: I pray you are right, my lady. Sanatio shall serve as your guardian in my stead.

Nigel: I shall invoke the Father's blessings every morn and eve until your eventual return.

Alain: You are welcome to stay, you know. Albion would be in quite the predicament if their new pontifex were to fall in battle.

Scarlett: Their pontifex will not be going anywhere.

Scarlett: As long as I am with you, I am nothing more than an ordinary priestess. And your friend, of course.

Alain: Are you sure about this? Can I promise I am the savior you seek?

Scarlett: I can, without a shadow of a doubt.

Scarlett: Father always knew it would be someone important to me. There is no one who fits that description more than you, Alain.

Scarlett: I will restore the sanctuaries to their function, broken seal or no.

Sanatio: The ring plays an integral role in all this. After all, the ring will not be fully restored until Alain performs the rite of covenant.

Scarlett: Then let us head for the altar, Alain.

Alain: Considering what lies ahead, it would be prudent to determine the location of the sanctuaries now rather than later.

Sanatio: I have taken the liberty of marking all of them on your map.

Alain: I am in your debt, Sanatio.

Sanatio: My staff is yours to command forevermore, O Savior of Fevrith.

#### Scarlett and Alain - Ring of the Maiden

Scarlett: What is it, Alain?

Alain: I would like you to have the Ring of the Maiden.

Scarlett: Is there not someone else you would rather give it to? Or am I just the most convenient choice?

Alain: Not at all. The rite of covenant can only be performed if the two parties are of one mind and one heart.

Scarlett: Is that true?

Alain: It is you, Scarlett. It has always been you.

Alain: These feelings are not mere friendship. They are deep and utterly profound. I believe we both finally understand that now.

Scarlett: I always thought it was my mission that kept me standing beside you.

Scarlett: But I treasure you more than I could have ever dreamed.

Alain: Then stay with me, Scarlett, until the day we both drift off into eternal slumber.

Scarlett: So it is true. There is really no lying to the rings.

Scarlett: I love you, Alain. And I always will.

#### Scarlett and Alain - Final Battle

Galerius: Hmph!

Galerius: Gah.

Alain: Mother!

Galerius: Hahahaha. How does it feel, hm? Your dear mother, slain by your own hand.

Alain: What is happening to me?

Scarlett: Alain!

Galerius: What a poor fool he was. Doomed to the same fate as the pitiful queen before him.

Galerius: His strength surpasses even Ilenia's. The might of the unicorn runs deep in his veins.

Galerius: strike at this new body of mine, if you dare. You would simply be volunteering your own as my next vessel.

Galerius: The ring is mine to command, and a futile demise is all that awaits you now.

Galerius: None can ever hope to halt my designs. Bow to your emperor.

Galerius: Worry not. You will make a fine Zenoiran vessel once it is over.

Galerius: Enough. Cannot you see it is over?

Galerius: The ring... But why does it hold such vast energy?

Galerius: It will take more than this to defeat me.

Scarlett: Alain!

Alain: Emancipate his soul.

Alain: Galerius. You saw in Fevrith's innocent people mere vessels to house your fallen empire.

Alain: But as long as I live and breathe, you will never inflict such callous devastation on our world.

Galerius: How do you know of that?

Galerius: You will not!

Galerius: Their emperor shall never know defeat.

Baltro: Your Majesty.

Galerius: How goes the rite?

Galerius: Then these insects shall be more than enough. Grant me your strength, and we will stamp them out together.

Baltro: If it was not clear, Your Majesty, the sigil seeks none other.

Galerius: Traitorous fool. Finally gone senile, hm?

Galerius: Raagh!

Alain: Mother!

Ilenia: Ngh.

Scarlett: Thank the Father, she is okay.

Alain: Speak to me, please.

Josef: I never imagined he possessed such frightful mastery over the bodies of others.

Ilenia: Alain. I cannot say how much time has passed since that day, but you have grown so much.

Ilenia: If only I could have been there to witness it.

Ilenia: It seems I owe Josef a great deal for raising you in my absence.

Alain: Josef, see my mother somewhere safe.

Josef: And you, Your Highness?

Scarlett: We have to stop him. If anyone can do it, it is you, the Savior of Fevrith.

Scarlett: The sorrows of this tragic war must never again afflict our land. It is what my father would have wanted.

Alain: Spirits of Zenoira, hear my call.

Alain: Your emperor is no more, and in his place stands a tyrannical fiend who craves nothing but absolute control.

Alain: Tell me, is this what you truly desire? To sacrifice your very essence in service of this daemon?

Alain: Souls of the departed, if you have any humanity left within you, lend me your aid.

Alain: These souls are not a power one can wield, Baltro. They are human lives, human will in its purest form.

Alain: Let us lift the curse of the unicorn and bring the salvation of heaven to these lost souls.

#### Scarlett and Alain - Ending

Scarlett: Promise me you will make time for just the two of us later, okay?

Scarlett: I love you, Alain. And I always will.

Scarlett: Not that I am not confident. You will make a great ruler, I know that for a fact.

Raenys: King Alain. Witnessing your coronation with Lady Scarlett at my side moved me to tears, if I am completely honest.

Raenys: But for this moment alone, I am content to bask in the radiant warmth of your divine light.

Scarlett: Why do you not go take a look around? I am sure the others would love to see you.

Scarlett: Not that I am not confident. You will make a great ruler, I know that for a fact.

### Selvie

#### Selvie Recruited

Selvie: No money for a hired sword...

Alain: Excuse us, ma'am. Is something the matter?

Selvie: Whatever am I to do?

Alain: She seems not to have heard me.

Selvie: How can I fight the soldiers of the damned?

Lex: Lemme talk to her. Hellooo!

Selvie: Wah! When did you... how did you... who are you people?

Lex: You know, the ones defying Zenoira's rule.

Selvie: Ah, the ones who defy Zenoira's rule.

Alain: Our apologies.

Selvie: Nonsense. I share the blame for not minding my surroundings.

Alain: May we ask what you're doing here?

Selvie: Researching this magick sigil, as it happens.

Selvie: But I've encountered a roadblock, one I have no possible means of resolving alone.

Lex: What kinda roadblock are we talking?

Selvie: When I awakened the sigil, it breathed life into spectral beings. Warriors lost to time, who attacked me with reckless abandon.

Selvie: I closed my eyes and waited for the end, but it never came. There wasn't so much as a scratch on my beautiful skin.

Selvie: After repeated attempts met the same conclusion, I reached a hypothesis.

Selvie: The grounds we stand upon were used in days of yore to cultivate strength against the antagonistic apparitions.

Lex: If they can't lay a finger on you, it should be easy enough to keep doing the thing, right?

Selvie: That depends on the "thing." I want to know what happens when all of the sigil's guardians are defeated.

Selvie: But I'm just one woman, and hardly capable of such a feat alone.

Alain: Hence the worry.

Selvie: Yes. I've made it my goal of late to study the effects of combating the illusions.

Selvie: And should you be willing to help with my research, I'd be more than glad to join this Liberation of yours.

Alain: I understand. We'll do whatever we can to assist.

Lex: I was hoping you'd say that. Lady's got me all curious now.

Selvie: You mean it? Oh, that's wonderful.

#### Selvie and Alain - Voice from Heaven

Selvie: I've come to understand you heard a voice from the heavens, Alain.

Alain: At the sanctuary back in Cornia, yes.

Selvie: Interesting. But why were you able to receive its tidings, I wonder?

Selvie: An anatomical peculiarity of your royal bloodline, perhaps?

Selvie: Ah, if only I had the educational background to say for certain.

Selvie: still, whatever the answer may be, I find myself utterly captivated.

Alain: You're staring at me rather intently, Selvie.

Selvie: Ah! My apologies.

Alain: Have you any particular reason for that?

Selvie: "If you wish to create the ideal future, you must first understand the failings of history."

Selvie: That's what my father always used to say to me.

Selvie: And though my ambitions aren't quite as lofty as his were, I find there to be few things in this world more compelling than the mysteries of our past.

Alain: My mother often spoke in a similar way, of the inherent value in studying the chronicles of centuries gone.

#### Selvie and Alain - Buried in Ruins

Alain: Selvie?

Selvie: Alain?

Alain: Worry not. I will have you out of there in but a moment.

Selvie: Thank you, my prince.

Alain: It is a relief to see you unharmed. How did you come to be trapped beneath all that rubble?

Selvie: One moment I was in the midst of a peaceful investigation, and the next I found myself beset by spirits of the dead.

Alain: The same phantom soldiers we have encountered elsewhere, I presume.

Selvie: That is precisely what I thought at first, but I soon realized they were the ghosts of deceased children and housepets.

Alain: How somber.

Selvie: There is no sigil in the region, either, so it could not have been magick which manifested them.

Selvie: I believe the ghosts were trying to play a prank on me and accidentally brought the ruins crashing down in the process.

Selvie: They must have been awfully startled by the noise. They quickly fled the area, likely off to some spectral plane beyond our comprehension.

Alain: I am not so certain. Before I found you, I heard a young voice calling out to me from this direction.

Alain: Perhaps it was one of the children urging me to come to your aid.

Selvie: Then I plan to further my research into these lands, in hopes of learning more about the people they once were.

Selvie: I will forever be grateful for what you have done here today.

Alain: Speaking of research, perhaps you should not be doing it alone any longer. You may not be so lucky next time.

Selvie: A valid point. Thank you again for digging me out of that rubble.

Alain: It was nothing at all. I am merely pleased to know you are safe.

#### Selvie and Alain - Research and the Liberation

Selvie: I'm glad to hear it. And yet my research always tends to feel far more rushed than I would prefer.

Alain: I suppose that means we've no choice but to part ways.

Selvie: That's not what I'm saying at all.

Selvie: My life would be a great deal more difficult alone, not only with the sigils themselves, but even simply traveling between them.

Selvie: Given my contributions in battle, I feel our agreement is mutually beneficial.

Selvie: Field research requires a certain level of physical prowess, one I've honed over years of solitary wandering.

Selvie: No, actually. I made a point to hire mercenaries at every new site.

Selvie: But for some reason, they always ended up running away.

Selvie: I could bury myself in research day after day without a care for money, for guards, or even for time itself.

Selvie: As it so happens, that was meant to be a joke of my own.

Selvie: But the offer is an alluring one.

#### Selvie and Alain - Ring of the Maiden

Selvie: Yes, yes. Hilarious joke. Well done.

Alain: I'd like you to have the Ring of the Maiden.

Selvie: Glad you had your bit of fun for the day. I'll just be going now.

Alain: Did you hear me, Selvie? This is no joke.

Alain: There's no one I would rather spend the rest of my life with than you.

Alain: The ring is yours, assuming you want it.

Selvie: Nobody else treats me the way you do, Alain.

Selvie: I feel exactly the same. I couldn't imagine life without you.

Selvie: Now, how do we do this?

Alain: You can start by giving me your hand.

Selvie: So this is the Ring of the Maiden...

Selvie: Fascinating. I can feel a strange power flowing through every inch of my body.

Selvie: I must say, this ring is quite the curio. Yes, I think it'll do nicely for my experiments.

Alain: Just try not to break it, please.

Selvie: How could you even suggest such a thing? I'll treasure it for as long as I live.

#### Selvie and Alain - Final Battle

Galerius: End this, now.

Galerius: Hmph.

Galerius: Gah.

Alain: Mother!

Galerius: How does it feel, hm? Your dear mother, slain by your own hand?

Alain: What is happening to me?

Selvie: Alain!

Galerius: You will make a fine Zenoiran vessel once it is over.

Galerius: The ring...

Galerius: But why does it hold such vast energy?

Selvie: It has to be positive. I'm positive.

Selvie: Do you hear me, Alain? Wrest yourself free of the shackles that bind you.

Galerius: It will take more than this to defeat me.

Alain: Galerius. You saw in Fevrith's innocent people mere vessels to house your own fallen empire.

Alain: But as long as I live and breathe, you'll never inflict such callous devastation on our world.

Galerius: How do you know of that?

Galerius: Their emperor shall never know defeat.

Baltro: Your Majesty.

Galerius: How goes the rite?

Galerius: Then these insects shall be more than enough. Grant me your strength, and we'll stamp them out together.

Galerius: What do you think you're doing?

Baltro: If it wasn't clear, Your Majesty, the sigil seeks none other.

Galerius: Raagh!

Alain: Mother!

Ilenia: Ngh.

Selvie: I could never have foreseen this, but it's all right, Alain. She's alive.

Alain: Speak to me, please.

Ilenia: Alain. I can't say how much time has passed since that day, but you've grown so much.

Ilenia: If only I could have been there to witness it.

Ilenia: It seems I owe Josef a great deal for raising you in my absence.

Josef: And you, Your Highness?

Alain: We end this long-drawn war now.

### Sharon

#### Sharon Joins the Liberation Army

**Sharon:** Lady Ochlys?

**Ochlys:** My dear Sharon!

**Sharon:** I hear you sought their patronage in the hopes of ensuring my safety.

**Sharon:** You needn't worry, Lady Ochlys. The shards you confided here remain untouched.

**Ochlys:** The shards be damned. I placed your well-being in danger's path, and for that I am deeply sorry.

**Sharon:** Please, you needn't apologize. On the contrary, this matter has swept the doubts from my mind as the morning fog. If I truly wish to glory in the Creator's lands, I must see it manifest through my own acts.

**Ochlys:** If such is the journey you wish, I will raise no objection.

**Sharon:** Might you grant me leave to join the Liberation?

**Alain:** Skilled healers such as yourself are ever in high demand. We would gladly count you among our numbers.

**Sharon:** Oh, what joy. Such a benevolent show of trust will not go unmet. You have it on my word as a servant to the Almighty.

#### Sharon and Alain - Healer

**Liberation Soldier:** Thank you, ma'am.

**Liberation Mercenary:** I scraped my knee real bad, Sharon.

**Liberation Mercenary:** Oh, uh... my stomach hurts. Yeah, that is it.

**Liberation Mercenary:** You are just faking sick so you can see Sharon.

**Liberation Mercenary:** Like you can talk. Who has ever heard of going to a healer for a little scrape?

**Liberation Mercenary:** Not so loud, dammit. Just think what she would say if she heard us talking like this.

**Alain:** Especially on a day you are meant to be resting.

**Sharon:** I only wish to help where I can.

**Alain:** Your debt to whom?

**Sharon:** They received plenty of donations after Zenoira invaded, but there was still much suffering.

**Alain:** As I have noticed, yes. I only ask that you not overextend yourself beyond your means.

**Girl:** Bye, Miss Sharon!

#### Sharon and Alain - A Home Left Behind

**Alain:** At times, I have noticed a profound sadness behind their eyes.

**Sharon:** I have someone now who is able to soothe that pain, at least a bit.

**Alain:** You speak of Ochlys.

**Sharon:** I suppose. She always used to remind me I am not alone, that through all my toughest moments, she would be there to ease my worries. While it is true I never knew my birth parents, I only became the woman I am today through the love I have felt throughout my life, as well as that of Lady Ochlys, of course.

**Alain:** Yet now you have left that home behind in favor of our army. Tell me, Sharon, how have you found the Liberation in the time since?

**Sharon:** I see it in the way those children smile every time they approach us.

**Alain:** The pain of losing those you hold most dear...

#### Sharon and Alain - The Bird

**Alain:** Hm? What is she doing up in that tree?

**Sharon:** Ah!

**Alain:** Are you hurt, Sharon? You seem to have landed quite heavily on your leg.

**Sharon:** Please, it is nothing a bit of healing cannot tend to. Do you see the nest on that branch up there? I was returning a fallen chick, but I am embarrassed to say I lost my footing on the way back down.

**Alain:** You truly are a kind soul, Sharon.

**Sharon:** Would you not have done the same as me?

**Alain:** Well, yes. I suppose I would have.

**Sharon:** As I thought. In any case, we should move away from the nest before their mother grows too upset with us.

#### Sharon and Alain - Kindness

**Sharon:** You called me a kind soul once before, back at Rondmort. Forgive me for hiding my true nature from you, Prince.

**Alain:** Whatever the motive, you have dedicated yourself to the well-being of others and aided a great many people in the process. Far better that than to demand favors and offer nothing in return.

**Sharon:** You say that, but it is still a sin to act purely in self-interest.

**Alain:** Was it self-interest that drove you to return that bird to its nest, or purely compassion for an animal in need?

**Sharon:** Well...

**Alain:** In either case, I would rather you not help at all if you are going to get hurt while doing so.

**Sharon:** Thank you, Prince. I promise I will be more careful next time.

**Alain:** And should you ever require a steady hand to lift you up, I would be more than glad to volunteer.

**Sharon:** I would like that very much.

**Alain:** Look, Sharon. The mother bird has come bearing food for her children.

#### Ring of the Maiden

**Sharon:** I was told you have need of me.

**Alain:** Sharon, I'd like you to have the Ring of the Maiden.

**Sharon:** You would bestow so holy a relic on me, ser?

**Alain:** I would. Time and again, I have found myself restored by your sublime healing magicks. And in truth, simply having you at my side brings me more warmth and comfort than even the most soothing of flames.

**Alain:** I only hope you will grant me a chance to return that favor. Amidst your kindness, Sharon, I often forget that malice exists at all. Yet forgotten or not, it is always present, drowning people in a sea of pain and hurt. Were you not there to mend it, the world would be colder for it.

**Alain:** But who shall heal you when you falter?

**Sharon:** Heheh. I am not worried about that. Honestly, it feels like nothing could ever hurt me while you are here. Because I know you will do anything in the world if it means keeping me safe.

**Alain:** Those words are like a potent magick for my heart.

**Sharon:** Alain, I fear you will be hurt protecting me. But if you are, I will be right there to heal your wounds, and to kiss them better as well.

**Alain:** Perhaps I could pick up a few scrapes, then. And I will never allow harm to come to you, neither now nor ever.

#### Final Battle

**Sharon:** Alain!

**Galerius:** The ring is mine to command. Now, bow to your emperor!

**Sharon:** So please, return to us. Return to me.

**Alain:** Sharon!

**Alain:** Galerius, you saw in Fevrith's innocent people mere vessels to house your own fallen empire. But as long as I live and breathe, you will never inflict such callous devastation on our world.

**Alain:** Mother!

**Alain:** We end this long-drawn war now.

**Alain:** Spirits of Zenoira, hear my call. Let us lift the curse of the unicorn and bring the salvation of heaven to these lost souls.

#### Ending

**Sharon:** An orphan girl, chosen as queen of the grandest palace the continent has ever known. I will always be with you, Alain, to celebrate your victories, to kiss away the pain of your defeats, and to share the burden of a crown one man could never bear alone.

**Sharon:** I saw a number of people injure themselves today. That is a kind of joy only a new king can deliver, I suppose.

**Ochlys:** If anyone is capable of leading this nation, it is you. Come now, Sharon. I understand you bear a duty as the appointed healer, but you have barely had a chance to enjoy the festivities.

**Sharon:** That is all right with me. Just seeing everyone happy is more than enough.

**Ochlys:** And what of my happiness? All I wanted was to spend the day together.

**Sharon:** Ah. I suppose I could find someone else to fill in for a while, if you put it like that.

**Ochlys:** I would much appreciate that, yes. Shall we head for the shops?

#### Sharon and Alain - Healing and Rest

Mercenary: Sister Sharon, I may need healing.

Sharon: Another scrape?

Mercenary: Perhaps. I would hate to risk it.

Alain: Sharon, you should rest when you can.

Sharon: I know, but there is still so much to do. The orphanage at Rondmort depends on donations, and Zenoira left many people in need.

Alain: Then help them, but not beyond your means.

Sharon: If anyone should be asking that, it is me of you.

Alain: Then we will both try to be reasonable.

Sharon: That sounds fair.

#### Sharon and Alain - Children and Hope

Alain: The children were smiling, but I saw sadness in their eyes.

Sharon: They have suffered much. Lady Ochlys eases their pain in a way I cannot.

Alain: She has helped you, too.

Sharon: She reminded me that I am not alone. I never knew my birth parents, but I became who I am through the love of others, and through Lady Ochlys.

Alain: How does the Liberation feel to you now?

Sharon: I see it in the way the children smile when they see us. Wherever I am needed, I will be at your call.

#### Sharon and Alain - The Bird Nest

Alain: Sharon? What are you doing up in that tree?

Sharon: Returning a nest. The poor bird fell with it.

Alain: Careful.

Sharon: Ah!

Alain: I have you.

Sharon: I am sorry. I try to help, but sometimes my reasons are selfish. I do not want anyone to think too well of me.

Alain: Whatever your motive, you have helped many people. Did compassion or self-interest return that bird to its nest?

Sharon: I suppose compassion did.

Alain: Then accept that part of yourself. And next time, let me offer a steadier hand before you climb.

Sharon: I will.

Alain: Look. The mother bird has returned.

Sharon: With food. Thank goodness.

### Tatiana

#### Tatiana Recruited

Tatiana: Though, should it mean allowing such ignominious research to continue unabated, what say you, my prince?

Alain: You have my trust, Tatiana.

Lex: What about the rumors? Buying into this thing's not gonna reflect on us too good.

Alain: We meet them head-on. As long as the sick are treated with dignity and honor, that tide will turn.

Alain: In the end, these studies are meant to benefit all who call Fevrith home.

Alain: If he was even half the man you claim, that was Lord Ghislain's intention from the very beginning.

Tatiana: Am I to face no sentence?

Alain: Our enemy here is Zenoira, not you.

Tatiana: You only mean to shackle me in their stead.

Alain: The Liberation exists to grant freedom, not oppress the downtrodden further.

Tatiana: In that case, I'd like to exercise my freedom to join you on that journey.

Lex: What about your cure?

Tatiana: To be candid with you, it's almost finished. Enough so that I needn't stay here myself.

Tatiana: As for me, I'll take this opportunity to walk beside the man who robbed this world of Lord Ghislain's grace.

Tatiana: To see what ideals he chooses to fight for, and ultimately to die for.

Tatiana: And, when that moment inevitably arrives, to be the one to sound the death knell myself.

Lex: C'mon, Alain. Only an idiot would let you-

Alain: Very well, then.

Lex: Should've known that was coming.

Alain: Be warned. You may be awaiting my death a great many years.

Alain: That, and you'll be expected to earn your keep in the meantime. Welcome to the Liberation, Tatiana.

#### Tatiana and Alain - Moonlit Shells

Alain: Especially considering my own desire to study your work.

Tatiana: An amusing thought, but without years of dedicated study, you won't even understand what you're looking at.

Alain: Grant me that opportunity, Tatiana, please. I swear I'll not get in your way.

Tatiana: What a strange man you are.

Tatiana: First you decided not to punish my wrongs, and now you refuse to keep your distance, despite the fact that I clearly despise you.

Tatiana: I wonder, how will Cornia flourish with you at its helm? And more importantly, how will it fall?

Alain: Both now and after Fevrith is in its rightful hands once more.

Zenoiran Soldier: Well, well, well. Looks like we found ourselves a rebel.

Zenoiran Soldier: Lucky. Just the break we've been waiting for.

Tatiana: You intend to kill me, then?

Tatiana: It seems I'll be reunited with Lord Ghislain sooner than expected.

Zenoiran Soldier: Just stand still, and I'll make this quick.

Zenoiran Soldier: Hope you know it's nothing personal.

Alain: Tatiana!

Alain: What were you thinking, leaving camp alone at this time of night?

Tatiana: I want nothing to do with the man who murdered Lord Ghislain, or a fool who decides who lives and who dies on pure impulse.

Alain: I can't deny that.

Alain: Yet those he sacrificed were not nameless victims. They had families. Lives. People who cared for them.

Alain: Just as you did for him.

Tatiana: Hmph.

Alain: He no doubt believed his deeds to be a necessary evil.

Alain: But I refused to stand and watch while your lord made unwilling martyrs of his own citizens.

Tatiana: You know nothing of the horrors that plague brought upon us.

Alain: If you wish to call that mere impulse, then so be it.

Alain: Yet once I become king, I'll no doubt be forced to make even crueler decisions regarding the fate of my people.

Alain: And I'm certain Ghislain bore much the same resolve.

Tatiana: You imply that you and he are alike?

Tatiana: To me, there was no thought more terrifying than that.

Tatiana: The fear that I unwittingly brought about his death, rather than fulfilled the dream he so desperately yearned for.

Tatiana: The fear that I could have prevented my savior's demise.

Alain: Then hate me all you want, on Lord Ghislain's behalf.

Alain: I would rather that than request that everyone in this army adore my every action.

Tatiana: As if you even need to ask. I wouldn't forget what you did so easily.

Alain: What is this?

Tatiana: The shell of a lunas clam. It has powerful medicinal effects, but only when first bathed beneath the light of the moon.

Alain: Ah, so that's why you were out here.

Tatiana: Nobody deserves to be sacrificed, even for the noblest of causes.

Tatiana: We all want to keep living, and yet...

Alain: Forgive me, Tatiana, for not giving Ghislain that chance.

Tatiana: You should go. I still have a few more shells to find myself, and doubt there'll be any further patrols tonight.

Alain: As you wish. Be careful, Tatiana.

Tatiana: But I swear on my life, I'll rid our world of that foul disease, just as you had always dreamed.

Tatiana: Farewell, my lord.

#### Tatiana and Alain - Ring of the Maiden

Tatiana: A fine place you have here. What's the meaning of this?

Alain: I'd like you to have the Ring of the Maiden.

Tatiana: Hm. I knew you were a strange one from the moment we met.

Tatiana: I've been an outcast my entire life. Reviled, shunned by the world.

Tatiana: But you and Lord Ghislain greeted me with acceptance, not hate.

Alain: I merely did what I felt was right.

Tatiana: Then tell me. What happens once you give me the ring?

Alain: First, we bring Zenoira's reign to an end. You and I, together.

Alain: After that, I could entice you back to Cornia. Perhaps as the royal physician, or more, if you were so willing.

Tatiana: Looking to keep me as close as possible, I see. Are you sure you're ready for all that entails?

Alain: I've never been readier for anything. This ring is proof of that.

Tatiana: Heheheh.

Tatiana: I can think of no greater way to await your death than to stand with you.

Tatiana: Just know that I'm not giving it back, even if you change your mind years in the future.

Alain: Nor could I ever want you to.

Tatiana: Ah, and Alain?

Tatiana: Thank you.

#### Tatiana and Alain - Final Battle

Galerius: End this, now.

Galerius: Hmph.

Galerius: Gah.

Alain: Mother!

Galerius: How does it feel, hm? Your dear mother, slain by your own hand?

Alain: What is happening to me?

Tatiana: Alain.

Galerius: What a poor fool he was, doomed to the same fate as the pitiful queen before him.

Galerius: His strength surpasses even Ilenia's. The might of the unicorn runs deep in his veins.

Galerius: strike at this new body of mine, if you dare.

Galerius: You'd simply be volunteering your own as my next vessel.

Galerius: The ring is mine to command, and a futile demise is all that awaits you now.

Galerius: None can ever hope to halt my designs. Bow to your emperor.

Galerius: This day is won.

Galerius: You will make a fine Zenoiran vessel once it is over.

Galerius: Enough. Can't you see it's over?

Galerius: The ring...

Galerius: But why does it hold such vast energy?

Tatiana: This can't be how your story ends, Alain.

Tatiana: No. I refuse to watch you die in so feeble a manner.

Galerius: It will take more than this to defeat me.

Tatiana: Alain!

Alain: Galerius. You saw in Fevrith's innocent people mere vessels to house your own fallen empire.

Alain: But as long as I live and breathe, you'll never inflict such callous devastation on our world.

Galerius: How do you know of that?

Galerius: You will not!

Galerius: Their emperor shall never know defeat.

Baltro: Your Majesty.

Galerius: Then these insects shall be more than enough. Grant me your strength, and we'll stamp them out together.

Galerius: What do you think you're doing?

Baltro: If it wasn't clear, Your Majesty, the sigil seeks none other.

Galerius: Traitorous fool. Finally gone senile, hm?

Alain: Mother!

Ilenia: Ngh.

Tatiana: There's nothing to worry about. She appears to be quite stable.

Alain: Speak to me, please.

Josef: I never imagined he possessed such frightful mastery over the bodies of others.

Ilenia: Alain. I can't say how much time has passed since that day, but you've grown so much.

Ilenia: If only I could have been there to witness it.

Ilenia: It seems I owe Josef a great deal for raising you in my absence.

Alain: Josef, see my mother somewhere safe.

Josef: And you, Your Highness?

Alain: We end this long-drawn war now.

Tatiana: Today shall be the day Baltro draws his final breath.

Tatiana: I've nothing to fear, as long as we're together.

Baltro: What evil should I reanimate next? A monster capable of crushing you beneath its heel, perhaps.

Alain: Spirits of Zenoira, hear my call.

Alain: Your emperor is no more, and in his place stands a tyrannical fiend who craves nothing but absolute control.

Alain: Tell me, is this what you truly desire? To sacrifice your very essence in service of this daemon?

Alain: Souls of the departed, if you have any humanity left within you, lend me your aid.

Alain: These souls are not a power one can wield, Baltro. They are human lives, human will in its purest form.

Alain: Let us lift the curse of the unicorn and bring the salvation of heaven to these lost souls.

#### Tatiana and Alain - Ending

Tatiana: It's actually my lack of regret which feels so odd.

Tatiana: Watching over you for as long as I live...

Tatiana: Just a moment's rest, and I'll be getting back to my work.

Tatiana: You're welcome to observe, if your feelings compel you.

Tatiana: As long as you don't get in my way, that is.

### Travis

#### Travis and Alain - Books

Alain: It is a surprise to find you buried in a book, Travis.

Travis: Reading is actually one of my favorite hobbies, I will have you know, though it is a little harder to keep up with nowadays.

Travis: We used to have a huge library back home, filled floor to ceiling with any book you could ever want.

Travis: It is all gone now, thanks to Zenoira.

Alain: I am sorry to hear that.

Travis: Do not be. We are not the only ones. Just about the whole continent has been through the same ordeal.

Travis: That is why it is so important we take back what is ours, and get rid of Zenoira once and for all.

Alain: Right you are.

Alain: By the way, what is that you are reading?

Travis: Caught your eye, did it?

Alain: I would love to read it myself once you are finished.

Travis: I did not realize you even knew how.

Alain: It is entirely thanks to Josef's mentorship, of course. I should at least remember well enough to manage.

Travis: Then here. I will let you have it now. I practically know this one by heart anyway.

Travis: Just let me know if there is anything you are having trouble understanding.

Alain: My thanks, Travis.

Travis: Any time. I will be looking forward to hearing what you think of it.

#### Travis and Alain - Making Friends

Alain: You seem troubled, Travis. Is everything all right?

Travis: I am fine. Though maybe you might know how to help.

Alain: With what, exactly?

Travis: Hypothetically speaking, there is someone in our army your friend is having trouble getting along with.

Travis: How would you go about fixing that?

Alain: Your friend wishes to be on better terms with them?

Travis: I am not asking for me, actually. Just a friend.

Alain: In that case, the simplest thing for your friend to do is tell the other party precisely how they feel.

Travis: What if he is not so good at speaking his mind?

Lex: What are you two talking about over here?

Travis: Might as well see what you think, too. Hypothetically speaking...

Lex: If you ask me, the quickest way to make a new friend is by being nice to them.

Travis: A surprisingly sensible idea, coming from you.

Lex: What is that supposed to mean?

Travis: I have to wonder, though. What does being nice even entail?

Alain: If it were Lex, he would likely do so by treating this person to a hearty meal.

Lex: Not a soul in Fevrith who does not like a warm bowl of food.

Travis: I had better get back to town. Thanks for the help.

Lex: He was definitely asking for himself, yeah?

Alain: Not a doubt in my mind. I only hope this venture of his proves successful.

#### Travis and Alain - A Shared Library

Alain: I appreciate you lending me so many books, Travis. It has been quite gratifying, this journey through the various genres of literature.

Travis: Glad you are having fun with it. What did you think of this one?

Alain: I consider that to be a rather self-evident idea myself.

Travis: With how long most of them live, you would normally think they would be talking about the future instead.

Alain: Regardless of lifespan, it is vital to exist in the here and now.

Alain: I plan to cherish every second I spend with my friends along the way, our triumphs and our troubles both.

Travis: Cannot disagree with you there.

Travis: I know it will not last forever either. Things will change once you take the throne.

Alain: The crown shall never keep me from speaking with you like this.

Travis: I hope you are right.

#### Travis and Alain - Ring of the Maiden

Travis: It is funny. I have spent some time looking into the legends about the Unicorn, and I do not see where I fit in.

Alain: I would like you to have the Ring of the Maiden.

Travis: Sorry, do I look like a maiden?

Alain: It does not matter what you look like. I ask this covenant not for your appearance, but your strength.

Travis: Could have said that sooner.

Travis: still, this seems like a pretty big decision. Not the kind of thing you work out standing up. Let us sit.

Travis: If swearing this oath is really how we beat Zenoira, I will be expecting a nice, cushy job in your court to make up for it.

Alain: Simply name the position and it is yours.

Travis: You know that means there will be no getting rid of me, right?

Alain: I do not mind. I could not think of a greater friend to have at my side.

Alain: Please, Travis. This rite is all that I desire, even should our war efforts ultimately fall short.

Travis: I can tell you are serious about this. Come on, hand that ring over.

Alain: It is an honor. Truly.

Travis: Guess that was it, then.

Travis: Once this is all over, maybe we can build ourselves a library. A huge one, with books from every corner of Fevrith. A place I can get lost in for days on end.

Alain: That sounds wonderful. You will have to save me a seat beside you.

#### Travis and Alain - Final Battle

Galerius: End this, now.

Galerius: Hmph.

Galerius: Gah.

Alain: Mother!

Galerius: How does it feel, hm? Your dear mother, slain by your own hand.

Alain: What is happening to me?

Travis: Hey. You feeling okay?

Galerius: You will make a fine Zenoiran vessel once it is over.

Galerius: The ring... why does it hold such vast energy?

Travis: Good news is, I am not ready to call it quits either.

Travis: I cannot say I feel any different, but I am not stopping yet. Not when we have already come so damn far.

Galerius: It will take more than this to defeat me.

Travis: Alain!

Alain: Galerius. You saw in Fevrith's innocent people mere vessels to house your own fallen empire.

Ilenia: Ngh.

#### Travis and Alain - Ending

Travis: All this time, I have been practically dying for a chance to just sit down and read together.

Bruno: Maybe I did get kind of caught up in the moment.

Travis: Thankfully, Alain did not really seem to mind. Guess that is our noble king for you.

Berengaria: We would never have come half this far if it was not for you.
