Melisandre: Now come, Colm. We will need our energy for tomorrow.

Colm: Of course, my lady. Rest well.

#### Melisandre and Colm - Ambush

Colm: Ngh!

Melisandre: Colm?

Colm: It is an ambush, my lady. You must escape.

Melisandre: And abandon you to die? I will do no such thing.

Colm: I will not be far behind you, I swear it. Go, while you still have time.

Colm: I beg you, do not waste your energy on me.

Melisandre: I am not leaving you here.

Colm: You must. There is no knowing what numbers the enemy brings.

Melisandre: We are making it back together, Colm, even if I have to carry you myself.

Colm: What incredible skill, my lady. You deflected their arrows as though they were a child's playthings.

Melisandre: You are awfully chipper for someone who has just been shot in the leg. Does it hurt?

Colm: The true wound here is to my pride. I have placed you in great danger.

Melisandre: Come. We should be out of their sight if we can make it over that ridge.

Colm: Very well.

Colm: Especially not for the sake of a mere servant in your employ.

Colm: Should a similar predicament ever arise again, there shall only be one proper course of action. Forsake me, and see that you live on.

Melisandre: You are hereby forbidden to die before my wedding day.

Colm: I understand, my lady.

Colm: As you wish. I will not depart this world without first witnessing your happiest of moments.

Colm: As for me, I am simply honored to serve such a wonderful woman.

### Colm and Miriam

#### Miriam and Colm - Devotion and Rest

Colm: Yes, that should be everything.

Colm: Lady Miriam, was it?

Miriam: Quite so. Forgive the interruption. I could not help but be captivated by the fervor with which you approach your work.

Miriam: If you will allow me the question, do you ever stop to rest or grant yourself a moment's leisure?

Colm: As for leisure, I have recently begun research into how I might brew the perfect cup of tea.

Colm: A labor which Lady Melisandre has benefited quite greatly from, I might add.

Miriam: Is that not merely another form of work?

Colm: I also enjoy fishing. It is a great pleasure, ensnaring Lady Melisandre's favorite varieties.

Miriam: That seems to be more work yet.

Colm: Perhaps the only reason I enjoy such hobbies at all is their prospective benefit to my lady.

Colm: I suppose I have been fated to the servant's life since the day I was born.

Miriam: It would seem I still have much to learn in the ways of devotion. I shall take this exchange to heart, Ser Colm.

Colm: It is a rare sight to witness one inspired by my duty rather than repulsed by it. I accept your words with pride.

Miriam: In any case, apologies again for the interruption. You clearly have much left to do.

Colm: Not at all. My tasks for the day are already complete.

Miriam: Then how do you plan to occupy yourself?

Colm: I suppose my lady's tent could use some tidying up, and I should begin thinking about tomorrow's dinner.

Miriam: It would seem an attendant's work is never truly complete.

### Colm and Railanor

#### Colm and Railanor - Searching for Their Ladies

Colm: Where are you, my lady? And how many times must I warn you not to pester Prince Alain?

Railanor: What if she has been hurt, or abducted by bandits?

Colm: Lady Railanor. Are you searching for your liege as well?

Railanor: Indeed I am. I am sorry you have to see me in such a state.

Colm: Please, you need not worry yourself over it. It would seem we are both held captive to the whims of our superiors.

Railanor: It was only later, when peace fell upon the region, that we learned he was in fact the leader of a local bandit ring.

Colm: I cannot say whether it was a sense of justice or simply attraction to their leader which first drew her interest.

Railanor: Excitable though they may be, both of our masters clearly bear immense skill and wisdom.

Colm: We have some luck indeed to be able to serve such fine women.

Colm: Now then, I should really be getting back to my search.

Railanor: As should I, though I suspect neither of them have any need of our help.

### Colm and Sharon

#### Sharon and Colm - Tailoring for Melisandre

Colm: Lady Melisandre deserves attire worthy of her noble stature, yet every tailor I find falls short.

Sharon: Then perhaps you should make it yourself.

Colm: I have no skill with needle or thread.

Sharon: No tailor can match your care or attention where Lady Melisandre is concerned.

Colm: You believe so?

Sharon: I do.

Colm: Then I shall become the greatest tailor in all Cornia.

Sharon: That may be more than I suggested.

Colm: For Lady Melisandre, nothing less will do.

#### Colm and Sharon - Tailoring for Melisandre

Colm: I could always hire a tailor in town, of course, but such humble attire would ill fit her noble stature.

Sharon: Is something the matter, Colm?

Colm: What fine timing, Lady Sharon. Might I trouble you for a moment of your wisdom?

Sharon: Have you ever thought about making her clothes yourself?

Colm: I have not even the skill of an amateur, and these weathered hands are far past their days of holding a needle.

Colm: Granted, I could attempt it, yet I fear it would take me years before I produced anything actually worth wearing.

Sharon: Which means none can possibly offer the caring, attentive tailorship that you can.

Colm: Am I truly capable of such artistry?

Sharon: You are, and I am certain the Father himself will see to it that you succeed.

Colm: Thank you, Lady Sharon. This day you have stoked the flame of servitude which burns deep within my breast.

Colm: Mark my words. From this moment forth, I shall become the greatest tailor the world has ever seen.

Sharon: I am not sure I have ever seen him that inspired before.

Sharon: Let us pray it does not have too severe an impact on his other work.

### Dinah and Primm

#### Dinah and Primm - Children

**Primm:** What are you doing out here, Dinah? You should be back inside, where it is warm.

**Dinah:** Bastorias was a country of bestrals, and no one else. For us kids, it was the most exciting thing you could ever imagine.

**Primm:** I suppose all children love the same things, no matter where they are from.

**Dinah:** But that was the last I would ever see of them.

**Primm:** What?

**Dinah:** Sometimes I think no matter what fights us bestrals get into, there are some lines we just will not cross. Abducting kids, for example. It is terrifying beyond belief.

**Primm:** I am sorry. At times, I have felt that same fear myself, come face to face with the darkness in our hearts.

**Dinah:** It might take some time, but I am trying to move on. Promise.

### Dinah and Railanor

#### Dinah and Railanor - Desert Heat

**Railanor:** Urgh. I have never experienced such sweltering heat in all my life.

**Dinah:** It is pretty rough out here, yeah. We had better start heading back to the oasis.

**Railanor:** I understand this may be a rude question, Dinah, but aren't you troubled by all that warm fur?

**Dinah:** Even if I were, do not dare say I should cut it. That would be like me telling you to scratch your own skin off.

**Railanor:** I did not mean to cause offense.

**Dinah:** Apparently, that summer coat is what kept him nice and cool through all this heat.

**Railanor:** Then there is your answer. Go on, shed.

**Dinah:** And would you mind not standing so damn close? That armor of yours is hot enough to grill a steak on.

**Railanor:** My apologies.

**Dinah:** What about you? Ever thought about cutting that hair of yours?

**Railanor:** It shall take far more than a little perspiration to break my conviction.

**Dinah:** Either way, the only thing we can do now is deal with it together.

### Dinah and Rolf

#### Dinah and Rolf - Hunting

**Dinah:** I hear you were a hunter before the war. The way you treat animals, like they exist for your savage sport and nothing more...

**Rolf:** That is not how all of us feel. I myself respect the sacrifice of every life that sustains my own.

**Dinah:** Then why be a hunter at all?

**Rolf:** Because my father was one. Because this was the only way I knew to right his wrongs.

**Dinah:** What do you mean?

**Rolf:** I felt complicit in his loathsome ways. I wished to give thanks to the natural world for all it provides us, rather than destroy its bounties for my own damned pleasure.

**Dinah:** Sorry for assuming otherwise. I have had plenty of bad experiences with your type in my day.

**Rolf:** It would seem all of Fevrith is plagued by ruthless men like my father.

**Dinah:** Maybe so, but that has nothing to do with you. Do not go punishing yourself for someone else's sins.

**Rolf:** And thank you for hearing my story, Dinah.

#### Rolf and Dinah - Respect for the Hunt

Dinah: Hunters treat animals like sport. As if killing them were a game.

Rolf: Some do. I do not.

Dinah: Then what is the difference?

Rolf: I respect every life that sustains my own. I hunt to live, and I give thanks for what I take.

Dinah: You speak as if you are making up for someone else's sins.

Rolf: My father hunted differently. I chose another path to right those wrongs as best I could.

Dinah: Then I am sorry for judging you. But do not punish yourself forever for another person's cruelty.

Rolf: I will try to remember that.

### Dinah and Yunifi

#### Dinah and Yunifi - Claws

**Yunifi:** Say, Dinah, everyone in the Liberation is pretty nice, huh?

**Dinah:** Guess they are not bad for outsiders.

**Yunifi:** Aha! I knew you were warming up to them.

**Dinah:** You say that like I am colder than the damn snow. Not what I would call friendly.

**Yunifi:** Are you sure you are not just avoiding them?

**Dinah:** If I had to guess, I would bet they are all afraid of the scary bestral and her sharp claws. And they are right to be. If I get too close, it is really easy for me to accidentally cut someone.

**Yunifi:** You do not want to hurt anyone, so you are subconsciously staying as far away from them as you can. Remember that time we were holding hands when we were just kids? Now, you say you only look after yourself, but I know you have kept them filed down ever since.

**Dinah:** Hmph. Did not think you would notice that.

**Yunifi:** With a friend I care about as much as you? How could I not? I will not hear another word of it, Dinah. I have got news to spread.

**Dinah:** Yunifi, wait!

#### Yunifi and Dinah - A Promise

**Yunifi:** Hey, Dinah?

**Dinah:** Yeah?

**Yunifi:** Hmm. Oh, nothing.

**Dinah:** Like I am gonna buy that. Come on, out with it.

**Yunifi:** It has just been ages since we have gotten to bask in the sun like this.

**Dinah:** This is the same spot where we used to do it, too. Then we would sneak over into the checkpoint after dark and scare the life out of all the soldiers.

**Yunifi:** I guess I understand why Ramona was always so mad at us when we told her about it.

**Dinah:** We thought we were invincible, that nothing could touch us so long as we were together. Sometimes I wish we were still those same kids. Innocent. Happy.

**Yunifi:** Dinah?

**Dinah:** Listen to me, Yunifi. This war with Zenoira is getting worse every day, and it is not stopping any time soon. Alain will keep you safe. I am sure of it.

**Yunifi:** What are you talking about, Dinah? We always promised we would protect each other, not just one way around!

**Dinah:** Hmph. You are a good kid, you know that? But sometimes you have gotta forget the past and look ahead.

**Yunifi:** I cannot believe you would even think such a thing. As long as we have known each other, it has always been what you want, what you feel. Well, how about me, huh? Please, never talk to me about dying again.

**Dinah:** There is no guarantee that any of us will make it back alive.

**Yunifi:** I do not care. The only thing that matters to me is being with you.

**Dinah:** I am not going anywhere. I swear it.

**Yunifi:** Thank you, Dinah. You are the best friend a girl could ever ask for.

**Dinah:** Heh. I guess this is what I get for indulging you all the time.

### Eltolinde and Galadmir

#### Eltolinde and Galadmir - Guardian

**Galadmir:** If I may, Terras, it is a great honor to serve at your side once more.

**Eltolinde:** When the magick which clouded my mind finally lifted, you were nowhere to be seen.

**Galadmir:** All I could do was bide my time until the proper moment presented itself.

**Eltolinde:** And if you had died, I would never have been able to live with myself.

**Galadmir:** Especially if it were you after my life.

**Eltolinde:** My, is someone feeling confident?

**Galadmir:** I have never lost a single sparring match to you in all our years together.

**Eltolinde:** I am no longer the child you may remember me as, and I shall prove as such in a bout this very moment.

**Galadmir:** Then may luck be with you.

**Eltolinde:** That was... quite the battle, Galadmir.

**Galadmir:** Indeed it was. You have truly grown, Terras.

**Eltolinde:** Heheh.

**Galadmir:** What is it?

**Eltolinde:** It simply struck me how many moons have passed since we have been able to speak like this. Growing up here in Laurhal, few regarded me as anything beyond their blessed Turenos. Yet at times, you would laugh with us like the third sister we never had.

**Galadmir:** I suppose I would, yes.

**Eltolinde:** I was so extremely grateful to have you, Galadmir. Just the same as I am now.

**Galadmir:** Such words are wasted on a failed guardian.

**Eltolinde:** What matters now is that you are here. And I could not ask for anything more.

#### Eltolinde and Galadmir - A New Elheim

**Eltolinde:** Ah, Galadmir. Precisely the woman I was searching for.

**Galadmir:** Terras?

**Eltolinde:** No longer do I wish to return to the days of yore. Instead, I would found a new Elheim where people of all races and creeds can live in harmony.

**Galadmir:** To my ear, it sounds as though you seek to excise the roots of our very society.

**Eltolinde:** I do. And I could not imagine doing so without you at my side. One whose support, and whose love, I could not bear to be without in the trying times which lie ahead.

**Galadmir:** ...

**Eltolinde:** Have I said something to offend?

**Galadmir:** Not at all, Terras. It is merely that your kindness moved me to tears.

**Eltolinde:** Did it now? I hardly thought myself capable.

**Galadmir:** Indeed, it is difficult to believe the little girl I once knew can truly deliver such touching words.

**Eltolinde:** It would seem you will always consider me that same child.

**Galadmir:** You have grown to be an elegant woman, Terras, and a fine Turenos at that.

**Eltolinde:** And what of my proposal? Will you join me, Galadmir?

**Galadmir:** Both as your retainer and as your friend.

**Eltolinde:** Thank you, Galadmir, from the very depths of my heart. I hope never to lose your loyalty, your strength, or your compassion.

### Eltolinde and Lex

#### Eltolinde and Lex - Elves and Dark Elves

**Lex:** Y'know, the more I spend time with you, the more I realize how similar you and Rosalinde look.

**Eltolinde:** I should not think that much of a surprise. We are sisters, after all.

**Lex:** Maybe. But, uh... Look, don't take this the wrong way, but I don't think I get how race works over here in Elheim.

**Eltolinde:** 'Tis quite simple, really. Our father is an elf, while our mother is a dark elf. Rather than combine their traits as happens with humans, the offspring of such a pairing will either be one or the other.

**Lex:** I think I get it. Huh. But now I'm just wondering how they met in the first place.

**Eltolinde:** It began when my grandmother, our former Turenos, visited Quantipelt, the subterranean capital of dark elven civilization. She had brought my father along for the journey, and it was there he laid eyes upon the most beautiful elf he had ever seen.

**Eltolinde:** Fresh-picked flowers one moment, handiwork from our finest artisans the next. The two were soon wed, thus dedicating themselves to the good of Elheim and the unity of our races.

**Lex:** And that's how a dark elf like your mom ended up Turenos.

**Eltolinde:** Until at last, all who opposed her reign relented. Through their marriage, the age-old rift between our disparate races could finally begin to heal, no matter how ingrained prejudice may be in our lands.

**Lex:** Plenty more were singing our praises when we drove those bastards out of your towns. Hell, by the time this war is over and done with, I bet humans and elves'll be the best of friends.

**Eltolinde:** I only hope I can aid in that pursuit, however minor my contribution may be.

### Eltolinde and Lhinalagos

#### Eltolinde and Lhinalagos - Childhood

**Eltolinde:** Hello there, Lhinalagos.

**Lhinalagos:** It has been some time, Terras. Is there aught I can assist with?

**Eltolinde:** There is, in fact. Might I speak with you for a moment? In truth, those moments together are what gave me the strength to endure the rigors of my training to become Turenos.

**Lhinalagos:** Ah.

**Eltolinde:** Tell me. What caused us to grow apart all those years ago?

**Lhinalagos:** A commoner such as I bears no right to associate with one of your royal blood.

**Eltolinde:** Even if I myself wished for it? I must know. Do you regret the time we spent together, even now?

**Lhinalagos:** My only regret is that I was not there that horrible day. If only I had been, perhaps those fiends would never even have reached your door.

**Eltolinde:** Should that truly be how you feel, Lhinalagos, then I pray you will not make the same mistake twice. Allow me to ask you again: would you do me the honor of joining my personal guard?

#### Eltolinde and Lhinalagos - Brother

**Eltolinde:** Lhinalagos, there you are.

**Lhinalagos:** Is there aught I can help you with, Terras?

**Eltolinde:** It concerns our time together as children. Amidst all those hours we spent roaming the city, enjoying our time together until the sun made its nest beneath the horizon, I was able to treat you as the second sibling I never had.

**Eltolinde:** 'Twas an act most selfish of me. Granted, such thoughts are hardly appropriate given our social distinctions.

**Eltolinde:** Please, Lhinalagos. Let us relive our youth, then never speak of this again.

**Lhinalagos:** I am proud of you, Eltolinde. Proud of everything you are, and everything you have become these past ten years. 'Tis a memory I will treasure greater than any other, for as long as I walk this sacred earth.

**Eltolinde:** Thank you, my brother.

### Eltolinde and Rosalinde

#### Rosalinde and Eltolinde - Tea

**Eltolinde:** Rosalinde, wait!

**Rosalinde:** Hm? What seems to be the matter?

**Eltolinde:** We have yet to even find the time to have tea together.

**Rosalinde:** Feeling lonely without your ionisa to keep you company, I see?

**Eltolinde:** Is there a problem with that?

**Rosalinde:** Heheh, not at all. I am actually glad to see you so desperate to overcome my disregard.

**Eltolinde:** Even knowing how alone I felt in your absence?

**Rosalinde:** I am sorry, uin nisa. It is just too fun not to tease you every now and then.

**Eltolinde:** How cruel. I only ever wished to spend time with you, and this is my reward?

**Liberation Soldier:** Pardon the interruption, my lady. I come with a report concerning the guards for your sister, and...

**Liberation Soldier:** Ah!

**Rosalinde:** Now is not the best time, as I think you can see.

**Liberation Soldier:** Of course, my lady. We will speak more of this later.

**Eltolinde:** Would you care to explain?

**Rosalinde:** Given what happened to Laurhal, I was afraid elven guards alone would not be enough to keep you safe. But I did not expect it would take quite so long to find humans I could trust with the task.

**Eltolinde:** While you were acting out of concern for my well-being, I behaved like little more than a spoiled child.

**Rosalinde:** Enough of that, please. So what do you say? Shall we head to town for that cup of tea you mentioned?

**Eltolinde:** I would be glad to. Ah, there is so much I have to talk to you about!

#### Eltolinde and Rosalinde - Sisters

**Eltolinde:** That cake you brought seemed every bit real, mushroom-chocolate dirt and all.

**Rosalinde:** I am glad you liked it. I had it made especially for you, you know.

**Eltolinde:** To be honest, I had such fun that day that I am certain a smile still graced my lips as I fell asleep.

**Rosalinde:** Heheh. It is good to see you are still as excitable as ever.

**Eltolinde:** I have to ask, though. Did you enjoy yourself as well, ionisa? I struggle to tell if you ever have any fun yourself.

**Rosalinde:** Oh, Eltolinde. You really have no idea, do you? Of course I had fun with you. How could you possibly ever think otherwise?

**Eltolinde:** I feel like I can barely tell the first thing about you.

**Rosalinde:** So if you really care about how I feel, you will keep that smile of yours as warm and beautiful as ever.

**Eltolinde:** Rosalinde... I feel exactly the same. Now let us enjoy the evening stars together.

### Eltolinde and Scarlett

#### Scarlett and Eltolinde - Flower Reading

Scarlett: I could do this a thousand times and it would always end the same way.

Eltolinde: What offense have our flowers committed to see you tear an entire field apart petal by petal?

Scarlett: Eltolinde. I was hoping I might do a little flower reading, and I thought there would be no better place than Elheim.

Eltolinde: And what is that, pray tell?

Scarlett: Whichever you say as you pick the last petal tells you how the person feels about you.

Eltolinde: I see. This is difficult for me to say, Scarlett, but you could simply choose one with an odd number of petals.

Scarlett: You surely cannot be serious. If you already knew what would happen before you started, it would not be much of a game.

Eltolinde: That is true, yes.

Eltolinde: Then I suppose no amount of disappointment could ever subdue you.

Scarlett: This is a matter of the heart, Eltolinde, not logic.

Scarlett: Alain brought this flower from Cornia, too, so I have no idea how many petals it has.

Eltolinde: Forgive me. I should never have offered my opinion without first experiencing it on my own.

Eltolinde: Alain loves me. He loves me not. He loves me...

Scarlett: Wait. Why did you choose Alain?

Eltolinde: He loves me not. He loves me. He loves me not. He loves me.

Scarlett: No.

Eltolinde: Did you give me that flower knowing it had an even number of petals?

Scarlett: I would not dream of it.

Scarlett: But now you understand, right? How horrible it feels to end on "he loves me not."

Eltolinde: This reading has only served to sow a deep seed of doubt in my heart.

Eltolinde: My mind is set. I will not ignore this grave portent.

Scarlett: Something tells me you are still not getting the point of all this.

### Eltolinde and Umerus

#### Eltolinde and Umerus - Flowers

**Eltolinde:** Umerus, I hear you have quite a breadth of knowledge regarding flowers and their many varieties.

**Umerus:** I do, yes. Before she passed, my mother taught me everything she knew of the blossoms she loved so dearly.

**Eltolinde:** In truth, I bear a similar memory. My nursemaid spent many of her days tending to our palace's flower gardens. She was also the one responsible for training me to become Turenos.

**Eltolinde:** From dawn until dusk, she would instruct me in all manner of prayers and rituals, never allowing me to leave the castle walls. In an act of clandestine defiance, I began to cultivate a garden of my own in the basement.

**Umerus:** Away from the sun? But how?

**Eltolinde:** It brought to mind scenes from the greatest fictions I had ever read.

**Umerus:** It sounds closer to a horror story to me.

**Eltolinde:** Yet nothing lasts forever. One day, my nursemaid discovered the garden I had worked so hard to keep from her. It was the most terrible sight I had ever witnessed.

**Umerus:** I cannot say I altogether blame her.

**Eltolinde:** Thus, I decided to grow an herb: the lively mint plant.

**Umerus:** Mint? But left unchecked...

**Eltolinde:** It consumes everything in its path, yes. In the end, it choked the very life from my nursemaid's beloved flowers.

**Umerus:** How could you do such a thing?

**Eltolinde:** Heheh. There is nothing like a bit of quiet horticulture, hm?

### Eltolinde and Yunifi

#### Yunifi and Eltolinde - Clouds

**Eltolinde:** In this land of snow, the sky seems to be a single blue petal, set ablaze at its edge by dawn's first light. Our dawns are more akin to golden nectar spilling down the side of a ripe persimmon.

**Yunifi:** This one time a few years ago, I was walking on the beach when I spotted a cloud shaped like the fuzziest cat you have ever seen. I tried running after it to see where it was heading, and ended up falling straight into the ocean.

**Eltolinde:** In your eyes, perhaps it truly was there, prowling the heavens in search of a mouse to catch. A lovely idea, made all the lovelier by the colors of the rising sun.

**Eltolinde:** Hm. Do you see that one there? It resembles a poisonous herb which grows rampant in my homeland.

**Yunifi:** I think that is a little more intense than what I had in mind.

### Fodoquia and Scarlett

#### Fodoquia and Scarlett - Hymns

**Scarlett:** I would recognize those hymns anywhere.

**Fodoquia:** During my rule of Peyston, my citizens would often flock to church in order to raise their voices in dutiful song. Despite the atrocities inflicted upon my family, they sought one of their own amidst the Father's embrace.

**Fodoquia:** Just as it was for me. The thought alone mocked me day in and day out. And now to hear those hymns once more, freed as I am from my mournful past, it feels as though fate itself mocks me as well.

**Scarlett:** Come, then. Let us head back to camp.

**Scarlett:** Lord Fodoquia?

**Fodoquia:** Yet 'tis only now I realize: casting aside my faith shall ever deny me the progress I so desperately seek. I pray that none shall ever have to suffer the wretched sorrow I have.

**Scarlett:** I have some words I would like to offer the Father myself, both for you and for your son.

**Fodoquia:** You have my thanks, Lady Scarlett.

#### Fodoquia and Scarlett - Memory of His Son

**Scarlett:** You might not realize this, but we have met before. Years ago, when I was just a young girl. Your son and I were quite close, in fact. As for you, I remember a man of great integrity, great warmth.

**Fodoquia:** Yes. I recognize you now. You have grown so much since I saw you last.

**Fodoquia:** The time has finally come to see my son once again.

**Scarlett:** If you would, hold to his memory.

**Alain:** Are you certain you are well enough to fight, Fodoquia?

**Fodoquia:** I realize now you wished to grant me an opportunity to seize revenge against Zenoira.

**Alain:** That is not why. I pray that with your aid, we can ensure none will ever again have to experience what you did.

**Fodoquia:** 'Tis a merciless way to think of the world.

**Alain:** Forgive me.

**Fodoquia:** Please, lift your gaze. After the torment inflicted upon my citizens out of pure spite, I cannot claim to be any better. But I will fight to see that no further innocents are met with an early demise.

**Alain:** Then let us take up arms once more, Fodoquia, not as enemies as we were before, but as allies.

### Fran and Hilda

#### Fran and Hilda - Feared Beasts

Drakenhold Soldier: The hell are they thinking, keeping that wyvern around? You never know when a beast like that might go for your throat.

Drakenhold Soldier: I am certain they chain it up outside battle. There would simply be no controlling it otherwise.

Hilda: You are wrong. This beast is akin to my own family, and he would never attack anyone without good reason.

Drakenhold Soldier: Apologies, ma'am. Please do not hurt us.

Hilda: I take it you saw that?

Fran: I cannot believe you stood up to those soldiers, Hilda.

Fran: I hear them repeating the same cruel things about my gryphon sometimes, but I never have the courage to say anything.

Fran: Maybe I am the cruel one for not defending her.

Hilda: Your fear does not excuse the hurtful manner in which the rest of this army treats our companions.

Fran: Maybe there is a way we can help everyone overcome those fears.

Hilda: Go on, then.

Fran: They could go on walks together and feed them treats. It would be fun, at least I think it would.

Hilda: I cannot wait to see what those three from earlier have to say once we force them into it.

Fran: I will have to start planning right away. And you will be joining the festivities yourself, right?

Hilda: I would not miss it for the world.

### Fran and Kitra

#### Fran and Kitra - The Rabid Liberation Dog

Mercenary: We will get you for this, girl. Just you wait.

Fran: What is going on?

Kitra: Those mercs were making fun of me, so I taught them a little manners.

Fran: Is that really all it took? You cannot resort to violence over every bad word said about you.

Kitra: I am not a noble, Fran, and neither are you. Not anymore.

Fran: We will be. Once His Highness takes the throne, everything will go back to the way it used to be.

Kitra: That is what they say, yes. Me, I am not holding my breath. That is how it is, and that is how it has always been.

Kitra: Anyway, I should get going. Places to be.

Fran: I wonder if that is a promise she can really keep.

#### Fran and Kitra - Self-Restraint

Fran: More mercenaries, Kitra?

Kitra: I was hoping you would not find out about that.

Fran: Do you know what those mercenaries are calling you now?

Kitra: What?

Fran: Rabid Liberation dog.

Kitra: If they were not talking about me behind my back...

Fran: Most of the other orders want nothing to do with us now, likely in fear of what your hammer might do to them.

Kitra: Same goes for the princess, you know.

Fran: They might even try to ambush you. What then?

Kitra: Is it not obvious? I would smack them into next week.

Fran: If you would only learn restraint, perhaps the rest of the army would not turn and walk the other way when they see you coming.

Kitra: They really do that?

Fran: Ahem. It is time we start working on that self-restraint of yours.

Kitra: How are we going to do that?

Fran: I gathered a number of anonymous complaints. It only came out to five hundred pages.

Kitra: You have got to be kidding me.

Fran: You just have to stand there and figure out how to manage your emotions while I read.

Kitra: I never agreed to this.

Fran: "Kitra never helps sharpen the weapons, so we always have to do it instead."

Kitra: Agh.

Fran: Next is from a soldier who spends much of their time on cooking duty. It says it is anonymous, but I think you can guess who that is.

Fran: "It would be wonderful if Kitra could please stop eating three people's worth of food in one sitting."

Kitra: All right, all right. I get it already.

Fran: Patience, Kitra. We are only just getting started.

### Fran and Miriam

#### Fran and Miriam - Family Gifts

Fran: What can I possibly do with all this? I could not ask Kitra again, not after last time.

Miriam: Is this how I learn you are abandoning our order?

Fran: I am thankful for the gift, of course, but I will never be able to eat it all on my own.

Fran: They also sent me an array of formal wear, which has about as much use in battle as a hibernating gryphon.

Fran: Knowing the company we keep, wearing anything too fancy would only make me stick out.

Miriam: Might you be able to send it all back?

Fran: I would rather not hurt my parents' feelings if I can avoid it.

Miriam: The only missives I have ever received from my father demanded that I honor our family name on the field of battle, and nothing else.

Miriam: I suppose I should be pleased to hear anything at all from him. The man is taciturn, to say the least.

Fran: Even so, I am sure he worries about you in his own unique way.

Fran: I would bet no feat of bravery could ever make him happier than seeing you get home safe.

Miriam: I pray you are correct.

#### Fran and Miriam - Expectations

Miriam: It merely grazed me. Nothing to worry about, I assure you.

Fran: Miriam, you were struck by a stray arrow.

Miriam: I only have my own recklessness to blame. Such is my punishment for pressing too far into enemy territory.

Miriam: If I fail in tasks as simple as this, how shall I ever earn my family the glory my father expects?

Fran: Your father's demands stem from the regret he bears for swearing fealty to Zenoira, a matter in which he had little choice.

Miriam: Thank you for saying so.

Miriam: Hard as I try, I shall never be a warrior of your innate talent.

Fran: You do not need to be me.

Miriam: But it is the one way I will prove that I deserve to exist at all, both to my father and to myself.

Fran: Then I am glad you can say that aloud. We can help one another bear it.

Miriam: I am glad to hear you say that, although Kitra claimed me to be more of a nagging mother than anything.

Kitra: Hey, why are my ears burning? Nobody better be saying anything bad about me.

### Fran and Ramona

#### Fran and Ramona - Desert Heat

Ramona: What sweltering heat. I have never experienced such a sensation in all my years.

Fran: There is a good girl. You must have really needed that.

Ramona: What are you doing out here, Fran?

Fran: You hear that, girl? We are heading back to camp.

Ramona: To feel the sand between my unclothed feathers, without so much as a care in the world.

Ramona: Calm, Ramona. You are no simple bird, but a dignified bestrale.

Ramona: Perhaps I could indulge just this once.

Fran: Ramona? His Highness would like to speak with you.

Ramona: It is not what it seems like, I assure you.

Ramona: Just look away while I put my garments back on, please.

Fran: I will let His Highness know you will be there soon.

Ramona: What utter embarrassment. I will have to remind myself never to visit this bewitching desert again.

### Fran and Umerus

#### Fran and Umerus - Incense

Fran: No matter how long it has been, I will never get used to that accursed tent.

Fran: Oh, Umerus. Are you having trouble sleeping as well?

Umerus: No, actually. I was enjoying quite a relaxing rest until I heard someone rustling around outside camp.

Fran: I am sorry for waking you.

Umerus: It is not a problem. If you need help falling asleep, I may have just the thing.

Fran: What beautiful incense. Are you sure you are willing to give it away so easily?

Umerus: I would do that and more if it meant helping you get a good night's sleep.

Fran: Thank you, Umerus.

Umerus: Good morning, Fran. How did you sleep?

Fran: Wonderfully, thanks to you. The incense works great.

Fran: Though it turns out Miriam was not too happy about being denied her reading time.

Umerus: Apologies. It seems I only added to your worries.

Fran: Oh, no. You helped plenty.

### Fran and Virginia

#### Virginia and Fran - Packing

Fran: I have my armor. I have my belt. But why does it feel like I'm forgetting something?

Virginia: Have you really been inspecting your gear all morning, Fran? It's been hours by now.

Fran: I was hoping to lighten my pack before we set off, actually.

Fran: I've gathered my essentials and checked them over dozens of times, but I still feel like there's something I'm forgetting.

Virginia: Besides, it can't be that important if you're struggling that hard to remember.

Fran: Yes, you're probably right.

Virginia: Now stop thinking about this and go get some rest. That's an order.

Fran: Of course, Princess.

Fran: But what if you come across an insect and I'm not there to chase it away?

Virginia: Whatever happens, Kitra and I will handle it.

Virginia: Even a bug, if necessary.

Fran: But I could never impose on you like that, Princess.

Virginia: You can, and you will, whether you like it or not.

Fran: There she goes.

Fran: How am I supposed to sleep when I can't stop wondering if she's okay?

### Galadmir and Gammel

#### Gammel and Galadmir - Recognition

**Galadmir:** Hah!

**Gammel:** Hey, what's the big idea? Ya got a problem with me, ya can say it to my face.

**Galadmir:** Is that you, Gammel? From where I stood, your physique resembled that of a fugitive who has long plagued this region.

**Gammel:** Woulda pierced him clean through the heart. Guessin' ya weren't plannin' to take him in alive.

**Galadmir:** I was not, no. Not only is the man a prolific thief, but a murderer, too. One who takes great pleasure in his cruel deeds. So if we ever face an enemy who brandishes his blade with utter glee, then we will know it is him.

**Gammel:** Makes me sick to my stomach, seein' what some people are capable of.

**Galadmir:** Tell me, did the guilt of your actions not weigh heavy on your heart?

**Gammel:** Crimes are crimes, even if they got good reasons behind 'em.

**Galadmir:** Indeed. I hope you know that yours will be punished in kind once this war is over.

**Gammel:** Fine by me. At least I know my sister will have some good people watchin' over her after I'm gone. And I bet once he is, nobody will have to thieve to survive ever again.

**Galadmir:** I pray you are right.

### Galadmir and Ithilion

#### Ithilion and Galadmir - Snow

**Ithilion:** Is it only me, Galadmir, or is there something oddly calming about these frozen lands?

**Galadmir:** Standing still for even a moment will see us buried to our waists in snow, while battle consumes twice the energy as it does elsewhere. Ah, I see now. That was meant to be a joke, in hopes of alleviating the unfamiliarity between us.

**Galadmir:** To be frank, I had not thought you the jesting type.

**Ithilion:** I did not realize I was quite that unsociable. And I will have you know, it was no joke. This place reminds me of the subterranean city I am from. I feel at home here, almost as though I could lie down for a nice rest.

**Galadmir:** Yes, and it would be the last rest you ever took. It is clear to me now that frigid climes have dulled your wits. Come, we should get you somewhere warm before the stupor grows worse. I will drag you back to Ter Rosalinde myself if I must.

**Ithilion:** If anything, I would guess the only ailment afflicting me is a severe case of homesickness.

### Galadmir and Ridiel

#### Ridiel and Galadmir - Hunting Chickens

Ridiel: Just hold still.

Brown Chicken: Bawk bawk!

Ridiel: And now you are mocking me, are you? Damned birds.

Galadmir: I do not mean to interrupt, Ridiel, but what exactly are you doing here? You have been away from camp for some time now.

Ridiel: Can you not tell? I am hunting chickens.

Galadmir: It does not seem as though you are having any luck.

Ridiel: stand back and watch me.

Galadmir: Very well. Let us see how true those arrows of yours can fly.

Ridiel: Why? I do not understand. I cannot hit them.

Galadmir: It certainly is not a matter of skill, I assure you. The issue lies in your lack of patience.

Galadmir: Once you fall prisoner to the need to hit your mark, an animal will sense that desperation and easily dodge your attack.

Galadmir: This time, quiet your mind and focus on nothing but the arrow in your hand.

Ridiel: All right. I will try.

Brown Chicken: Bawk!

Ridiel: Another miss.

Galadmir: Not entirely. You masked your intent rather well, and grazed your target as a result.

Ridiel: No point complaining if I am taking another shot.

Ridiel: Phew.

Galadmir: That should be all your chickens, yes?

Ridiel: Granted, one of them did get away, but I do not think they will be causing me any more trouble.

Ridiel: Thank you for this, Galadmir.

Galadmir: Next time you buy chickens, perhaps you should make sure they never escape at all.

Ridiel: Great advice. Thanks.

### Gammel and Mandrin

#### Gammel and Mandrin - The Bow

**Mandrin:** Wish it did not take all my coin to do it, but...

**Girl:** Ah! My bowl!

**Mandrin:** Tell me something, kid. You did not get hurt there, did you?

**Girl:** Well, no, ser. But what about your bow?

**Mandrin:** You saved me the trouble of getting rid of it, if anything. Now go on and run home before it gets dark. Wouldn't want your parents worrying about you, yeah?

**Girl:** Okay. Bye, mister!

**Mandrin:** There goes my new bow, floating in pieces down the damned river.

**Gammel:** Ya always have been good with kids, Mandrin. Shame about the bow, though. I know ya had your eye on it for a while. Ya sure ya wanna watch it just float away?

**Mandrin:** I was about to get rid of it anyway.

**Gammel:** Heh. Sure ya were. Here, go and buy yourself another one.

**Mandrin:** Is this some kind of joke?

**Gammel:** Does it look like I'm laughin'? Don't really need the coin anymore. Ya earned it, mister.

**Mandrin:** Ugh. Well, no point looking a gift horse in the mouth.

#### Gammel and Mandrin - A Named Bow

**Gammel:** It is always the same thing, too. Bugs crawlin' all over me, callin' my name the whole time.

**Gammel:** People are sayin' ya seem like a new man since buyin' it.

**Mandrin:** Well, I feel like one, and it is all on account of Gammel II here. Figured nobody deserved the honor more than my old partner in crime. It is only fair after you gave me the coin to buy it.

**Gammel:** But ya don't gotta give it my name.

**Mandrin:** Carved your name right into the grip the day I got it. Not happening. If that does not prove I picked the right name, I do not know what will. A friend like that will never let you down.

**Gammel:** Ya mean you have been sayin' my name in the middle of the night?

**Mandrin:** Sure have.

**Gammel:** And you have been doin' it while I was sleepin' next to ya?

**Mandrin:** That is the short of it, yep.

**Gammel:** Mandrin, you're the reason I'm havin' all those nightmares!

### Gammel and Nina

#### Nina and Gammel - Rock Rats

Gammel: I could have sworn they had taken you hostage.

Nina: How could you think such a thing? The Rock Rats would never harm anyone without proper reason.

Gammel: Guess it is true what that captain of yours says. He would not hurt a fly if he thought it had something worth living for.

Gammel: still cannot see you fitting in, though. The other thieves ever give you any trouble?

Nina: Even after I tore a hole in a stolen sack of flour, leaving clouds of white powder scattered throughout town?

Gammel: The way I heard it, people thought the whole place was going up in smoke.

Nina: They must truly have thought of me as little more than a liability.

Gammel: I do not know about that. Sounds to me like they really cared about you.

Gammel: And that is not even mentioning how good you are with that hammer. I would take you in my gang any day of the week.

Nina: You truly mean that? Well, I suppose I will not argue.

Nina: Let us talk again sometime, shall we?

Gammel: That girl's not half bad, in spite of the tongue.

### Gammel and Rolf

#### Gammel and Rolf - A Shadowed Past

**Gammel:** If you're gonna ambush me, ya better do it quick. Ya won't get another shot.

**Rolf:** You knew I was following you.

**Gammel:** Of course I did. A rogue like me would have noticed the minute you picked up my trail. Spend enough time livin' in shadow, and it starts becomin' a part of ya, whether ya want it to or not.

**Rolf:** It is the least you deserve for the cruelty you have committed.

**Gammel:** So, can I help ya with somethin'? Or are ya just gonna stand here and insult me?

**Rolf:** Prince Alain has granted you a place in our army, and I do not intend to criticize that decision. But had those innocent villagers encountered Zenoiran soldiers instead, they would now be nothing more than corpses.

**Rolf:** Now tell me. Do others deserve to die so that your sister might live?

**Gammel:** Back then, I woulda said yes. Wouldn't even have to think about it. But I'm a whole new man now, and it is all thanks to our prince. Wouldn't touch a hair on those girls' heads.

**Gammel:** Doubt you'll believe it, though.

**Rolf:** I believe you are a coward who will stab us in the neck the first chance you get.

**Gammel:** Suit yourself. But I promise ya, I'm never goin' back to that life again. If ya ever think I'm gonna turn on ya, just put an arrow between my eyes and be done with it.

**Rolf:** Hell will be a kindness after the life you have led, one which will greet you no matter what end you face.

**Gammel:** Guess so, yeah. Doesn't matter how hard I try. There's no washin' the blood off these hands.

#### Rolf and Gammel - Blood on the Hands

Gammel: You have been following me. If you are going to shoot, best get it over with.

Rolf: I wanted to know whether you had changed.

Gammel: And?

Rolf: If innocent villagers stood between you and your sister's safety, what would you do?

Gammel: The man I was would have answered one way. The man I am now owes the prince better than that. I would not hurt them.

Rolf: That answer does not erase what you did.

Gammel: No. There is no washing this blood off my hands.

Rolf: Then remember that every day.

Gammel: I intend to.

### Gammel and Travis

#### Gammel and Travis - Taking Over

**Gammel:** Hmph. I knew somethin' was wrong when ya stopped reportin' back.

**Travis:** I messed up, Gammel. Bad.

**Gammel:** Well, don't worry. That's why I'm here to take over for ya.

**Travis:** What about the others?

**Gammel:** None of that stuff is gonna matter if ya end up gettin' yourself caught, y'know.

**Travis:** Yeah, guess not. Oh, and thanks again for doing this for me.

**Alain:** Have you seen Gammel anywhere, Clive?

**Gammel:** Right here, boss. He says Zenoira's runnin' outta supplies, and fast at that.

**Alain:** I should be off to alert Travis of the plan as well.

**Gammel:** Nah, you just keep doin' your thing from here. I'll let him know what's what.

**Travis:** Sorry about earlier, Alain. Must have caused some real problems for Gammel back there. I got hurt pretty bad while I was out on my scouting mission. At least, till Gammel showed up and took over for me. What, he didn't tell you?

**Gammel:** Only fair I went in his place. Go on, then. I'll stomach whatever punishment ya wanna dish out.

**Alain:** Had you delayed for even a moment, my order to halt our advance would have come too late, magnifying our fatigue even further.

**Gammel:** Well, look who's gone all soft on me.

### Gilbert and Gloucester

#### Gilbert and Gloucester - The Desert

**Town Girl:** Thinking about the family I lost 'cause of you, even if it wasn't really "you" in control... I dunno.

**Gloucester:** I am truly sorry for the pain I have caused.

**Town Girl:** If you really mean that, then leave. And never come back.

**Gilbert:** She was a denizen of the desert, was she?

**Gloucester:** Apologies you had to witness that, my king.

**Gilbert:** Please, it is quite all right. 'Tis a shameful thing to admit, but today is the first time I have ever set foot in Drakenhold's desert.

**Gloucester:** I suppose I cannot blame you for that. But that does not change how the rest of our nation views it. Many who seek a new life outside the desert are met with extreme discrimination, often failing to find work because of it.

**Gloucester:** Most resort to banditry as a means to survive, thus perpetuating the cycle of distrust. My family owes this desert and its people a great debt.

**Gloucester:** It was the kindness of these sands which saw my parents and I, still an infant at the time, survive being stranded in the scorching wilderness.

**Gloucester:** No. I shall aid them in breaking the chains of hatred and doubt which shackle them. Though try as I might, the nobles of our nation have turned a deaf ear to my unending pleas.

**Gilbert:** Ludwig never has been one to care for public sentiment.

**Gloucester:** Indeed. Owing to my role in Prince Ludwig's royal guard, I was able to reside in the desert once more. I bear an immense respect for these people, my king: for their tenacity, and for their unity.

**Gilbert:** Thank you, Gloucester. When such a day comes, I would have you guide its people forth.

**Gloucester:** Me? My king, I would be glad to accept, but after all I've done, I could never deserve to rule even a single town.

**Gilbert:** Then perhaps I shall entrust the matter to the nobles you mentioned prior, the same men who refused to answer your pleas.

**Gloucester:** ...

**Gilbert:** I understand you feel unprepared. But fleeing from my duty is not an option, no matter how much I may wish to. Rule this desert with the very ideals you shared with me here, and its people will surely accept you once more.

**Gloucester:** King Gilbert is rather different from his brother. Though, if any is worthy of governing our nation, it would be him.

### Gilbert and Jeremy

#### Gilbert and Jeremy - The Tavern

**Jeremy:** Ahhh! Nothin' like a good drink to keep the ol' spirits high.

**Gilbert:** Pardon me, barkeep. I'd like to sample a flagon of your finest mead, if you would.

**Jeremy:** Uh... What's a king doin' in a run-down little alehouse like this?

**Gilbert:** I have heard the fare here is quite palatable indeed. All of you march for the Liberation, yes? Then worry not. Your meals this eve shall come straight from the royal treasury.

**Gilbert:** Now let us drink to a day well won, and greater luck in the battles ahead.

**Jeremy:** Ugh. How am I supposed to relax now? One wrong word and my head'll be decoratin' the walls of Soldraga. Unless... maybe this is just the chance I've been waitin' for.

**Jeremy:** Listen, boss. This is your first time here, yeah? How 'bout I show ya how it's done?

**Gilbert:** Jeremy, was it? I would be much obliged. Thank you.

**Jeremy:** All right. But not with a knife and fork. Whaddya think this is, one of your fancy feasts?

**Gilbert:** My apologies. The barkeep was kind enough to provide utensils, so I assumed it only proper that I make good use of them.

**Jeremy:** Well, that's what ya get for assumin'. Slice that cheese any thinner, and it might as well not even exist.

**Gilbert:** Ah, our drinks. Most common folk prefer to finish them in as few gulps as possible, yes? In that case, pray for me, friends. I do this in the name of knowledge.

**Jeremy:** Ya don't gotta...

**Gilbert:** Ahh! This tavern is every word as magnificent as I had heard. Another round, barkeep!

**Jeremy:** Hey, ya might wanna take it easy, less you're lookin' forward to a poundin' headache in the mornin'.

**Gilbert:** A rightful king shall never fear the pains of tomorrow. Now come, join me, Jeremy!

**Jeremy:** Uh-oh. We got a long night ahead of us.

**Gilbert:** Ah... 'Twas truly a finer evening than I can remember.

**Jeremy:** Maybe next time I'll just slip out the back when I see him comin' in.

### Gilbert and Leah

#### Gilbert and Leah - A Dream

**Gilbert:** Tell me, Leah. How fare your efforts of late?

**Leah:** Well enough, Your Majesty. All is as calm with the princess as can be expected.

**Gilbert:** Is there anything you desire, Leah? A simple wish, a displeasure to stifle, or perhaps a dream left unfulfilled?

**Leah:** Where is this coming from, exactly?

**Gilbert:** If there is anything I can do to better your days, you need merely say so.

**Leah:** In that case, I already have what I want: to serve you and our nation for as long as I live.

**Gilbert:** Then I have no choice but to supply you with a sizable jar filled to its brim with the pickled radishes you love so dearly.

**Leah:** Please, my king. I could never accept such a lavish gift.

**Gilbert:** Yet accept it you shall. That is, unless you have another request to make of me?

**Leah:** Well, I suppose I do have one dream. I'd very much like to gaze upon a three-headed beast.

**Gilbert:** Is that so?

**Leah:** I know the idea to be a fictitious one, but they appeared in one of my favorite stories as a child.

**Gilbert:** From this day forth, I shall scour all of Fevrith for even the most tenyous mention of a three-headed beast.

**Leah:** You don't think it childish, Your Majesty?

**Gilbert:** Of course not. No dream could ever be too fanciful, for that is precisely what makes them dreams. Now, my search shall take time, but I would be glad to provide you with literature from the castle library in the meanwhile.

**Leah:** Thank you, truly.

#### Gilbert and Leah - A Smile

**Leah:** Your Majesty!

**Gilbert:** 'Tis quite unlike you to be so agitated, Leah. What is it?

**Leah:** I had never heard such peculiar anecdotes regarding three-headed beasts before.

**Gilbert:** And I have never seen you quite so relaxed, Leah.

**Leah:** Forgive me, Your Majesty. It seems as though I have forgotten my station.

**Gilbert:** 'Twas for this very reason that I offered you those books in the first place. And while I will not discount your devotion to the throne, no amount of devotion will fill your heart as happiness can.

**Leah:** But Your Majesty...

**Gilbert:** Furthermore, what hope have I of bringing joy to my people if I cannot do the same for the woman who stands beside me?

**Leah:** Even if you and I were the only souls here to witness it, the fact still remains. I betrayed our standings and disrespected you all the while.

**Gilbert:** Enough. There is nothing disrespectful about a simple smile.

**Leah:** I may not always show it, but there is no greater pleasure in life than standing in your service.

**Gilbert:** And there is no greater smile than yours.

### Gilbert and Travis

#### Gilbert and Travis - Siblings

**Gilbert:** Tell me, Travis. Why do you refuse to meet my gaze?

**Travis:** Isn't it obvious? It's because I'm embarrassed. I'm sure you remember walking in on me and Ren apologizing to each other after we took Soldraga back.

**Gilbert:** 'Tis nothing to be ashamed of. Ludwig and I embraced in a similar way, I'll have you know.

**Travis:** Guess that stuff's the same no matter what class you were born into.

**Gilbert:** Indeed. Beneath the crown and crest, a king is no different than any other man.

**Travis:** Tracking down my sister was trouble enough for me.

**Gilbert:** Yet that was no minor task, and Alain had naught but praise for the manner in which you carried it out. I am proud to call you a citizen of Drakenhold, Travis. I only pray that our relations with House Zechshelm may grow ever stronger in the days to come.

**Travis:** Sounds like we're agreed on that, at least. Same goes for Ren. I actually get the feeling she's starting to like this place again, thanks to you.

**Gilbert:** I am honored to hear that. And I hope with every ounce of my being that one day, all of our people may feel the same as her.

### Gilbert and Virginia

#### Virginia and Gilbert - Sparring

Virginia: But you proved otherwise in that last battle.

Gilbert: And I assure you, I never meant to conceal your prowess, neither from you nor anyone else.

Virginia: Oh? Then what would you say to a little sparring match?

Gilbert: I would refuse, of course.

Virginia: Come now. It will be fun.

Virginia: Not to mention the scandal you might face in failing to meet a challenge from the princess of Cornia.

Gilbert: Hrm. I suppose I've no choice, then.

Virginia: It would be endearing, if it wasn't so predictable.

Gilbert: I'm well aware of my failings, thank you.

Gilbert: Though strangely enough, I only seem to succumb to them when I'm with you.

Virginia: Oh? Do go on.

Gilbert: We've spoken long enough already. If you wish to spar, let us do it now before my next strategy meeting.

Virginia: Don't worry. I'll make sure this is over quick.

Gilbert: Just spare me the sobbing when you're soundly beaten.

Virginia: Hmph. It seems the match is yours yet again.

Gilbert: One victory in every three bouts is quite the damning proportion, Virginia.

Gilbert: Powerful though your attacks may be, you shall always struggle if you remain so blatantly ignorant of your opponent's intentions.

Gilbert: Our positions might well be reversed if only you remembered to dodge every now and again.

Virginia: Maybe so, but you can't expect me to get out of the way of everything. That's what my shields are for.

Gilbert: The same applies in battle as well. Truthfully, my blood runs cold every time I watch you charge forth alone.

Virginia: Is that why you always ask to keep me in your unit?

Virginia: Because you're worried about me?

Gilbert: What's more, I suspect I've more confidence in giving you orders than anyone in our entire army.

Virginia: Even more than Alain?

Gilbert: 'Tis not a competition, merely a matter of who is able to keep your violent inclinations in check.

Virginia: It sure sounds like a competition. You just can't resist, can you?

Gilbert: To be honest, Virginia...

Virginia: What is it?

Gilbert: Having watched you overcome such great adversity, I began to despise my own cowardice.

Gilbert: 'Twas then that I resolved never again to succumb to its grasp. To don my father's mantle and restore Drakenhold to its former brilliance.

Virginia: Am I hearing this right, Gilbert?

Virginia: Are you claiming you got your competitive edge from me?

Virginia: Heheh.

Gilbert: Why do you laugh?

Virginia: Oh, nothing. Just thinking I could go for another sparring match or two.

Gilbert: Given our shared reluctance to admit defeat, I fear this match shall never truly come to an end.

Virginia: That's fine by me.

Gilbert: Yet be warned, Virginia. This next victory shall be mine as well.

Virginia: We'll see about that.

### Gloucester and Govil

#### Govil and Gloucester - Fur and Winter Clothes

**Gloucester:** What...

**Govil:** They have got plenty of nice, warm clothes over in town.

**Gloucester:** I welcome the advice, but I often struggle to contend with the crudity of winter attire.

**Govil:** Oh yeah? You got opinions on how crude my fur is, too?

**Gloucester:** It is merely the sensation on my skin which I find disagreeable. The garment wriggled around my neck with such bristly ferocity, I could hardly sit still all evening.

**Govil:** Sounds pretty funny when you put it like that.

**Gloucester:** Ser Govil, please keep your fur at arm's length. I beg you.

**Govil:** Sorry, sorry. Could not help myself.

**Gloucester:** You have my thanks, brave wolf.

**Govil:** Sure. Do not mention it.

### Govil and Jerome

#### Govil and Jerome - Fighting Styles

**Govil:** We got a problem, old man?

**Jerome:** Ah, Ser Govil. I am afraid I do not know what you mean.

**Govil:** You should be up at the front with me, not sitting around while everyone else does all the work.

**Jerome:** Perhaps, but I thought it prudent to formulate a strategy first, rather than charge in with reckless abandon.

**Govil:** You have got some speed, too. Real shame we never see you use it.

**Jerome:** As you have stated, that does occasionally cause me to miss opportunities to strike.

**Govil:** Now you are getting it. You and me, we will be clawing at Zenoira's throat before they know what hit them.

**Jerome:** However, such as the heedless aggression you showed in our most recent battle...

**Govil:** Guess I might have gotten a little carried away, yeah.

**Jerome:** When the flames of war next lap at our feet, I shall stand beside you leading the charge.

**Govil:** That is what partners do, right?

### Govil and Yunifi

#### Yunifi and Govil - Brushing Fur

**Yunifi:** Do you do something specific to take care of it?

**Govil:** Nah, not really. I have barely even had time to groom with all the fighting we have been doing.

**Yunifi:** Huh. Well, if it is already this perfect now, just think about how much softer it will get once we brush it.

**Govil:** You are gonna brush it for me?

**Yunifi:** Oh...

**Govil:** I am not gonna go rubbing my face on your brush like a damn housecat, either. still, I know you offered out of the kindness of your heart, so at least for a bit.

**Yunifi:** Wow, really? I cannot wait!

**Govil:** Let us just do it somewhere away from camp, yeah? Think I would just about die on the spot if someone saw us.

#### Yunifi and Govil - Grandparents

**Yunifi:** Urgh. I do not think I will ever get to sleep. Wait, is that Govil? Where is he going at this time of night?

**Govil:** Grandpa. Grandma...

**Yunifi:** Govil?

**Govil:** Who is there? Oh, it is just you, Yunifi.

**Yunifi:** Are you crying?

**Govil:** Me? Not a chance in hell.

**Yunifi:** But...

**Govil:** Listen. You had better not tell anyone about this, or else.

**Yunifi:** I promise I will not. So what are you doing here, anyway?

**Govil:** What about you?

**Yunifi:** Is there a reason you are out in the middle of nowhere by yourself?

**Govil:** Fine. It is my grandparents, all right? Ever since they died, I cannot stop thinking about them.

**Yunifi:** Govil, I am sorry. I did not realize.

**Govil:** It was the happiest time I can ever remember.

**Yunifi:** You must have really loved them.

**Govil:** I did. still did not think you would catch me crying over it.

**Yunifi:** Seems like I am always finding the parts of you you never plan on sharing. Maybe you could tell me for real, then. About your grandparents, I mean.

**Govil:** Guess I do not have a choice when you put it like that. But just a few stories, okay? My grandpa used to run a tavern over in town, and one day...

### Hilda and Yunifi

#### Yunifi and Hilda - Wyverns

**Yunifi:** That is some wyvern you have there, Hilda. He is gorgeous.

**Hilda:** Oh? Especially when it comes to battle. There is no sight quite like a wyvern tearing an enemy soldier apart.

**Yunifi:** People must really love wyverns where you are from, huh?

**Hilda:** Few humans are willing to ride them, and even fewer wyverns are willing to trust us. In a sense, it was almost a stroke of fate that we met.

**Hilda:** One day, I could not stomach it any longer and ran off to the hillside where wyverns were known to nest.

**Yunifi:** You mean by yourself?

**Hilda:** Indeed. My wyvern here, the most handsome of his brood, was being viciously attacked by his very siblings. That shock soon gave way to blind rage, and I found myself foolishly attempting to intervene in the struggle.

**Hilda:** Mere moments before the creatures' claws pierced my skin, my friend here ushered me upon his back and took to the skies. After we returned home, my own harassers never dared speak ill of me again.

**Yunifi:** I never realized you had so much in common.

**Hilda:** Well, now you know. There is none I could ever trust more in all the world.

**Yunifi:** That is the kind of legend they tell every kid in Bastorias, to teach them to welcome strangers instead of fear them.

### Hodrick and Josef

#### Hodrick and Josef

Josef: Pardon the curiosity, Hodrick, but how are you feeling?

Hodrick: As you can see, I am more than capable. Nrgh.

Josef: Though their spell may be broken, we know not what ill effects it may have imparted upon your body.

Hodrick: A valid point, yes. Yet in truth, what pains me now is not some vague magickal spasm, but the wounds I received when fighting Prince Alain. In fact, I'm rather grateful. I am still impressed he managed to find a way past my armor.

Josef: As am I. Yet his prowess does not surprise me, not after years of diligent work under my tutelage.

Hodrick: 'Tis nice to see your blade has not lost its brilliance either, Josef.

Josef: For now, Hodrick, tend to your wounds. We've a long road yet to march.

#### Josef and Hodrick - Ilenia

Josef: Good eve, Hodrick. Is there something on your mind?

Hodrick: Memories, yes. Vague remembrances of that horrible day, ten years past.

Josef: Tell me, did Queen Ilenia meet a dignified end?

Hodrick: I can't remember. I was drifting on the edge of consciousness as my body bent to an unknown will. Ten years. Ten years I served as Zenoira's thrall.

Josef: If anyone should blame themselves for what happened that day, 'tis me. Valmore's declarations seemed little more than the idle ravings of a man gone mad.

Hodrick: I fear this campaign will be unlike any we have ever known.

Josef: Indeed. And the task of defending His Highness and the others rests upon our shoulders, Hodrick.

Hodrick: 'Tis one I'll not fail again. I swear it upon the man I once was, and upon Queen Ilenia herself.

### Hodrick and Lex

#### Lex and Hodrick

Hodrick: Where do you think you're going, Lex? 'Tis already past midnight.

Lex: Oh, uh... I was just gonna grab a little water. All this wandering makes a guy thirsty, y'know?

Hodrick: I know you're lying.

Lex: All right, fine. I was planning on sneaking myself an early breakfast, too.

Hodrick: How long have you been stealing off to train like this?

Lex: Urgh, caught me red-handed.

Hodrick: I applaud your dedication, I truly do, but wearing yourself too thin now will come at great cost during actual battle.

Lex: Oh, don't worry about that. I've been doing this for weeks, and no problems yet.

Hodrick: I doubt you wish to impede the prince's march due to mere lack of sleep.

Lex: Figures you're only saying this stuff 'cause of Alain.

Hodrick: You shouldn't malign him so, Lex. He only keeps you at his side because he trusts you.

Lex: Maybe I should get some sleep after all.

#### Lex and Hodrick

Lex: Yo! You mind if I ask you something, Hodrick? How'd you get that scar?

Hodrick: Years ago, I came upon two children lost in the woods, about to be carried off by a foul bandit. At the time, I preferred fabric and leather over wrought metals.

Lex: Hard to imagine that.

Hodrick: But weary as I was from constant battle, I let my guard slip a mere moment, and the bandit landed a glancing slash across my face. In the end, I cut him down, yet it was then I realized the risk I had taken in forgoing defense.

Lex: And now you and that armor are practically inseparable.

Hodrick: And now I stand an impenetrable shield, both to myself and to those I care about most. That includes you, Lex. Should danger ever approach, you need only position yourself behind me.

Lex: It's a real relief knowing I've got you backing me up!

### Hodrick and Renault

#### Hodrick and Renault - Ending

Hodrick: You filled me with the greatest pride imaginable, Alain.

Hodrick: Tell me everything you discerned from atop the royal balcony.

Hodrick: Shall we, Renault? Our work here is far from finished.

Renault: Of course. Let us be off at once.

Renault: My own atonement remains ever distant, yet know that I am eternally grateful to have played a part in our victory.

Renault: You have redeemed my life on more than one occasion now, Hodrick. I am grateful, old friend.

Hodrick: Words shall only carry us so far. Come, let us dedicate our strength to Cornia reborn.

#### Renault and Hodrick - The Name Renault

Hodrick: Renault. I see you still wield the same lance you did ten years past.

Renault: It would seem I kept it rather well maintained, even whilst serving as Zenoira's puppet.

Hodrick: Does it not call to mind painful memories every time you gaze upon it?

Renault: My pain matters not. This weapon serves as a reminder of the torturous acts I committed with my own two hands.

Renault: It is a warning, both for myself and for you.

Renault: We must always remember their suffering, for as long as we draw breath.

Hodrick: Yet dwelling on such matters will one day shatter your very soul.

Renault: And so I shall, even should it cost me everything. For my people, for my nation, and for my prince.

Hodrick: But Renault...

Renault: Enough. I have chosen the path on which I walk, yet I am ever grateful to walk it beside you.

Zenoiran Soldier: Lord Renault? Is it truly you?

Zenoiran Soldier: Have you come to brandish your lance in the name of the local garrison?

Renault: I know not who you are.

Zenoiran Soldier: Hm? But you taught me everything I know about the arts of war. Surely you must remember.

Renault: The Renault you speak of is no more.

Renault: Now begone from my sight, or be run through.

Hodrick: You seem troubled, Renault. Is everything all right?

Renault: 'Tis merely a man I encountered.

Renault: In truth, I had thought to inquire upon details of their military, but one such as he couldn't possibly know much of value.

Renault: Yet more than that...

Hodrick: Your rage took hold of you.

Hodrick: I too have been approached by a former soldier of mine. An enemy, who spoke to me with the utmost reverence and warmth.

Hodrick: 'Twas an odd feeling to hear such kind words from a man I bore no memory of.

Hodrick: The voice which met my ears was not that of an old friend, but a mere stranger who bore no memory of our time together.

Hodrick: Not only that, but upon your release from their spell, you came to us only under the guise of the wanderer Laurent.

Renault: Does it anger you, the way I cast my name aside in favor of simple anonymity?

Hodrick: Indeed it does.

Hodrick: And for me, fighting at your side is one way in which I do just that.

Renault: Thank you, Hodrick.

Renault: Though no matter what weapon I wield, I look forward to doing so at your side.

### Hodrick and Yahna

#### Yahna and Hodrick - Clothing

Hodrick: Lady Yahna, is that outfit truly suitable for travel?

Yahna: It has served me for longer than you have been alive.

Hodrick: That is precisely what concerns me.

Yahna: It is practical for a witch. Do not let the lack of armor fool you.

Hodrick: I would feel better if you allowed me to stand guard.

Yahna: Very well, Sir Hodrick. But do try not to look so worried.

#### Yahna and Hodrick - Old Sigils

Hodrick: These markings are ancient.

Yahna: Old magick sigils. Most people would have walked past without noticing.

Hodrick: I have had a long life to learn what deserves attention.

Yahna: Then help me finish tracing them.

Hodrick: Gladly.

Yahna: Careful. If you step there, you may startle the fish.

Hodrick: The fish?

Yahna: Magick has a sense of humor.

#### Hodrick and Yahna

Hodrick: Good day, Lady Yahna.

Yahna: Same to you, my little Hodrick. But tell me, is there a reason you seem so flustered?

Hodrick: Ahem. In truth, your choice of clothing is rather revealing, is it not?

Yahna: I much prefer the mobility it provides, especially compared to a bulky suit of armor like yours. They wouldn't quite suit a wizened old court sorceress, now would they?

Hodrick: In that case, I shall strive to respect your choice in attire, Lady Yahna.

Yahna: That includes you, my little Hodrick. Have you ever considered taking off all that stuffy metal for a moment?

Hodrick: The day I remove my armor is the day I fail my duty as the shield of the Liberation.

Yahna: Somehow I knew you'd say that.

#### Hodrick and Yahna - Old Mischief

Yahna: The day you unmade the magick sigil I had drawn to defend Gran Corrine from potential invaders...

Hodrick: The misfortune began when I stumbled over...

Yahna: In all my years on this earth, I've never seen a more amusing sight. I do wonder, though: what were you doing with all those fish to begin with?

Hodrick: They were for my blademaster at the time. He was a difficult man, yet I had heard he loved cats more than anything in the world.

Yahna: still, I assume any cat would have done the job, spectral or no.

Hodrick: The day's training was canceled, as you might expect, and I found myself faced with a rather lengthy suspension from duty.

Yahna: Perhaps this blademaster was a more timid man than he led you to believe.

### Ithilion and Lhinalagos

#### Ithilion and Lhinalagos - The Blade

**Lhinalagos:** Ithilion!

**Ithilion:** Please, Lhinalagos. Embrace me any tighter and you will squeeze the life out of me.

**Lhinalagos:** One who seemingly refuses to use anything but my full name now. I rather like Lhin, you know.

**Ithilion:** Enough. I am not a child anymore.

**Lhinalagos:** Yes, I can see that. Having observed you in our most recent battle, I daresay your skill with a blade surpasses even my own.

**Ithilion:** Do you really mean that?

**Lhinalagos:** You have come a long way from your days of mischief, waving twigs at any faerie who dared venture too close.

**Ithilion:** Spare me the mockery, I beg you.

**Lhinalagos:** In all seriousness, though, it seems you were right to have chosen the blade rather than the bow.

**Ithilion:** It was either that, or live in your shadow for the rest of my life. But now I can stand on my own, unmatched in my prowess with the sword. Even now, I shudder to think of the shame I would feel if Ter Eltolinde were to see you coming to my rescue.

**Lhinalagos:** Yet you have grown more than strong enough to ease such fears.

**Ithilion:** Hmph. Only because I had you teaching me.

**Lhinalagos:** All the same, I am certain Ter Rosalinde is proud indeed to have a fencer of your caliber at her side.

### Ithilion and Magellan

#### Ithilion and Magellan - The Handkerchief

**Magellan:** Hold on, pal. Think ya dropped somethin'.

**Ithilion:** Ah!

**Magellan:** Though, I dunno. This handkerchief looks kinda dainty for a stern guy like you, unless ya got it from a lady, of course.

**Ithilion:** Leave it be. I have not seen her in some time now.

**Magellan:** Yet here ya are, carryin' her stuff around like it's the most important thing in the world.

**Ithilion:** If you must know, she is a human woman who fled to these lands, a woman not subject to a life of violence and war.

**Magellan:** Well, that wasn't so hard, now was it? Me, I have never had much luck with the ladies myself. When they're not callin' me an unthinkin' oaf, they're busy claimin' I spend too much time with my sister.

**Ithilion:** I am sorry to say I can imagine both quite vividly. Now, this may sound odd coming from me, but my advice is this: once you have found someone you care for, make sure you put them before everything else.

**Magellan:** You mean even Liza?

**Magellan:** Sorry, but I am always gonna put my flesh and blood over some girl I just met.

**Ithilion:** Then you have your answer right there.

### Ithilion and Railanor

#### Ithilion and Railanor - Life, Not Death

**Ithilion:** I hear Zenoira really had their fangs in you, Railanor. I would honestly expect better from the person who put me through hell all those years in training.

**Railanor:** Were my life not dedicated to Ter Rosalinde, I would surely have taken it myself by now.

**Ithilion:** Hmph. Not even willing to fight back, are you?

**Railanor:** If it is blood you are after, Ithilion, simply cut me down and be done with it.

**Ithilion:** No. That is not why I am here. Yet you weigh yourself down with all this talk of redemption and forgiveness. It infuriates me to no end.

**Railanor:** Does it, now? That is quite the change from the days you used to spend cursing my name. It seems you are kinder at heart than you tend to let on.

**Ithilion:** Or are you truly that ready to die for the sake of your duty?

**Railanor:** Worry over me if you will, but I assure you, I am no different now than the day we met.

**Ithilion:** Then prove it. Show Ter Rosalinde how deep your devotion runs, not in death, but in life.

**Railanor:** I suppose I will.

#### Railanor and Ithilion - Composure

**Ithilion:** Forgive me for saying, Railanor, but I was watching the way you fought in that last battle.

**Railanor:** still concerned for my health, hm?

**Ithilion:** Not anymore. It was as if your blade had a mind of its own, while you yourself moved far quicker than I am frankly used to these days. Almost like the Railanor of years past stood before me, ready to scold me again for the slightest step out of line.

**Railanor:** Proving my devotion in life, not in death. Besides, what sort of instructor would I be if my old apprentice feared for my safety? I must admit, I am impressed at just how much your awareness of the battlefield has improved.

**Railanor:** In your youth, you would fly into a blind rage the very moment you drew your sword.

**Ithilion:** I learned that composure from you, you know: to let the fire burn within, while keeping my mind both calm and clear. It is the only way to protect the things that matter most.

**Railanor:** Time has certainly changed you, Ithilion.

**Ithilion:** How so?

**Railanor:** As a boy, you always used to think of your allies as little more than impediments, obstacles to overcome rather than people to cherish. That is precisely the reason you have continued to watch after me, is it not?

**Ithilion:** It was not a conscious intent, I assure you, though I cannot deny the fellowship I feel when I fight at your side. And I could not just watch as you cast your life away for nothing.

**Railanor:** Perhaps it was not time that changed you at all, but meeting Alain.

**Ithilion:** It is perplexing, to say the least.

**Railanor:** Yet it is all the more reason we must claim victory in this war, both for him and for Ter Rosalinde.

**Ithilion:** After everything we have been through together, I could expect nothing less.

### Ithilion and Rosalinde

#### Ithilion and Rosalinde - Stories

**Rosalinde:** Nice work today, Ithilion. You never cease to impress me.

**Ithilion:** Thank you, Terras. Before we head back, would you mind if I have a word?

**Rosalinde:** Oh? I am not used to getting requests from you of all people. What is it, then? A matter of the heart?

**Ithilion:** Do not be absurd.

**Rosalinde:** Too bad. Well, go on.

**Ithilion:** The tales of your travels beyond our city walls. I could not be more grateful for them.

**Rosalinde:** How could I forget? You always pretended not to pay attention, but it was obvious you were hanging onto my every word.

**Ithilion:** I did not think you had noticed.

**Rosalinde:** With the way your ears twitched in enthusiasm? It was impossible not to. In fact, I should be thanking you for providing me a peace of mind that few others can.

**Ithilion:** Your words honor me.

**Rosalinde:** You are welcome to join me, if you would like.

**Ithilion:** Me, Terras? I would be glad to. Though I cannot say I will make for the best storyteller.

**Rosalinde:** Just have confidence, and I am sure they will love it. Now come, we should not keep them waiting.

**Ithilion:** But of course.

#### Rosalinde and Ithilion - Elina

**Rosalinde:** I have to know, Ithilion. Have you spoken to Elina at all after leaving Simtukka?

**Ithilion:** That is some way to start a conversation.

**Rosalinde:** I never did expect you to fall for a human, you know, though I cannot say I do not see their appeal. still, this separation of yours is rather wasteful, do you not think? There are few things better in life than a good romance.

**Ithilion:** She simply protected me when I was running from Zenoira. That is all. And even if it were romance, the gulf between elf and human is far too large to bridge.

**Rosalinde:** No matter what prejudiced fools might try to convince you otherwise.

**Ithilion:** Enough of this, Terras. All I could ever want is for Elina to live in peace, and staying away is the only way to ensure she does so.

**Rosalinde:** Maybe you could move to her village after the war. Settle down.

**Ithilion:** And abandon my post as your personal guard? Never.

**Rosalinde:** Ithilion, please. There is more to life than duty and obligation. If you still want to serve me a hundred years from now, you will be more than welcome.

**Ithilion:** Thank you, Terras.

### Jeremy and Mordon

#### Mordon and Jeremy - An Excellent Bottle

Mordon: That is unfamiliar booze I smell.

Jeremy: You have an alarming nose.

Mordon: Share a cup.

Jeremy: No.

Mordon: One cup.

Jeremy: Fine. One.

Mordon: Smooth. Balanced. Fine quality. Another?

Jeremy: Absolutely not.

Mordon: Too late. The bottle is finished.

Jeremy: Mordon!

Mordon: I praised it properly first.

### Josef and Lex

#### Lex and Josef - Alain's Greatest Friend

Josef: It is a surprise indeed, Lex. You have grown far quicker than I had previously thought possible.
