Lex: Yeah, maybe. But I am still nothing compared to Alain.

Josef: Such was the case with his mother before him, and her father before her.

Lex: Did not realize it ran in the family.

Lex: Can I ask you something, Josef? Why did you ever agree to start teaching me, all those years ago? For all you knew, I was just the kid of some local fisherman.

Josef: You are His Highness's greatest friend, Lex. The one he trusts above all others.

Lex: That is kind of hard to believe. Even you? Not sure he would pick a fool like me over any of them.

Josef: You have been that friend to him for many years. All I ask is that you continue to do so.

Lex: You are going to make a guy blush when you put it like that. But trust me, you did not even have to ask.

Josef: I merely thought to return your ample sincerity in kind.

#### Lex and Josef - After the War

Josef: Lex? What are you doing out here?

Lex: Thinking about what I am going to do once this war is finally over.

Lex: Alain will be busy being king, and I doubt he will want to keep me hanging around the place either.

Josef: As one of His Highness's most loyal retainers, you shall surely be able to come and go as you please.

Lex: Not a chance. A guy like me just cannot cut it with all those stuffy noble types.

Josef: Is that truly what you think? Then imagine yourself in His Highness's position.

Josef: What would you wish for your dearest friend upon taking the throne?

Lex: Well, I...

Josef: Do you understand now? That distance is merely one of your own creation.

Lex: You are probably right. But knowing the problem is only half the battle. I have still got to figure out what to do about it.

Josef: Simply do whatever you feel is right, and that shall be enough. Such is the ironclad bond you and His Highness share.

Lex: Thanks, Josef.

Lex: But that is enough pouting for one day. There will be plenty of time to think about this stuff after we beat Galerius.

Josef: Whichever path they choose to walk, their bond shall endure forevermore.

### Josef and Miriam

#### Miriam and Josef - Knights of the Rose

Miriam: All matters considered, I should never have let her take flight to begin with.

Josef: At ease, Miriam. In such a state, none could have possibly hoped to stop her.

Josef: On the contrary, I owe you a debt of gratitude for standing as her shield when few others would bear such courage.

Miriam: Even still, I struggle to come to terms with the hardship I caused our army.

Josef: You wished to finally have vengeance for the cruel decimation of your order.

Miriam: You have the right of it, yes.

Miriam: For as long as our hearts beat in our chests, the Knights of the Rose shall ever bleed for the princess.

Miriam: They were always ready to lay down their lives for the sake of duty. And so they did.

Miriam: In sooth, the events of our battle here come as something of a relief.

Miriam: Not only did I fulfill my duty as a Knight of the Rose, but we struck Ciethe down and avenged my fallen sisters in the process.

Josef: Queen Ilenia surely looks upon you with great pride.

Miriam: Thank you, Ser Josef.

### Josef and Renault

#### Renault and Josef - Jousting Memory

Josef: At long last, you've found the conviction to join our march.

Renault: Ah, Ser Josef.

Josef: Yet the thrust of your lance soon made your identity clear as the evening sky.

Renault: Was it truly that obvious?

Renault: I had hoped to slay Renault so that Laurent might live, but it seems my efforts were to little avail.

Josef: Though despite your failings, you live on, striving for a greater future.

Renault: As I've sworn to do in the Liberation's name, yes.

Josef: If I recall, such skill once earned you top honor in a jousting competition held by the Ashen Blue.

Renault: 'Tis a fond memory indeed, yes.

Josef: I only pray the point of your lance is as sharp as ever.

Renault: But of course, Ser Josef.

Renault: And with it, I shall pierce the heart of Galerius's foul ambitions.

### Josef and Scarlett

#### Scarlett and Josef

Scarlett: He was a friend of yours, yes?

Josef: Indeed. A former knight, and a rather defiant one at that. I never thought he would trade his blade for the sacred vestments.

Scarlett: I learned a great deal from him, you know. He was always such a large presence in my life. Kind, of course, but intimidating at times.

Josef: It seems he was blessed with a far greater student than he deserved.

Scarlett: He also told me lots of stories about when you were young.

Josef: What?

Scarlett: How you always used to challenge anyone who could hold a sword to a duel.

Scarlett: Or the way you would hold drinking contests when you ran out of gold, then make the loser pay for your lodging.

Josef: Well...

Scarlett: He said the man tried to have your head for it, but the two of you stormed his stronghold and decimated his entire band instead. He always seemed to enjoy sharing those stories, too.

Josef: Yes, I imagine he would.

Scarlett: Oh, come now. Though it was still a surprise to hear you were such a little troublemaker. Hehe!

Josef: What right did that scoundrel of a priest have to reveal such humiliating details?

### Josef and Selvie

#### Selvie and Josef - Duties

Josef: A word, Selvie.

Josef: Such tardiness impacts not only yourself, but the lasting morale of our entire army.

Selvie: There is only so much time I have for my work, and I do not enjoy being pulled away from it.

Josef: While you march as a member of the Liberation Army, you have no choice but to follow His Highness's every order.

Selvie: I suppose so. I cannot deny how much he has done for me.

Selvie: I will try to improve, for his sake.

Josef: Do you, now?

Selvie: At times I have wondered if my lack of offensive magick was a burden to the army.

Josef: And I, for one, put great stock in your strengths. If only you would do the same.

Selvie: Thank you for saying so, Josef.

Josef: All I ask in return is that you perform your duties with the utmost care.

Josef: Speaking of which, I trust you have not forgotten our upcoming battle.

Selvie: Of course not. I could never.

Josef: Somehow I struggle to believe you. Very well, let us depart together.

### Josef and Tatiana

#### Josef and Tatiana

Tatiana: Your quill, your notebook, your gloves, a small pouch, an old button, a pendant you received from your wife... If I could only hear you speak of them again, but one more time.

Josef: How has your faith in him continued to hold true, despite everything you witnessed under his command?

Tatiana: You ask that as though telling you will make any difference.

Josef: Forgive me. I didn't intend to speak of him so coldly.

Tatiana: Now you pretend to care, hm? Fine, then, I'll tell you. It was at the gates of that settlement that Lord Ghislain saved my life.

Josef: And thus, you chose to serve him in order to repay that debt. Yet were the victims of his experiments not innocent civilians like your sisters? How could you ever support such research?

Tatiana: "Once I'm gone, use my body however you must. Find a cure, and deliver our lands from the curse which blights them." At first, he refused, as any loving husband would. But after much internal strife, he tearfully did as she asked, even enlisting the help of that horrid necromancer to do so. We have repelled the plague and the horrors of its reality, and for now, that is enough.

Josef: Despite his methods, it's clear to me that your lord acted with naught but the utmost conviction. Pray, forgive this old soldier his ignorance. And please, do what you must to honor Ghislain's memory.

Tatiana: I will.

### Josef and Travis

#### Josef and Travis

Travis: Hmph. Should've known it wouldn't be that easy.

Josef: How went the negotiations, Travis?

Travis: With the world we're living in, no merc worth their salt will ever join us on the cheap. The tougher they are, the more they're gonna cost us, and not a one of them's willing to cut a deal. Sorry I couldn't be much help.

Josef: Not only are you the finest scout in all of Cornia, but a steady hand in even the most trying of times.

Travis: Well, I'm glad to hear you say so.

Josef: Let us return to this venture at another time.

Travis: Right. I'll hold off on any further negotiations until then.

Josef: You have my thanks, Travis. I'm certain you shall see this through soon enough.

#### Josef and Travis - Rest

Josef: Have you ever considered resting a moment, Travis?

Travis: Who, me? I'm fine.

Josef: You'll not be "fine" if your exhaustion gets you captured by the enemy.

Travis: Maybe I wouldn't mind letting someone else handle things for today.

Josef: At times, it seems you care more about making a strong impression than looking after your own health.

Travis: I'm glad I had someone like you watching out for me.

Josef: 'Twas the only way I could be certain you weren't a mere spy for Zenoira.

Travis: That just makes me even more thankful you decided to let me stick around.

Josef: We would have been fools not to. Your talent is an indispensable part of the Liberation's cause, Travis. We've a long road to walk until that day, of course, yet I pray you continue to assist him for years to come.

Travis: Easy there, Josef. You don't need to grovel.

Josef: Ah, forgive me. I should be going now.

Travis: Looks like I've got plenty more work ahead of me.

### Josef and Virginia

#### Josef and Virginia

Virginia: I have to wonder, how did he fare after fleeing Cornia?

Josef: He scarcely ate one meal a day, and neither study nor swordwork could hold his interest. Yet over time, he made friends on the island. They trained together, learned together, and reveled together in the carefree way only children can. Before I knew it, a smile had gradually returned to his face.

Virginia: Even now, they're practically inseparable when we're not in battle.

Josef: Even if I had tried, I doubt I could have ever healed his broken heart the way they have. From what I could gather, he feared he may never see you again. I thank the Father above for reuniting you after all this time.

Virginia: Heh. Maybe I should try a little harder to connect with him, then.

#### Virginia and Josef - Ilenia's Garden

Virginia: I have to wonder, how did he fare after fleeing Cornia?

Josef: He scarcely ate one meal a day, and neither study nor swordwork could hold his interest.

Josef: Yet over time, he made friends on the island. They trained together, learned together, and reveled together in the carefree way only children can.

Josef: Before I knew it, a smile had gradually returned to his face.

Virginia: It's good to see he's found people he cares about.

Virginia: Even now, they're practically inseparable when we're not in battle.

Josef: Even if I were able, I doubt I could have ever healed his broken heart the way they have.

Josef: From what I could gather, he feared he may never see you again.

Virginia: Really, now?

Josef: I thank the Father above for reuniting you after all this time.

Virginia: Maybe I should try a little harder to connect with him, then.

Josef: Our journeys here, infrequent as they were, surely provided Queen Ilenia with the respite she so dearly needed.

Josef: It wasn't often she eased her royal countenance, but here she would smile as if nothing could ever trouble her again.

Virginia: I hadn't realized this place held such meaning to her.

Josef: Is that you, my queen?

Virginia: Is everything all right, Josef?

Josef: In all honesty, no. For a moment, you appeared to mine eye as Queen Ilenia herself.

Josef: And here you stand, regal and dignified as she once did all those years ago.

Virginia: You honor me with the comparison, Josef.

Virginia: All this talk has brought back memories.

Josef: Of what, I might ask?

Virginia: When Alain and I were young, we spent much of our time playing in the garden at Gran Corrine.

Virginia: I can still remember the feeling of her hand caressing my cheek. The warmth, and the love.

Virginia: All my life, I've tried to follow in her footsteps.

Virginia: To one day be every bit as strong and gentle a woman as she once was.

Virginia: Say, Josef? I can't thank you enough for bringing me here.

### Josef and Yahna

#### Josef and Yahna

Yahna: I had always believed you made it out alive, but it's still a shock to see you actually standing here in the flesh. And a personal advisor to the prince, no less.

Josef: It has been far too long, Lady Yahna.

Yahna: Why the formality, Josef? Is it uncomfortable, having an ally who knew you when you were just a child?

Josef: It is indeed, especially given the endless trouble my younger self made for you.

Yahna: I remember it well, even after all these years. Or the time you hid in one of the suits of armor which lined the halls, just so you could jump out and scare me as I walked by. This was all before you'd become a squire, of course.

Josef: Even still...

Yahna: Between you and Hodrick, we had no shortage of troublemakers roaming the castle during King Gerard's reign. If nothing else, at least the two of you kept things interesting.

Josef: 'Tis a relief to hear you say so, yet I must ask that you never speak a word of these matters to anyone else.

Yahna: All that mischief you used to get into, yet here you are having raised the prince into a respectable young man.

Josef: I deserve no credit, Yahna. Such character is in his very nature, and any other growth owes to the friends he made while living on Palevia.

Yahna: Or the time you've spent bringing joy back into that lonely child's life.

#### Yahna and Josef - Childhood Mischief

Josef: You have not changed as much as you pretend, Yahna.

Yahna: And you have become terribly fond of sounding old, Josef.

Josef: Someone had to become responsible.

Yahna: You were no such thing as a child.

Josef: I recall you were not exactly innocent yourself.

Yahna: Perhaps. But my mischief had better planning.

Josef: And more magick.

Yahna: Naturally.

### Kitra and Liza

### Kitra and Miriam

#### Miriam and Kitra - Hot Springs

Kitra: Those hot springs felt great, huh?

Miriam: Had you not convinced me to join you, I surely would not feel this rejuvenated.

Miriam: I tend to grow cold rather easily, as you know, and this proved a wonderful way to combat the ever-present chill of Bastorias.

Kitra: Maybe next time we can bring Fran and the princess, too.

Kitra: Hey, Miriam? You want to grab a bite in town before we head back to camp?

Miriam: It would seem I have no choice.

Kitra: You are the best, Miriam.

Miriam: That was unlike any stew I have ever eaten, yes.

Kitra: Guess it is about time we head back to camp.

Miriam: I must say, Kitra, this only goes to show there are few things in life more important than proper relaxation with a good friend.

Kitra: That is what I have been trying to tell you. I think you were always too strict to realize it.

Miriam: Perhaps so.

Kitra: It is the only way to really relax at the end of a long day, if you ask me.

Miriam: Are you suggesting that for my benefit, or purely for your own?

Kitra: That obvious, huh?

Miriam: As plain as the midday sun.

#### Kitra and Miriam - A Cold

Kitra: It is just a sneeze.

Miriam: So you do have a cold. I could recognize a sneeze like that anywhere.

Miriam: It would seem you have caused quite the commotion of late. I fully expect an explanation once you have recovered from your ailments.

Miriam: We shall postpone this conversation until then.

### Kitra and Mordon

#### Mordon and Kitra - Stonework

Mordon: Fine stone in that statue.

Mordon: A craftsman ought to know good material when he sees it.

Kitra: Huh. I did not expect that from you.

Mordon: From an old drunk, you mean?

Kitra: I did not say old.

Mordon: You implied it loudly.

Kitra: It reminds me of my old hammer, actually.

Mordon: Then you have good taste in tools.

#### Mordon and Kitra - Uncle Mordon

Child: Uncle Mordon, your belly is big.

Mordon: That is because I am full of wisdom.

Kitra: Feels more like an old wine barrel.

Mordon: Must everyone poke me today?

Kitra: Why is it so big? Too much drinking?

Mordon: Then perhaps I should ease up a little. For them.

Kitra: Good. I will tell them they won.

#### Mordon and Kitra - A Finished Bridge

Kitra: Really?

Kitra: When I was little, I fixed something and someone complimented me. I think I have been chasing that feeling ever since.

Mordon: Aye. I understand that.

Kitra: You do?

Mordon: Of course. Come here and I will show you a few pointers for next time.

#### Kitra and Mordon - Stonework

Mordon: Mighty fine statue they have got here.

Kitra: Mordon? I did not think you would be into this kind of stuff.

Mordon: I was just admiring the quality of the stone.

Kitra: It looks the same as any other statue to me.

Mordon: The only reason it has held up this well is the material it was built out of.

Kitra: You can tell that just from looking?

Mordon: At least once the paint is all worn off like this.

Kitra: So what kind of stone did they use for this?

Mordon: Tough stuff. It must have been hard carving it up in this much detail.

Kitra: Now I have to wonder about my old hammer.

Mordon: That is why you see stone like this in all sorts of buildings and everyday tools.

Kitra: Especially from an old drunk.

Mordon: Did you really have to put it like that?

#### Kitra and Mordon - Uncle Mordon

Boy: Poke, poke.

Girl: Your belly is so big.

Town Girl: Kids! Time to go.

Girl: Come play with us again, Uncle Mordon.

Mordon: Like you even have to ask. I will be back before you know it.

Kitra: Poke, poke.

Mordon: What do you think you are doing?

Kitra: Giving this old wine barrel a little nudge.

Mordon: You have got some nerve.

Kitra: Why are you so big, anyway? Probably all the drinking, right?

Mordon: It is none of your business.

Kitra: Guess not. But too much booze will make you sick.

Mordon: Preach all you want. I am not giving it up.

Kitra: Imagine how those kids will feel if their Uncle Mordon drinks himself to an early grave.

Mordon: Hmph.

Kitra: Take care of yourself, okay?

Mordon: Suppose I would not mind easing up for them.

#### Kitra and Mordon - The Bridge

Kitra: There. That should do it.

Mordon: What are you up to, Kitra?

Kitra: They needed a hand fixing the bridge, so I handled it.

Mordon: You did it yourself instead of coming to me?

Mordon: Let us see here. You know, this is actually some pretty fine work.

Kitra: One day back when I was a kid, I got asked to fix something.

Kitra: I can still remember how good it felt finishing the job, and getting complimented for it.

Kitra: So I kept chasing that feeling. Learned as much as I could and helped fix things whenever I had the chance.

Kitra: Working on this bridge helped remind me how much I like building things.

Mordon: Turns out we are more similar than I thought.

Kitra: Huh?

Mordon: Your work is good, Kitra. At least for someone just getting started.

Mordon: If you want a couple pointers, I would be glad to teach you a thing or two you can improve on.

Kitra: You really mean that? I am sure it will be perfect by the time you are done showing me the ropes.

Mordon: Good to see you excited about it. Now look here. If you want a stronger foundation, all you have to do is...

### Kitra and Sharon

#### Sharon and Kitra - The Knight with a Hammer

Kitra: I am just getting them moving. They will not cross otherwise.

Kitra: With a hammer.

Sharon: You are every ounce the knight they wished for, and more.

#### Kitra and Sharon - Helping Animals

Kitra: My parents never came around to it, though. Kept trying to get me to ride a horse like a proper knight.

Sharon: A familiar struggle.

Sharon: But in my eyes, Kitra, you are every ounce the knight they wished you would become, and much more.

### Leah and Virginia

#### Virginia and Leah - Market

Leah: Are you certain you wish to join me, your ladyship? I'd think such markets to be rather beneath you.

Virginia: You're always following my every move, so it's only fair we do what you want now and then.

Leah: As long as you remain where I can see you, I'll not protest any further.

Virginia: I'm not your child, Leah. Now, lead the way.

Leah: Very well. Ah, look here. What a cute little sculpture.

Virginia: Never thought I'd see the day you called something "cute." Let me see it.

Virginia: Oh.

Virginia: Have you lost your mind, Leah? Where would you even put such a thing?

Leah: Beside my pillow, of course. That way, I could see it every morning when I wake up.

Virginia: Hmph. If it were me, I think the beast would just give me nightmares.

Virginia: But don't let my preferences stop you from buying what you want. Go on.

Virginia: Leah is always so willing to do anything I ask of her, but I wonder if there's a limit to how far she'll go.

Virginia: Perhaps I'll put that to a little test.

Virginia: Oh, Leah? I just had a sudden craving for fish and was hoping I might catch and cook one for myself.

Leah: Gladly, your ladyship, as long as we stay within relative proximity to the fort.

Virginia: Then come, we have a Cornian trout to hook.

Virginia: And once we've returned with our quarry, we can roast it whole for a nice, hearty meal.

Leah: I shall summon one of our hunters at once and prepare our packs for the journey.

Virginia: I, erm... thank you. I look forward to it.

Virginia: Tell me something, Leah. Why do you not flinch in the face of my exorbitant demands?

Leah: I'm not certain what you mean. I've grown quite accustomed to your whims over the years, and today's requests are no different.

Virginia: Are you saying I'm always this unreasonable?

Leah: In light of that truth, nothing you ask could be too excessive.

Leah: Yet I admit, there have been some occasions where I felt you overstepped your welcome.

Virginia: Oh yeah?

Leah: And one which makes me forever proud to serve at your side, my princess.

Virginia: That's how you feel, is it?

Virginia: I would rather turn to no one else than you, Leah.

Leah: Thank you, your ladyship. Though do keep them within reason, would you?

### Lex and Railanor

#### Railanor and Lex - Elven Fencers

**Lex:** There is a reason elves dress like that, right?

**Railanor:** There is. The fae who grant us their blessings despise apparel made of iron and steel, so we dress ourselves in as little of it as possible.

**Lex:** But doesn't that mean you get hurt more easily?

**Railanor:** If the enemy is able to hit us, yes. But fencers such as I prefer to evade attacks rather than guard them. As mentioned before, the fae can bestow upon us the protection of the wind.

**Lex:** Whoa.

**Railanor:** In battles between fellow elves, arrows are the greatest threat to our safety. Yet the wind's protection allows us to nullify their strength and close great distances in the blink of an eye.

**Lex:** Hey!

**Railanor:** Even still, this manner of combat poses quite a substantial problem, one which became all too apparent when Zenoira's armor-clad forces overran our nation. Try as we could, none of our usual tactics were able to surmount their defenses.

**Railanor:** You would do well to make use of such a valuable trait.

**Lex:** Huh. And here I could have sworn they just liked how it looked.

### Lex and Selvie

Selvie: You mean for aesthetics rather than functionality?

Selvie: Such a simple hypothesis, yet I find it difficult to refute its conclusion.

Lex: Selvie?

Selvie: Perhaps what I thought to be magick runes on this wall are simply the idle scrawlings of an unburdened youth.

Lex: Snap out of it, Selvie.

Selvie: Apologies. I seem to have grown lost in concentration.

Lex: How about I stick around and watch your back? You can focus on your history business in peace.

Selvie: You would truly do that for me?

Lex: Sure would, as long as you tell me about all the stuff you find.

### Magellan and Rosalinde

**Rosalinde:** Again you surprise me, Magellan. It seems you are quite the poet.

**Rosalinde:** The majority of elves favor the rays of the midday sun, though it does vary from elf to elf, of course.

**Magellan:** Huh. Doesn't that mean ya should be doin' this at night, then?

**Rosalinde:** There is nothing quite like standing in the warmth of the sun, either.

**Magellan:** I hear ya. It all comes down to wantin' somethin' ya can't usually get. That's enough of this damn heat. I'm headin' back to town for a nice, freezin' sharbat. Have fun out here with your faeries and all.

**Rosalinde:** Hm. That does sound rather refreshing. Let us just hope he has enough gold for the both of us.

### Mandrin and Rolf

#### Mandrin and Rolf - A Friend's Burden

**Rolf:** A word, Mandrin.

**Mandrin:** What do you need?

**Rolf:** I hear rumors you have spent much of your life consorting with the bandit Gammel.

**Mandrin:** That's the truth, yep.

**Rolf:** Why aid him in his cruelty, rather than convince him to amend his ways?

**Mandrin:** There was no changing his mind, not with what he was doing it for. So I did the only thing I could. Nobody else made that choice for me. I did. After all, there's nothing lower than a damn thief.

**Rolf:** But Mandrin...

**Mandrin:** No buts. I was a fool, and I know it. I have got no excuse for not pushing Gammel harder, for not trying to find another way, even if it meant him turning on me.

**Mandrin:** Whatever it takes, so long as he doesn't have to suffer alone.

**Rolf:** You would really do all that for a mere friend?

**Mandrin:** I will be returning that favor for the rest of my life.

**Rolf:** You are a better friend than a bastard like him deserves.

#### Rolf and Mandrin - A Friend's Choice

Rolf: You chose to share his burden.

Mandrin: The choice was mine. I will spend the rest of my life returning the favor, so he does not have to suffer alone.

Rolf: You are a better friend than Gammel deserves.

Mandrin: Maybe. But he is still my friend.

### Melisandre and Monica

Melisandre: I am glad to see your hair is just as radiant a gold as always.

Monica: You have remained much the same as well, Melisandre.

Melisandre: How do you mean?

Monica: While you may have struggled with decorum at times, you bore a keen eye for seeing matters as they truly were.

Melisandre: Did I?

Monica: A thief found his way into the manor proper, past every last one of our skillful sentries.

Monica: At the time, it seemed as though you were simply infatuated with him. Somehow, you had suspected the man from the very beginning.

Melisandre: I cannot say I remember it myself.

Melisandre: Though I welcome the praise, we both know what happened afterward. I sided with Zenoira rather than defend my home.

Melisandre: So please, do not act like I am some wonderful judge of character.

### Melisandre and Sanatio

#### Melisandre and Sanatio - Courtship Advice

Sanatio: It is here I shall take my leave, O savior.

Alain: Of course. You have my thanks, Sanatio.

Melisandre: Grr.

Sanatio: Might I help you with something, Lady Melisandre?

Melisandre: You can, actually. I have noticed you have been spending a lot of time with Alain lately.

Melisandre: If you are going to follow him around, at least have the decency not to look so miserable while you do it.

Sanatio: You think my countenance is miserable, my lady?

Melisandre: It is not your face that is the problem. It is your attitude.

Melisandre: Keep it up and you will soon find yourself all alone without a single friend in the world.

Sanatio: If such is my fate, then so be it. None shall ever sway me from my sacred path again, even if I must walk it alone.

Melisandre: You are just as unsociable as I thought. Maybe that would change if you fell in love.

Sanatio: Pardon?

Melisandre: Fine, then I will instruct you in the time-tested courtship rituals of House Meillet.

Sanatio: I never asked for your tutelage, nor is a sinner such as I deserving of the charity.

Melisandre: I am sure no one would fault you for finding a soulmate to share your burdens with.

Sanatio: Tell me, what is the reason for this sudden concern?

Melisandre: Is it not obvious? If you turned your gaze to someone else, I would have Alain all to myself again.

Sanatio: I suspected as much. You are nothing if not stubborn, my lady.

Melisandre: Say what you will. Now, as for the courtship ritual...

Sanatio: I fear I will have to decline the offer.

Melisandre: Get back here.

Sanatio: I will do no such thing. Before I go, I have to wonder: have any of these techniques proven effective with our savior?

Melisandre: Well, Alain is rather impervious to my advances, but...

Melisandre: At least let me finish my sentence before you go running off.

### Melisandre and Scarlett

#### Melisandre and Scarlett - Shopping Competition

Melisandre: Here we are, then. Are you ready to begin?

Scarlett: Do we really have to do this, Melisandre?

Melisandre: I am sorry to say we do.

Melisandre: Today we learn who can fashion the ensemble Alain likes best.

Melisandre: It is strange, Scarlett. Despite the competition, I rather enjoyed shopping with you.

Scarlett: As did I. Let us do it again sometime, but maybe as friends instead of enemies.

### Miriam and Selvie

#### Miriam and Selvie - Speaking to Horses

Miriam: Yes, I see. How truly wonderful.

Selvie: Pardon the question, Miriam, but who exactly are you speaking to?

Selvie: There does not seem to be anyone else here, except the spirits of the dead.

Miriam: Please, it is nothing as fanciful as that. I was merely conversing with my loyal steed.

Selvie: You mean to imply you speak the tongues of beasts?

Miriam: Not directly. It is more of a vague understanding I have acquired from her various sounds and behaviors.

Miriam: If you extol their beauty every now and again, they grow more vibrant than you could ever imagine.

Miriam: On the other hand, speaking ill of them shall cause them to wilt and wallow in despair.

Selvie: Fascinating. I thought such effects applied only to human children.

Miriam: Hence, I always address her with all the warmth and kindness I can muster.

Selvie: I wonder if flattering a patch of ruins would produce similar results.

Miriam: Perhaps you could slow their deterioration, or even unearth an ancient artifact with relative ease.

Selvie: I will have to test this theory at my soonest convenience.

### Miriam and Virginia

#### Virginia and Miriam - Armor in the Heat

Virginia: Is everything all right, Miriam?

Miriam: Yes, 'tis no problem at all, Princess.

Virginia: You say that, but then why do you look like you're about to faint?

Virginia: Have you considered maybe taking some of your armor off, just to cool down for a minute?

Miriam: This armor is a symbol of my devotion to our order, and I shall never remove it in the line of duty.

Virginia: Very well. Consider this an order from your princess, Miriam.

Virginia: Take it off this instant.

Miriam: As you wish, my lady.

Virginia: That's more like it. Trust me, it's for your own good.

Alain: Perhaps it's best I steer clear of the situation.

### Monica and Nina

#### Nina and Monica - Painting for Mille

Nina: I have a feeling Mille is going to love this.

Monica: What are you painting, Nina?

Nina: A picture of a flower to send my family.

Monica: Do you write home like this often?

Nina: The picture is for Mille. She has always adored my little artworks.

Monica: I take it you enjoy the hobby yourself, then?

Nina: I suppose I have never really thought about it. I only ever learned it for the sake of my schooling.

Monica: If I could paint even half as well as you, I would gladly retire my sword in favor of a brush.

Nina: I appreciate you saying so. Did you not study the arts as well? I thought such things were tradition at just about every noble house in the land.

Monica: I did indeed. I would be glad to draw something for you, if you would like.

Nina: Of course. Here, I have plenty of paper left.

Nina: Hm. What is it meant to be, exactly?

Monica: It does not resemble the bird at all. Even I know that to be true.

Nina: I would have guessed a savage beast, or perhaps a building that has fallen into disrepair.

Monica: That is something of an overreaction to a mere lack of talent, would you not say?

Nina: I do not know. The more I look at it, the more I am starting to understand how they felt.

### Monica and Ramona

#### Ramona and Monica - Love Potions

**Monica:** Have you heard the rumors, Ramona? They say a local witch is selling hand-crafted love potions in that town over there.

**Ramona:** Oh? I had not realized you take interest in such frivolous topics.

**Monica:** If anything, I fear this "potion" conceals a tonic with a more wicked purpose than we are led to believe.

**Ramona:** Perhaps we should take a moment to investigate.

**Monica:** I would very much appreciate that.

**Ramona:** It does not, however, produce feelings of love for another.

**Monica:** Should the potion truly yield such fierce emotions, perhaps it is not as deceitful as first thought.

**Ramona:** Do you speak from experience, Monica?

**Monica:** Though I cannot say it ever came from a drink in my case.

**Ramona:** And what if the potion did as it claimed? Would you have used it?

**Monica:** A vow of love spoken through unsober words would always ring hollow compared to one from the heart.

**Ramona:** Perhaps so. Genuine affection must come from a place of mutual understanding, not heightened moods and garish tinctures.

**Monica:** Heheh. Well said, Ramona.

### Monica and Selvie

#### Selvie and Monica - A Passion for Research

Monica: What happened, Selvie? You look utterly exhausted.

Selvie: Is that you, Monica? I require nourishment.

Monica: And you shall have it. Stay strong while I fetch you some food.

Selvie: Thank you again, Monica. At times I grow so absorbed in my research that I forget to eat for an entire day.

Monica: I cannot help but admire your single-minded devotion to knowledge.

Monica: I admire your motivation, Selvie. I could never find the energy to spur myself on as you have.

Selvie: My research is the only pleasure I know in life.

Selvie: Surely you have other joys which drive you forth, joys beyond the pursuit of scholarship.

Monica: My instructors shunned such fanciful hobbies and urged me ever toward the noble and sublime.

Selvie: How very callous of them.

Selvie: I simply found where my curiosity lay and chose to pledge my life to its calling. That is all.

Monica: I hope to do the same as you someday.

Selvie: I am sure you will, Monica, and I cannot wait to see where your passion leads you.

### Morard and Ramona

#### Ramona and Morard - Armor

**Morard:** Ramona!

**Ramona:** Is there a problem, Morard?

**Morard:** No, it is nothing.

**Ramona:** It does not appear to be nothing. The laces holding your armor together are frayed beyond belief.

**Morard:** To be honest, I was hoping to find someone who might be able to mend them. I would do it myself, of course, but there is not much craft in hands like these.

**Ramona:** Just give me a moment and I will have it handled.

**Morard:** I cannot possibly ask that of you, given all the time you spend laboring through war councils. But...

**Ramona:** You know there is nothing to worry about, Morard.

**Morard:** Very well. Thank you, Ramona.

**Ramona:** I am glad to do it. Now stay right here. I will have your armor back to its former glory in no time.

**Ramona:** All done, Morard. I also noticed an alarming lack of decoration, so I added a touch of embroidery to the leather as well. A lion, of course, to match your ferocious image.

**Morard:** You what? Thank you, that is. I appreciate the help, Ramona.

**Ramona:** As always, simply let me know if you need any further assistance.

**Morard:** Ramona is a wonderful seamstress, I cannot deny that, but she always has to add something extra to all of her work. Yet although this lion is a little too cute for me, I will be proud to wear it, just like everything else she has made.

#### Ramona and Morard - Family

**Ramona:** I am relieved to see my worries were unfounded.

**Morard:** That is actually exactly what I was planning to do. I thought an old soldier like me did not have any right to stay here.

**Morard:** Even as Zenoira's cold dominion pushed farther and farther into our lands, the warmth of our bond never faded. You, humming proudly as you embroidered my armor with decorations more fitting for a young boy than a grown man...

**Morard:** No matter how much I wanted to cast that life aside, I could never bring myself to do it.

**Ramona:** I would have been furious if you had abandoned us without so much as a single word. Yet I wonder, is there not another family waiting for you out there? A human family?

**Morard:** I think that explains the comfort I have felt in my life here in Bastorias.

**Ramona:** Ah.

**Morard:** Every time, it ends with me in tears, struggling to bear such powerful emotion. You and Yunifi are the greatest family I could ever ask for.

### Morard and Yunifi

#### Yunifi and Morard - Childhood

**Yunifi:** It is funny, Morard. You are doing just fine now, but I can still remember a time you were the clumsiest bestral in all of Bastorias.

**Morard:** Even simple tasks like eating a meal or changing my clothes took far longer than they ever should have.

**Yunifi:** You would always try to sit in one that was way too small for you, then fall straight out of it a few minutes later.

**Morard:** You were not so normal yourself, you know. Most of your time as a child was spent climbing trees and roaring at passersby.

**Yunifi:** Guess so, huh? It is almost like I was better at being a bestral than you were.

**Morard:** If only you had been good at coming home on time, too. You worried Ramona half to death on more than one occasion.

**Yunifi:** I must have been a real handful for her.

**Morard:** We should find a moment to thank Ramona for everything she has done for us, whenever we have time to spare.

**Yunifi:** Ooh, I like the sound of that. Let us take her out for dinner, then, and maybe get some presents, too.

**Morard:** Yes. I am sure she will enjoy that very much.

**Ramona:** It has been some time indeed since the three of us last dined like this, but I pray we can do it again sooner rather than later.

**Yunifi:** You think she was happy with that?

**Morard:** Think? I am sure she was.

**Yunifi:** Seeing how much Ramona was enjoying it, I honestly could not help but smile too.

**Morard:** Indeed. It was one of the finest days I can ever remember.

#### Yunifi and Morard - Mittens

**Yunifi:** Do you not think it is a little colder than usual today?

**Morard:** Not particularly, no. Have you come down with a fever, Yunifi? Let me feel your forehead. Hm. Your body temperature seems to be normal, but your hands are practically frozen solid.

**Yunifi:** Speaking of hands, I actually have a present for you, Morard.

**Morard:** You do? What magnificent mittens.

**Yunifi:** Sorry about earlier. I only asked if you were cold because I was not sure how to bring it up.

**Morard:** Do not apologize, Yunifi. The truth is, I bought you a pair of mittens as well.

**Yunifi:** And they are even the same style as the ones I got you, just a lot smaller!

**Morard:** My comment about your hands was the best attempt I could make.

**Yunifi:** Heheh! Here I thought this kind of stuff only happens in faerie tales.

**Morard:** Thank you, Yunifi. I will think of you every time I put them on.

**Yunifi:** Same here. Coincidence or not, I am glad we get to match now.

**Morard:** Though I imagine Ramona would feel left out without mittens of her own.

**Yunifi:** That is an easy problem to solve. Let us buy her some!

**Morard:** Yes, let us.

**Yunifi:** I cannot wait to see the look on her face when we give them to her.

### Mordon and Rolf

#### Rolf and Mordon - Morning Practice

Mordon: Come now, Rolf. One cup of wine before bed never hurt anyone.

Rolf: I turn in early. First I check my equipment, then I sleep, then I practice archery at dawn.

Mordon: Dawn? That sounds like punishment.

Rolf: You may join me if you wish. It may do you good.

Mordon: I will pass.

Rolf: As you like.

Mordon: Wait. You were serious?

Rolf: The morning breeze is pleasant, is it not?

Mordon: Pleasant? I can barely stand.

### Nina and Tatiana

#### Nina and Tatiana - Night Terrors

Nina: Not again. Another nightgown torn to shreds.

Tatiana: I could feel your night tremors from the next tent over.

Nina: As you might have noticed from the fact that this is the third nightgown I have ruined this month.

Tatiana: Perhaps we should move you a few steps outside camp from now on, in the interest of safety.

Nina: Please do not. I could not bear having to sleep out on my own like that.

Nina: What about your medicines, Tatiana? Do you know anything that can help me?

Tatiana: If anything, I have the opposite problem myself.

Tatiana: Once, I awoke to a band of clerics praying over my body because they believed I had passed away during the night.

Nina: I cannot imagine that is a pleasant way to start your day. Though I am sure the clerics were just as startled as you.

Nina: If only we could each be a little more like the other.

Tatiana: I have no desire to be anywhere near as needlessly spirited as you.

Nina: Needless? But my spirit is one of the best things about me.

### Nina and Yahna

#### Nina and Yahna - Crows and Selfhood

Nina: Yahna? Who were you speaking to just now?

Yahna: merely one of the swamp's resident crows.

Nina: You can converse with crows?

Yahna: What kind of witch would I be if I could not? Communing with animals is one of the first things we learn how to do.

Yahna: I cannot talk to horses or gryphons either, in case you were wondering.

Nina: That would have been rather surprising.

Nina: I have to wonder, why did that witch decide to turn herself into a bird?

Yahna: It is all too common here in the swamp. Many of my apprentices have left to start new lives as different animals entirely.

Yahna: Only one "you" exists in the world, and I cannot see the reason for wanting to discard that.

Nina: Have you never wished to become someone else, Yahna?

Yahna: I have wished to become as strong as others, but that did not mean I wanted to be them.

Yahna: Once you have achieved your goals, you can take pride in knowing it was your effort which got you there, and yours alone.

Nina: Then while the journey ahead may yet be long, I am proud of myself for even taking the first step.

### Ochlys and Raenys

#### Ochlys and Raenys - Sharon

**Ochlys:** I saw you speaking with Sharon earlier, Raenys.

**Raenys:** I merely wished to express my gratitude for her always coming to my aid.

**Ochlys:** Yet did you truly need to share tea with her?

**Raenys:** You should have seen the way her face lit up as I presented her with an ornate arrangement of her favorite cookies. She nibbled at them in the most endearing fashion, dainty as a gentle forest creature.

**Ochlys:** You will not steal her from me, foul temptress.

**Ochlys:** Although, it has been some time since I enjoyed such a respite with Sharon myself.

**Raenys:** Then I believe you will be pleased to know that you were one of the few things she could bring herself to discuss. Your courage, your beauty, your kindness. She clearly values your friendship greatly, Ochlys.

**Raenys:** While our conversation did wander at times, she only wore the most brilliant smile when speaking of you.

**Ochlys:** Did she, now? Very well. You may speak with Sharon however you wish, but do not even think about turning her against me.

**Raenys:** Heheh. What a powerful bond they share.

### Ochlys and Sanatio

#### Ochlys and Sanatio - Duty

**Ochlys:** To simply rest a moment, rather than prattle on about duty and sacrifice...

**Sanatio:** Though I am aware you have been all too keen to abandon your obligations to the church.

**Ochlys:** How dare you imply such treachery. I would never.

**Sanatio:** Then allow me to share with you a few missives, penned by your own hand. "After the ceremony at Eisel Church, I plan to forego the banquet and return to Rondmort straight away." I have plenty more, if you wish to hear them.

**Ochlys:** Rgh. My one attempt at offering sympathy, and this is what I get?

**Sanatio:** Would you perhaps like to make a confession, Ochlys?

**Ochlys:** Sharon has nothing to do with this. We were sent out scouring Fevrith for divine shards, and I have still to hear one good reason why.

**Sanatio:** To ensure they never fall into Zenoira's evil hands again.

**Ochlys:** Oh? Tell me more about the divine shards.

**Sanatio:** Not until you repent for your abhorrent behavior at Rondmort.

**Ochlys:** I asked you first, divine blasphemer.

**Sanatio:** You take that back this instant!

### Ochlys and Sharon

#### Ochlys and Sharon - Sharon Joins

**Sharon:** Lady Ochlys!

**Ochlys:** My dear Sharon!

**Sharon:** I hear you sought their patronage in the hopes of ensuring my safety. You needn't worry. The shards you confided here remain untouched.

**Ochlys:** The shards be damned. I placed your well-being in danger's path, and for that I am deeply sorry.

**Sharon:** Please, you needn't apologize. On the contrary, this matter has swept the doubts from my mind as the morning fog. If I truly wish to glory in the Creator's lands, I must see it manifest through my own acts.

**Ochlys:** If such is the journey you wish, I will raise no objection.

**Sharon:** Might you grant me leave to join the Liberation?

**Alain:** Skilled healers such as yourself are ever in high demand. We would gladly count you among our numbers.

**Sharon:** Oh, what joy. Such a benevolent show of trust will not go unmet. You have it on my word as a servant to the Almighty.

#### Ochlys and Sharon - Flower Crown

**Sharon:** Lady Ochlys! I had not realized you had joined the Liberation as well.

**Ochlys:** Yes, my dear Sharon, and now that I have, we can be together once more.

**Sharon:** Wait. Is that a flower crown you are carrying?

**Ochlys:** I can still remember the delicate way you approached me, asking if I had lost my flower crown somewhere.

**Sharon:** It is rather a shameful memory, thinking on it now.

**Ochlys:** Now observe this dream blossom, capable of transforming a sunny afternoon into the darkest of nights. Raise your head, and gaze upon the flickering lights of the endless expanse.

**Sharon:** It is almost like we have been thrown back in time, to the days of our youth.

**Ochlys:** Indeed. Often did I wish to enjoy these sights together while we were apart.

**Sharon:** And now we can, whenever we want.

#### Ochlys and Sharon - Support

**Sharon:** Lady Ochlys? Is there something I can assist you with?

**Ochlys:** You seem rather troubled, Sharon. What is it that ails you?

**Sharon:** It was often obvious that you were quite exhausted from your duties back at Rondmort, yet you always found the energy to play with the children without so much as a moment's hesitation.

**Ochlys:** A pleasant memory, yes. But how does that relate to your present dismay?

**Sharon:** You are always doing whatever you can to protect me, while I never have the chance to support you in any way, neither in battle nor out of it.

**Ochlys:** You mean to say...

**Ochlys:** Are you certain you have no need of a rest, Sharon? In that case, perhaps I would rather like a nice wing massage. And your legs make as fine a pillow as ever.

**Sharon:** To be completely honest, our friendship has felt a bit one-sided of late. Though it feels a bit embarrassing to be saying that out loud.

**Ochlys:** Sharon, please. You do plenty. You may not always realize this, but the day I met you was the most blessed day of my life.

**Sharon:** I am pleased to hear you say so. And in the spirit of openness, I feel the same.

#### Sharon and Ochlys - Flower Crowns

Sharon: Lady Ochlys, you joined the Liberation?

Ochlys: I could hardly leave you to face this alone.

Sharon: You remember me?

Ochlys: Of course. You were the child who asked whether I had lost my flower crown, because the scriptures showed angels wearing crowns.

Sharon: I was so embarrassed afterward.

Ochlys: I was charmed. Here, a dream blossom.

Sharon: It makes the afternoon look like a night sky.

Ochlys: Then we can enjoy such skies whenever we wish.

#### Sharon and Ochlys - A Blessed Day

Ochlys: You should turn in, Sharon.

Sharon: I cannot. I keep wondering how I might better support you, when you are always the one protecting me.

Ochlys: Then support me now. Massage my wings.

Sharon: Your wings?

Ochlys: And I will rest my head here.

Sharon: Lady Ochlys, that is my lap.

Ochlys: Exactly.

Sharon: You are only trying to cheer me up.

Ochlys: That, and telling the truth. You already do plenty. The day we met was the most blessed day of my life.

Sharon: Lady Ochlys...

### Ochlys and Tatiana

#### Ochlys and Tatiana - Feathers

**Tatiana:** Mind sparing me a couple of feathers?

**Ochlys:** Who is there? It is you, the heretic responsible for nigh countless innocent deaths.

**Tatiana:** You have not answered my question. Will you be giving me the feathers or not?

**Ochlys:** I have nothing to give a heartless daemon like you.

**Tatiana:** You are correct. I have done terrible things in the name of a greater good, to save my people from a plague your church would do nothing to stop.

**Ochlys:** Yes, well, there is little point in arguing this now. What is done is done. Tell me, what do you plan to do with the feathers of an angel?

**Tatiana:** According to my studies, they can serve to enhance the efficacy of any tonic they are added to, though I have to admit I am rather skeptical. The plague still lingers in our lands, and there is no telling if the current cure will stay effective in subsequent outbreaks.

**Tatiana:** If that is how you feel, then I will leave you be. I promise, I will not make the same mistake again.

**Ochlys:** Hmph. We will see about that. By the way, I did think to help when your town was consumed, but there was nothing a mere angel such as I could do.

**Tatiana:** You...

**Ochlys:** I can tell you truly want to save as many people as possible. Just make sure it does not hurt, will you?

**Tatiana:** Very well. I promise to make this as painless as I can.

**Ochlys:** While I will never be able to condone such actions, I can at least understand why you chose to take them.

### Primm and Travis

#### Travis and Primm

Primm: Travis? Why are you carrying all that food?

Travis: Some of the locals gave it to me for chasing Zenoira out of their town. I was just on my way to test it for poison.

Primm: Oh? And do you do that every time, all by yourself?

Travis: I'd smell anything strong enough to kill me before I even took a bite.

Primm: Even so, are you sure you should be taking on such a grave responsibility alone?

Travis: I told you, I'll be fine. What's got you so concerned, anyway? Don't tell me you're only in this for a snack.

Primm: Oh, no! Well... my sister is particularly fond of a certain kind of cake you can only buy in that town. And so am I, actually.

Travis: Go on.

Primm: All I'm saying is, I can help cure you if you ever need it, Travis, and my appetite's not the only reason I'm offering.

Travis: Ah, but you admit it's a reason. Fine. Just in case something goes wrong.

Primm: Please don't call it taste testing.

### Raenys and Sanatio

#### Sanatio and Raenys - Condemnation

**Albion Soldier:** I heard His Holiness had long since risen to the heavens, and Father Sanatio was simply deceiving us.

**Albion Soldier:** Yes, and while the Orthodoxy claimed to be neutral in the war, the pitiful man was at Zenoira's every beck and call. Do you think he planned to install himself as the next pontifex?

**Sanatio:** Never. In the name of Lady Scarlett's sacred charge, a duty we shall accomplish no matter the cost. All the same, I shall deservedly bear any insult, should your enduring anger grant you worthy focus.

**Albion Soldier:** Hmph. If it could bring His Holiness back to us, I would have no end to my words for you.

**Sanatio:** If memory serves correct, you must be Lady Scarlett's former lady-in-waiting, yes?

**Raenys:** I am. It has been some time indeed, Father.

**Sanatio:** Should you too wish to criticize me, I would have no cause to dissent.

**Raenys:** You ask me to speak ill of you just as they did? I could never be so heartless.

**Sanatio:** Lady Raenys...

**Raenys:** Now you seek not to flee from the sins of your past, but to confront them directly. I could never bring myself to condemn such strength of will.

**Sanatio:** Forgive me. I did not intend to dishonor you so.

**Raenys:** Pay me no mind, Father. All I hope is that you can find peace within yourself.

**Sanatio:** I am not certain I deserve such kindness, but I thank you for it all the same.

### Raenys and Scarlett

#### Scarlett and Raenys

Scarlett: Tending to your feathers, Raenys?

Raenys: Ah, Lady Scarlett. Indeed, though I fear they've grown rather dry, with what little time I've had to groom myself of late.

Scarlett: I can't imagine the Drakenhold air is helping, either. By the way, is that what I think it is?

Raenys: Both for myself, and for you when I brushed your hair in the mornings.

Scarlett: You always made me feel so beautiful, Raenys.

Raenys: Did I? Well, I would be more than glad to do so again, if you'd like.

Scarlett: Now, you mean? I would love that.

Raenys: As you wish. As I stood here earlier, I secretly hoped you would do just that, my lady.

Scarlett: Really? If you wanted to spend time with me, all you had to do was ask.

Raenys: And ask I shall, next time.

#### Scarlett and Raenys

Scarlett: I never could get enough of this rose oil, even as a child.

Raenys: I'm glad you were willing to let me brush your hair again. Though today, I was thinking we might make use of these cosmetics as well.

Scarlett: These are gorgeous, Raenys!

Raenys: But I often dreamt of sharing make-up with you, once you had become a woman grown. Of course, you're already radiant as it is, yet a few embellishments here and there could only serve to enhance that beauty.

Scarlett: Oh, how long I've waited for this day!

Raenys: As have I, my lady. Now, just stay still a moment.

Scarlett: Heheh, that tickles!

Raenys: Gaze into this mirror and tell me what you think.

Scarlett: This is incredible, Raenys. I barely even recognize myself!

Raenys: And to know that I'm the first to see how greatly it magnifies your natural charm.

Scarlett: Really, thank you for this.

Raenys: What would you say to a stroll through town before we remove it? Perhaps we could find some clothes to match your new look.

Scarlett: That sounds wonderful!

Raenys: Then let's be off at once.

Scarlett: Oh, I can't wait!

#### Raenys and Scarlett - Reunion

**Raenys:** Ngh...

**Albion Soldier:** Hurry, Raenys!

**Scarlett:** There is someone over there!

**Alain:** Poor woman. It would seem she was cut down from behind.

**Scarlett:** Oh, Raenys...

**Alain:** You know her?

**Scarlett:** She was once my lady-in-waiting, yes. stand back. I think I can heal her wounds.

**Raenys:** Lady Scarlett, I thank the Father for your safety. You have grown much since last we met. Before me stands not the child I remember, but a full-blooded soldier of the Liberation.

**Scarlett:** This is not exactly how I imagined our reunion, but I am glad you are alive, Raenys.

**Raenys:** I fight back, stringing my bow for a small resistance movement backed by almost every last of Albion's lords. As a result, the territories that fall outside the church's purview are locked in fierce civil war.

**Scarlett:** And how did you come to be knocked out on the ground here?

**Raenys:** I was sent as a messenger to request aid for the resistance. But I was soon discovered by a band of Zenoirans, who turned their blades upon me. My wounds ran deep, yet I was able to escape until... well, you know what happened next.

**Alain:** Raenys, was it? Zenoira is our enemy as much as they are yours. We will purge them from this holy land and see Albion restored.

**Raenys:** As I should have expected. Word of your noble actions has long reached our ears, Prince Alain. Allow me to lend my aptitude to the effort.

**Scarlett:** It has barely been ten minutes since we were rapping on the Father's door, begging him to welcome you. You need rest, and you are not fighting anyone until you get it.

**Raenys:** Of course, Lady Scarlett. I only pray you find success in my stead, Prince Alain.

### Railanor and Rosalinde

#### Railanor and Rosalinde - Thorns

**Rosalinde:** You are usually at my side morning, noon, and night, after all. I would hazard to say it was the longest time I had spent alone in decades.

**Railanor:** Forgive me for abandoning you in such a manner, Terras.

**Rosalinde:** I know you lured Zenoira away in order to protect me.

**Railanor:** At least then, I would never have turned my blade on you.

**Rosalinde:** If you are going to say anything, I would much prefer to hear how glad you are to return to my service.

**Railanor:** And yet I continue to bear the dishonor of betraying you for as long as I live.

**Rosalinde:** You know, Railanor, you are far too serious for your own good.

**Railanor:** I had thought you had turned in for the evening, Terras.

**Rosalinde:** I could not sleep without finding out why.

**Railanor:** I suppose I should not be surprised you noticed.

**Rosalinde:** Surely not after the decades we have known each other. Now tell me, what is wrong?

**Railanor:** There is no need for you to suffer the same thorn which pierces my heart.

**Rosalinde:** Maybe not, but I am better at removing thorns than you might think. Go on.

**Railanor:** If you insist. Thank you for your compassion, Terras. Later, I learned they had returned to the forest soil and become one with the Divine. I cannot say for certain who was responsible for their deaths. As such, I have come to believe they perished at my own hand.

**Rosalinde:** No. If that is true, then blame for their passing lies solely with me. Many have laid down their lives in my name, Railanor, a list which almost included you as well. And if I ever hope to repay their sacrifice, I will have to do so by winning the peace they desperately desired.

**Railanor:** But Terras...

**Rosalinde:** Despite all my claims to the contrary, I have a feeling we are no closer to removing it now than when we started.

**Railanor:** It appears I am not the only one too serious for their own good.

**Rosalinde:** A bond that has stood the test of time for decades by now.

**Railanor:** And one that will continue to do so for decades to come.

### Ramona and Yunifi

#### Ramona and Yunifi - Mother

**Yunifi:** You should have seen him, Ramona. I have never heard Morard so excited before.

**Ramona:** Heheh. As much as I love your stories, Yunifi, I really must begin preparing for dinner.

**Yunifi:** There is just so much I want to tell you about. I know! Why do I not help you get dinner ready, and I can keep talking to you while we work?

**Ramona:** Whenever you have been unable to do so, I have missed it rather dearly.

**Yunifi:** Really?

**Ramona:** Really. But do not forget, we are supposed to be preparing dinner here, not just reminiscing on the past.

**Yunifi:** Sorry. That kinda just slipped out. Because you are... not really my mom.

**Ramona:** Those words hurt me more than you could ever know.

**Yunifi:** That is not how I meant it, Ramona.

**Ramona:** I owe you an apology, Yunifi. I should have thought about how you felt instead of only focusing on myself.

**Yunifi:** I really do think of you as my mom, Ramona. And I am glad to know you feel the same.

**Ramona:** Then you are welcome to call me whatever you wish, my daughter.

#### Yunifi and Ramona - Family

**Ramona:** It is hard to believe how quickly time flies, Yunifi. Almost eight years have passed since the day I first found you.

**Yunifi:** Hey, Ramona? Have you ever regretted taking me in?

**Ramona:** Well, you always were a handful. If I ever took my eye off you for even a second, you would run off without so much as a word. Once, you went missing for an entire evening, only to have spent the night sleeping beside the creatures of the forest. Despite our frantic searching, Morard and I did not find you until you walked back into town come sunrise.

**Yunifi:** Yeah, I remember. Sorry for making you worry.

**Ramona:** I also remember your ability to befriend anyone you meet in but an instant. It is your kindness which made such feats possible. What I mean to say is that the only emotion I feel toward my time raising you is pride.

**Ramona:** You and Morard are my family, Yunifi. The most wonderful family I could ever imagine.

**Yunifi:** I am glad you are the one who found us all those years ago. Thank you for being the best mom in the world.

### Renault and Scarlett

#### Scarlett and Renault

Renault: So the foal has finally ceased braying, hm?

Scarlett: What are you planning to do with me?

Renault: I should think you already know.

Scarlett: I have no intention of helping you, if that is what you imply.

Renault: Your intentions matter not.

Renault: I have not the slightest inkling how he persuaded you to follow him, but his aims are scarce different from my own.

Renault: I would advise you against harboring false hopes of rescue, girl.

Scarlett: My hopes are true as the morning. They will come.

Renault: A commendable show of defiance. But our mercenaries will have made short work of your friends.

Renault: Worry not. You will be freed from your burdens ere long, once you have fulfilled your purpose.

Renault: In the meantime, behave yourself.

### Ridiel and Tatiana

#### Ridiel and Tatiana - A Difficult Personality

Tatiana: Are you okay, Ridiel? I have never seen a bruise this pronounced before.

Ridiel: I am fine. I just got kicked by a horse.

Tatiana: When, exactly?

Ridiel: Given their history, I could not help but let out a teasing whistle.

Ridiel: In that moment, I sensed something move behind me, and turned to see Monica's horse staring me straight in the eyes.

Ridiel: I think you can guess what happened next.

Tatiana: You have far too much time on your hands, do you not?

Ridiel: It is not like I was looking for them or anything. It all just kind of happened.

Tatiana: Spoken like a true sinner.

Tatiana: I cannot say I understand your tendency to meddle in the affairs of others.

Ridiel: You do not have many friends, do you, Tatiana?

Tatiana: This is precisely the kind of meddling I mean.

Ridiel: Neither do I, honestly. Not a lot of people like how direct I am.

Ridiel: I was thinking maybe we could be friends, you and me.

Tatiana: I am not sure what part of this conversation would make you believe that is a good idea.

Ridiel: You seem like someone who is not afraid to call me out if I do something wrong. You already did, earlier.

Tatiana: Would this friendship bring any new responsibilities along with it?

Ridiel: None. Just talk to me every once in a while, and that is good enough.

Tatiana: In that case, return to me the next time you have need of a healer.

Tatiana: I look forward to more amusing anecdotes of your injuries, Ridiel.

Ridiel: You think this is funny? I will have you know it really hurt.

Tatiana: It seems you are not the only one here with a difficult personality.

### Ridiel and Travis

#### Ridiel and Travis - A Gift for Chloe

Ridiel: I need to know the kind of stuff Chloe likes, but I do not want her catching on.

Travis: What do you need me for? Cannot you just ask her yourself?

Ridiel: I have heard unexpected shows of appreciation are actually pretty common where she is from.

Travis: Does not change the fact you can handle it on your own. I thought you were good at spying on people.

Ridiel: I am, but not when it is someone I know. She would figure out what I was up to before I got started.

Travis: And you do not think it would scare her if you showed up with the perfect gift she never even told you she wanted?

Travis: Last thing I want is to get in the middle of that.

Ridiel: She will understand. I am sure of it.

Ridiel: I almost forgot. There is a reward in it for you, too. Do not ask for elf nails, because you will not be getting any.

Travis: Do not worry, I was not planning on it.

Travis: Fine. I want you to get me a book on elven history. I have been looking for one for ages.

Ridiel: I did not think you the reading type.

Travis: Looks can be deceiving.

Ridiel: Maybe something like knife-throwing? Or trapping rabbits?

Travis: Keep mocking me and I might change my mind about this deal of ours.

Ridiel: Sorry. Just a harmless joke.

Ridiel: I cannot wait to see the look on Chloe's face when I surprise her.

### Rosalinde and Scarlett

#### Scarlett and Rosalinde - Jealousy

Rosalinde: Has no one ever taught you it is dangerous to be out alone in the middle of the night?

Scarlett: Oh. If it is not the dark elf who decided to join us.

Rosalinde: Yes, and you are the attractive little friend Alain seems to be so enamored with.

Scarlett: I would not say he is enamored with me. Or that I am attractive, for that matter.

Scarlett: Though we have known each other for a long time now.

Rosalinde: Is there a reason you have turned away from me? I am only trying to be friendly.

Scarlett: You are standing closer than even I tend to get with him.

Rosalinde: That seems a simple enough fix to me. stand right beside him and tell him exactly how you feel.

Scarlett: Do not make it sound so easy.

Scarlett: Besides, we are at war. This is no time to distract him with something as trivial as love.

Rosalinde: Trivial, is it? Then I suppose you would not mind me stealing him away while you are busy holding yourself back.

Scarlett: Of course I would mind. I knew you had your eyes set on him.

Rosalinde: Who is to say? And while I would love to put that theory to the test...

Scarlett: Is it even possible for you to happily marry one of our kind?

Rosalinde: Perhaps not, but time and age mean nothing when it comes to matters of the heart.

Scarlett: Mark my words, Rosalinde. I will not lose the fight for Alain, even to someone as gorgeous as you.

Rosalinde: What an adorable girl. It only makes me want to tease her all the more.

### Rosalinde and Yahna

#### Yahna and Rosalinde - Magick and Regret

Rosalinde: Do you regret your decision? The spell cost you much of your strength.

Yahna: Powerful magick demands time and effort. I had brilliant apprentices, and if I had died then, I would have had no regrets.

Rosalinde: I did not come only to question you. I wanted to reminisce as a friend.

Yahna: Then you are welcome in my village any time. My apprentices will be delighted.

Rosalinde: And you?

Yahna: I will be delighted, too.

#### Rosalinde and Yahna - Time

**Rosalinde:** still, are you sure it was the right decision? You lost almost every ounce of your strength in the process, after all.

**Yahna:** What need is there for strength when you have a slew of brilliant apprentices? You may not be aware, but the more powerful the magick, the more time and effort it demands.

**Yahna:** In the days it took to forge my body anew, my apprentices never left my side, even for a second. Had I died in that moment, Rosalinde, I would have left this world without a single regret to my name.

**Rosalinde:** That spell of yours sounds almost as wondrous as the miracle of life itself. I wish I could have been there to witness it.

**Yahna:** It is a good thing you were not. Every eye would have been on you instead of me.

**Rosalinde:** I have to wonder, Yahna. Do you think you could live as long as an elf if you kept performing rejuvenation rituals?

**Yahna:** By the time I am actually old again, I expect I will not be a witch at all anymore.

**Rosalinde:** Not for any sort of powerful sorcery, but just to spend time reminiscing with a dear friend.

**Yahna:** My apprentices and I will welcome you to our village whenever you wish.

### Sanatio and Scarlett

#### Sanatio and Scarlett - Rest

**Scarlett:** You barely even find time to sleep. I guess I am just worried you are not taking care of yourself.

**Sanatio:** Lady Scarlett, thank you for the concern, but I assure you it is entirely unnecessary. Should I fail to serve, I would be renouncing my very right to live.

**Scarlett:** Do not forget that rest is a natural part of life, too.

**Sanatio:** Why do you treat me with such kindness? After the horrors inflicted upon our lands, I deserve nothing but scorn and contempt.

**Scarlett:** That is quite enough of your self-loathing, Sanatio.

**Scarlett:** We decided to race from one end of the bridge to the other, to see which of us was faster. At first, I found myself in an early lead, though you soon grew tired and started flying instead.

**Scarlett:** I miss him, you know. That innocent boy who always wore a smile, no matter what. But things are different now. Day and night, you torment yourself with this talk of atonement and little else.

**Sanatio:** I had not realized you still remembered that, a time when we were merely friends rather than servants of the Orthodoxy bound by obligation.

**Scarlett:** That is what you have always been to me. Not a priest or a sinner, but a friend.

**Sanatio:** My lady... By the Father's grace, I will not cause you any greater grief than I already have.

**Scarlett:** Thank you, Sanatio.

#### Scarlett and Sanatio

Scarlett: Heheh.

Sanatio: Hm? Is something funny, my lady?

Scarlett: It's quite a difference from the way you used to walk behind me when you first joined our army.

Sanatio: Lex often claimed I looked like a poor, newborn duckling blindly following its mother.

Scarlett: Well, that's a rude way to put it!

Sanatio: And while I can't say I enjoyed it, I'm rather pleased to note that his acerbic wit can no longer harm me.

Scarlett: You're only here next to me because you didn't want Lex teasing you?

Scarlett: Then what's the reason?

Sanatio: I had only hoped to behave in a manner that might bring you joy, rather than solitude. Wait a moment. I see what you're doing here.

Scarlett: Please, go on.

Sanatio: Perhaps I should go on ahead, if that's what you want.

Scarlett: I'm sorry, Sanatio. I didn't mean it. And I won't do it again. I promise.

Sanatio: Forgive me, my lady. I simply couldn't help but partake in a jest of my own.

Scarlett: You what? I thought you were really upset with me!

Sanatio: Then all went precisely to plan.

Scarlett: It's good to see you smile again, Sanatio.

Sanatio: I merely pray I can one day be the very friend you remember me as.

### Scarlett and Umerus

#### Scarlett and Umerus

Scarlett: Umerus? What are you doing out in all those thorns?

Umerus: Picking flowers, of course. Come look.

Scarlett: They're beautiful. I don't think I've seen these anywhere before, not even in Albion.

Umerus: So I've decided to preserve at least one of each type, that I might remember them in years to come.

Scarlett: I'm sure the flowers appreciate what you're doing for them, Umerus. They would look incredible, all growing side by side in your garden.

Umerus: Well, that's what seeds are for. I was planning to plant a few once we got home, actually.

Scarlett: Really? Then can I be the first person to see them once they've finally blossomed?

Umerus: As if you even have to ask, Scarlett.

#### Scarlett and Umerus

Scarlett: Now that you've joined the Liberation, I want you to become the knight you've always dreamt of being.

Umerus: What do you mean by that?

Scarlett: I could have sworn you'd finally done what you set out to do. That you were suffering more than you had words to describe. I'm sorry, Umerus.

Umerus: Don't be ridiculous. There's nothing to apologize for.

Scarlett: Well, I won't stand for it. Not anymore. Chase the dream we both know you've always wanted.

Umerus: Scarlett, I... It was then I started to question why I even aspired to knighthood in the first place. Something I failed to do twice: when I let my brother be taken hostage, and when I turned against you.

Scarlett: I'd much rather hear who you're going to be. A brave, kind knight who shields us all.

Umerus: Thank you, Scarlett. I couldn't ask for a finer friend.

#### Umerus and Scarlett - The Garden

**Umerus:** The garden is just through here. Follow me.

**Scarlett:** Well? Let us go after her.

**Umerus:** This is the place.

**Scarlett:** It is stunning. We never had blossoms like these back in Palevia. I used to sit right here, braiding little crowns and necklaces out of different red flowers.

**Scarlett:** Do you remember, Umerus? You would dry them for us then.

#### Umerus and Scarlett - Forced to Fight

**Hodel:** Returned empty-handed, have you?

**Umerus:** Wait, I beg you. It is just as we thought: Scarlett stands with the rebel forces. But if we surround their limited ranks with both our armies, we should have...

**Hodel:** You presume to ask us to partake as well?

**Umerus:** Please, my lord. This final chance is all I request.

**Hodel:** Hmph. We can settle our agreement once she is ours.

**Umerus:** I would not be fighting you, were it up to me, but a deal is a deal. Relinquish Scarlett or relinquish your life.

**Scarlett:** stop this, Umerus. Please.

**Umerus:** I wish I could. I honestly do. Am I truly so powerless? No, I cannot be beaten this easily.

**Scarlett:** Listen to me, Umerus. Hodel is gone, slain by our hand. We should not keep talking about it here. Let us meet in the garden.

**Umerus:** If that is what you want, I will be there in a moment.

#### Umerus and Scarlett - A Dear Friend

**Umerus:** Why have you asked to meet? You know I could raise my sword at any moment.

**Scarlett:** I am aware. But I understand why you did it.

**Umerus:** It does not matter. I will never deserve your trust again.

**Scarlett:** Tell me, Umerus. Do you remember this?

**Umerus:** I cannot believe you are still holding on to that.

**Scarlett:** You gave them to me as a symbol of our friendship and asked me never to forget about you.

**Umerus:** It was all I could do to get you to stop crying.

**Scarlett:** Yes, and it did not work. Your shoulder was practically drenched with tears, and a bit of snot as well.

**Scarlett:** I have been blessed with a great many companions since that day, but I have never once considered getting rid of them. No matter how far apart we may be, you will always be a dear friend, Umerus.

**Umerus:** Scarlett...

**Scarlett:** Come with us, please. We have shed enough tears in this garden to last us a lifetime.

### Scarlett and Virginia

#### Virginia and Scarlett - Caterpillar

Virginia: Scarlett? What are you doing over there?

Scarlett: Perfect timing, Virginia. Look at the little friend I found. Isn't he adorable?

Virginia: That foul beast is no friend of mine.

Scarlett: What do you mean? He's harmless.

Virginia: Make haste, Alain. A grotesque new evil threatens to ravage our lands.

Scarlett: It's just a caterpillar, Virginia. We used to catch them all the time back on Palevia.

Scarlett: See? There's nothing to be afraid of.

Virginia: I'll not hear another word, vile temptress.

Scarlett: Oops. He crawled into your armor.

Scarlett: Oh, there he is! I'm glad you're safe, Ser Caterpillar.

Scarlett: Erm, Virginia?

Alain: What's the matter, Scarlett? We came as quick as we could.

Lex: Alain? The princess isn't looking so good.

Virginia: Mmm...

### Scarlett and Yunifi

#### Scarlett and Yunifi

Yunifi: And that's the legend they tell every kid in Bastorias, to teach them to welcome strangers instead of fear them.

Scarlett: That was wonderful, Yunifi. Far more comforting than the horror story I was expecting.

Yunifi: Speaking of which, I love horror stories! Do you know any?

Scarlett: One day while cleaning the manor, she opened a door, only to find nothing but his wings lying on the ground.

Yunifi: You mean, without the man attached to them?

Scarlett: Yes. Naturally, she started to wonder if all angels could remove their wings like her master had. Of course not. And what she saw on the floor was actually just a wrinkled old blanket. Makes you think, doesn't it? Maybe all of our fears boil down to little more than simple misunderstandings.

Scarlett: Well, that would be lovely, but... erm...

Yunifi: Uh, Scarlett? Who are you talking to?

### Virginia and Yunifi

#### Yunifi and Virginia - Bastorias Snacks

**Yunifi:** Mmm.

**Virginia:** What are you doing over here, Yunifi?

**Yunifi:** Just a little something Ramona taught me how to make.

**Virginia:** I would love a bite, as long as you are offering.

**Virginia:** Hm. It has quite the aroma, and the flavor is not bad either. Though I cannot say I love the way it scratches my throat as it goes down. What did you say this was made from, exactly?

**Yunifi:** They last for months if you boil them and dry them out, so they are the perfect snack for when we are on the move.

**Yunifi:** Someone, come quick! I think Virginia is in shock!
